+++
title = "upadhESa raththina mAlai"
+++
Source: [TW](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

**[Audio](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-audio/)**

e-book: <https://onedrive.live.com/redir?resid=32ECDEC5E2737323!240&authkey=!AGzFLZEVQ12wwU0&ithint=file%2cpdf>

**Introduction**

[Sriya:pathi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) that is [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), gave vEdhas, and also incarnated in this material world to help people reach Him in SrIvaikuNtam. To effect his wishes he further made [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) to incarnate. Those twelve [AzhwArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) gave us 4000 [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/). To spread their word and to live and show the ways, He got [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) incarnated. The [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) ([SrIman nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) et al) propagated along with its meanings the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), and also wrote additional [granthams](http://granthams.koyil.org//) to explain the sampradhAyam.

The last of such [AchArya guru paramparai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) is [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). While living in thiruvarangam, he authored upadhEsa raththina mAlai which explained the meanings of rAmAnuja dharsanam which came through upadhEsam (~teaching/advising) by earlier [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) of the guru paramparai.

In upadhEsa raththinamAlai, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) shows us the auspicious days when [AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) incarnated, their divine *places* of birth, about the vyAkyAnams for their prabandhams created by various AchAryas, and about the greatness of an AchAryan. As part of that he devotes a lot of pAsurams to tell us about the greatness of [piLLai lOkAcharyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/)‘s rahasya grantham, that is, SrI vachana bhUshaNam. Finally he dedicates this to [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) by saying that those who recite and hold its meanings in their mind would get the grace of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

His sishya (disciple) [kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/) spread the importance of this prabandham. He wrote the thaniyan for upadhEsa raththinamAlai.

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) wished to write 74 pAsurams in upadhEsa raththinamAlai to match with the number of simhAsanAdhipathis established by [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) for spreading the dharsanam, but stopped one short of that. Another sishya of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) by name [eRumbi appA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/) wrote a pAsuram which is recited as the last pAsuram (74th) of this prabandham.

[![mamunigal-srirangam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/mamunigal-srirangam.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/mamunigal-srirangam.jpg)[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) as giving divine dharshan at SrIrangam

It would be good to note that upadhEsa raththinamAlai has also been written in samskritham by mAmunigaL’s (pUrvAsrama) divine grand son, jIyar nAyanAr.

[piLLailOkam jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/08/pillai-lokam-jiyar/) has written vyAkyAnam (meanings) for this prabandham, in the style of maNipravALam (mixed words of thamizh and samskritham). This along with padha urai (meanings for phrases) has been published by **SrI sudharsanam trust, puththUr, and SrIvaishNavaSrI, SrIrangam,** with the review of the padha urai etc., **by SrImadh u.vE. thirumalai nallAn chakravarththi krishNamAchArya swAmy,** and others.

[![pillailokam-jeeyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokam-jeeyar-1024x695.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokam-jeeyar.jpg)piLLailOkam jIyar

**SrImAn u.vE mAdapUsi varadharAjan** **swami** has written a book, “**upadhEsa raththinamAlai – piLLai lOkam jIyar aruLiya vyAkyAnamum, thamizhAkkamum**” (original vyAkyAnam and thamizh translation). It provides meanings in simple thamizh for the maNipravALa vyAkyAnam of [piLLia lOkam jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/08/pillai-lokam-jiyar/), and also adds more text and references with the help of the swamis that the author has mentioned in his published book.

{About the swAmis mentioned in the above book:

Sri u.vE. P.B. AnnangarAcharyar and Sri U.Ve. SrI vaishNava sudharsanar krishNaswamy have collected the references from vEdham etc., for many of the samskritha slOkas found in the vyAkyAnam. Additional references have been quoted by SrImAn u.vE thirunArAyaNapuram araiyar srIrAma sarmA, and SrI u.vE. satakOpAchArya swami (in his very old age of 90) helped in getting their meanings. SrIrangam gOmatam SrImAn u.vE. sampath kumArAchArya swami also provided Akarams for the references.  
}

We are using the aforementioned books as the valuable sources for this translation into English.

Please write to us to correct any mistakes in our understanding and in our translation.

**maNavALa mAmunigaL vaibhavam can be read [here](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/).**

**piLLai lOkam jIyar’s vaibhavam can be read [here.](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillai-lokam-jiyar/)**

</details>


## Introduction
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[![paramapadhanathan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/paramapadhanathan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/paramapadhanathan.jpg)

[SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) with [SrI dhEvi (SrI mahAlakshmi)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), bhUdhEvi, nILA dhEvi and nithyasUris in paramapadham

[SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) is the supreme God who is filled with unlimited and wonderful auspicious qualities. Out of his divine and unconditional grace, he blessed selected [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s to become [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (great saints who preached pure and exclusive devotion towards [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)). Though He was the supremely independent master of the nithyasUris (eternally free souls) and mukthAthmAs (liberated souls), he wanted to rid himself of the one agony he had.

That agony is him suffering for the suffering of the bound souls in the material world. Him being the supreme father of every one, he was unable to bear the suffering of his children who are caught in the cycle of birth and death in the material world. One may question, if the supreme God will have any agony/sorrow – him being sathya kAma (one who can fulfill all his desires) and sathya sankalpa (one who can accomplish anything). Our [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) have explained that him feeling the pain for the suffering souls is also his auspicious quality. Just like an all-capable father who is happily living with his one child will still worry for his other child who is staying away from him on his own and struggling, [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), though being all-capable, he is feeling the pain looking at the plight of the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s in samsAram (material world) who are suffering since time-immemorial due to being covered by ignorance and lacking of true knowledge.

To facilitate the upliftment of such suffering [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s, he gives body and senses for the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s during srushti (creation), reveals the sAsthram (scriptures), himself descends in to the material world as various incarnations like SrI rAma, krishNa, etc. Even after all of these, the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s are not really willing to learn the true knowledge and accept his supremacy. Just like a hunter will catch a deer using another trained deer, He decides to uplift [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s through other [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s who are already in the material world. So he chooses a select few of them, blesses them with divine knowledge and makes them [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). AzhwAr means one who is immersed in bhagavath vishayam (spiritual matters). These [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) appeared in various holy places in the southern part of bhAratha dhEsam as foretold by vEdha vyAsa in SrI bhAgavatham. Totally, [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are said to be 10 in number. [poigai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (sarO yOgi),[bhUthaththAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (bhUtha yOgi), [pEyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (mahathAhvaya), [thirumazisai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) (bhakthi sAra), [nammAzhwAr (satakOpa/parAnkusa)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), [kulasEkara AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/),
[periyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) (vishNuchiththa),[thoNdaradippodi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) (bhakthAngri rENu),
[thiruppANAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) (muni vAhana yOgi) and[thirumangai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) (parakAla). They are also said to be 12 in number if [madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) (gOdhA – an incarnation of bhUdhEvi nAchiyAr, one of the divine consorts of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)) are included. While the 10 [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are said to be exclusively devoted to [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), [madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) were totally devoted to their [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and [periyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) respectively.

[![Azhwars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars-1024x235.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars.jpg)

[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)

[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) sung many pAsurams (verses) in glorification of [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). These pAsurams total up to 4000 verses approximately and are thus called 4000 dhivya prabandham. dhivya means divine and prabandham means literature (that which captures [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) himself). They brought out the essence of vEdham/vEdhAntham in simple and chaste thamizh. The whole purpose of these dhivya prabandhams is to uplift the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s by transmitting true knowledge. Several hundreds of years after the time of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), many [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) starting with [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/), centered with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and ending with [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) appeared and preached the divine message of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). While less intelligent people considered[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) pAsurams as simple thamizh songs, the most intelligent [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) established that these pAsurams bring out the ultimate philosophy of [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) being the means (to be uplifted from this material world) and the goal (to be situated in ones true nature of eternal service to [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) in paramapadham – spiritual world). Our [pUrvAchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) fully relished the dhivya prabandhams and centered their life around learning them, teaching them and living by those pAsurams.

[![azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)[nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) with[madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) in either side

There was a dark period in the history where the dhivya prabandhams were lost in time after the time of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). Eventually, it was [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) who took lots of hardships to locate AzhwAr thirunagari which is the birth place of [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and he learnt all the 4000 dhivya prabandham with their meanings by the divine grace of [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/). [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) classified the 4000 dhivya prabandhams into 4 parts as we see today, taught them to his sishyas and brought out the importance of these dhivya prabandhams. He added kaNNinuN chiRu thAmbu into 4000 dhivya prabandhams in honour of[madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) who showed unflinching devotion towards [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/).

[![Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur.jpg)

[SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)

[SrI rAmAnuja (emperumAnAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is considered as an incarnation of Adhi sEsha and who appeared a century later received the same through the guru paramparA by studying the same under various [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) per the desire of [yAmunAchArya](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/alavandhar/). He then spread the glories of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and their works to all sections of the society and greatly facilitated the propagation of this SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam. It is because of his great contribution, this sampradhAyam was declared to be known as [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) dharsanam by [SrI ranganAtha](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) himself. Also, rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi which was sung in glorification of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) by [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/26/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar/) was added into 4000 dhivya prabandham by the [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) due to his greatness. This rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi is glorified as “prapanna gAyathri” – that which is to be recited compulsorily by all prapannas (ones who are surrendered) every day, just like how gAyathri manthram is to be recited by brAhmaNas everyday.

[![nampillai-goshti1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) kAlakshEpa (lecture) gOshti (assembly)

[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) is an important AchArya (coming in the parampArA after [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), [embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/), [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/) and [nanjIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)) who should be mentioned at this juncture. He was living in SrIrangam and was the leader of SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam during his times. It was during his period in SrIrangam, the meanings of 4000 dhivya prabandham were given great importance. He was engaged in giving lectures everyday close to the sanctum sanctorium of [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – [SrI ranganAtha](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). It is explained that even [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) would stand up and try to peek through the window to hear his lectures. [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)‘s sishyas also greatly contributed to propagate the meanings of these dhivya prabandhams. [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) who is a sishya of[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) and also known as vyAkyAna chakkaravarthy (emperor among commentators) wrote commentaries for all dhivya prabandhams and his contribution is greatly hailed by our [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/). [vadakku thiruvIdhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/), who is another sishya of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), documented the lectures given by [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) on thiruvAimozhi and this document became to be known as eedu 36000 padi (the most cherished vyAkyAnam of thiruvAimozhi).

[![pillailokacharya-goshti](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokacharya-goshti.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokacharya-goshti.jpeg)piLLai lOkAchAryar kAlakshEpa gOshti

After [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)‘s time, [piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) leads the sath sampradhAyam and documents all the most confidential matters of dhivya prabandham in his rahasya granthams. These confidential matters were explained by various [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) at various times in various granthams.[piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) consolidated those and documented them in his 18 primary works. But towards the end of his life, tragedy struck SrIrangam in the form of mughal invaders who destroyed everything there.[piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) arranged for the safe journey of namperumAL (SrI ranganAtha – uthsavar) and escaped from the invaders from there along with namperumAL. Shortly in to the journey, he ascended to paramapadham due to the difficult journey through forests at such advanced age. Then came a lengthy period of suffering for the whole of SrIvaishNava community. After few decades, when peace prevailed and invaders were driven out, namperumAL eventually returned to SrIrangam.

[![srisailesa-thanian-small](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srisailesa-thanian-small.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srisailesa-thanian-small.jpg)[mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) kAlakshEpa gOshti – “srI sailEsa dhayApAthram” thanian submission

Finally, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) who is considered as an incarnation of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) himself, appeared in [AzhwAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/). He became a sishya of[thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) and learned all the esoteric meanings of vEdham, vEdhAntham and dhivya prabandhams from his own father and [thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). Under the orders of[thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) (his AchArya), he reached SrIrangam and spent the rest of his life in rejuvenating the sath sampradhAyam to its past glories. He personally searched for all the lost literature, studied them, recorded them in palm leaves with great difficulty and preserved them for future generations to come. Fittingly, in appreciating his great qualities and efforts, SrI ranganAtha himself listens to thiruvAimozhi kAlakshEpam from [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) for a whole year and at the end of the lecture series, he himself appears as a small boy and accepts [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) as his AchArya and submits him the most glorious “SrISailESa dhayApAthram…” thaniyan. Subsequently, many AchAryas who came in various lineages taught and lived by these dhivya prabandhams.

Thus, [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ dhivya prabandhams which were focussed on the upliftment of [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s which is to fulfill the desire of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) have been preserved by our [pUrvAchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) through the history. It is emphasised greatly that all SrIvaishNavas should learn the dhivya prabandhams, understand the meanings properly and live by them. Keeping this in mind, with the aim of translating all of 4000 dhivya prabandhams, we are starting humbly in this great endeavour. We have a great desire to complete this translation kainkaryam by 2017 May, when we will commemorate the 1000th year appearance day of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Initially we are starting with English translation but we would try to arrange for translation of these dhivya prabandhams in other languages as well.

It would be very useful to understand the validity and glories of AzhwArs and their dhivya prabhandhams. Please read the following articles which go through them in detail:

- part 1 –
  <http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2013/02/dhivya-prabhandha-pramanya-samarthanam-1.html>
- part 2 –
  <http://ponnadi.blogspot.com/2013/02/dhivya-prabhandha-pramanya-samarthanam-2.html>

With full dependence and faith on [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), we are planning to translate the dhivya prabandhams into simple English (and other languages too). We will provide word-by-word meaning for each pAsuram with specific highlights and important points from the vyAkyAnams. The website will be well organized and easily searchable. We would also attempt to add pictures wherever possible/applicable. With the blessings of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), bhAgavathas and [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), we plan to do a faithful kainkaryam of translating these dhivya prabandhams which will be useful for many generations to come.

Though dhivya prabandham only indicates the thamizh pAsurams composed by [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (and rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi of [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/26/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar/)), in this website/initiative, we would also cover many of the thamizh/samskritham prabandhams which are composed by our [pUrvAchAryas](http://guruparamparai.koyil.org) in the “[Other Prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/others/)” section. We revere our AchAryas SrIsUkthis (divine compositions) greatly too and will also provide translation for the same as much as possible.

adiyen sarathy ramanuja dasan  
on behalf of dhivya prabandham translations team

pramEyam (goal) – [https://koyil.org](https://koyil.org/)  
pramANam (scriptures) – <http://granthams.koyil.org>  
pramAthA (preceptors) – <http://acharyas.koyil.org>  
SrIvaishNava education/kids portal – [http://pillai.koyil.org](https://pillai.koyil.org/)

## Introduction
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[![paramapadhanathan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/paramapadhanathan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/paramapadhanathan.jpg)

[SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) with [SrI dhEvi (SrI mahAlakshmi)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), bhUdhEvi, nILA dhEvi and nithyasUris in paramapadham

[SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) is the supreme God who is filled with unlimited and wonderful auspicious qualities. Out of his divine and unconditional grace, he blessed selected [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s to become [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (great saints who preached pure and exclusive devotion towards [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)). Though He was the supremely independent master of the nithyasUris (eternally free souls) and mukthAthmAs (liberated souls), he wanted to rid himself of the one agony he had.

That agony is him suffering for the suffering of the bound souls in the material world. Him being the supreme father of every one, he was unable to bear the suffering of his children who are caught in the cycle of birth and death in the material world. One may question, if the supreme God will have any agony/sorrow – him being sathya kAma (one who can fulfill all his desires) and sathya sankalpa (one who can accomplish anything). Our [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) have explained that him feeling the pain for the suffering souls is also his auspicious quality. Just like an all-capable father who is happily living with his one child will still worry for his other child who is staying away from him on his own and struggling, [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), though being all-capable, he is feeling the pain looking at the plight of the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s in samsAram (material world) who are suffering since time-immemorial due to being covered by ignorance and lacking of true knowledge.

To facilitate the upliftment of such suffering [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s, he gives body and senses for the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s during srushti (creation), reveals the sAsthram (scriptures), himself descends in to the material world as various incarnations like SrI rAma, krishNa, etc. Even after all of these, the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s are not really willing to learn the true knowledge and accept his supremacy. Just like a hunter will catch a deer using another trained deer, He decides to uplift [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s through other [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s who are already in the material world. So he chooses a select few of them, blesses them with divine knowledge and makes them [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). AzhwAr means one who is immersed in bhagavath vishayam (spiritual matters). These [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) appeared in various holy places in the southern part of bhAratha dhEsam as foretold by vEdha vyAsa in SrI bhAgavatham. Totally, [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are said to be 10 in number. [poigai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (sarO yOgi),[bhUthaththAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (bhUtha yOgi), [pEyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (mahathAhvaya), [thirumazisai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) (bhakthi sAra), [nammAzhwAr (satakOpa/parAnkusa)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), [kulasEkara AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/),
[periyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) (vishNuchiththa),[thoNdaradippodi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) (bhakthAngri rENu),
[thiruppANAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) (muni vAhana yOgi) and[thirumangai AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) (parakAla). They are also said to be 12 in number if [madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) (gOdhA – an incarnation of bhUdhEvi nAchiyAr, one of the divine consorts of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)) are included. While the 10 [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are said to be exclusively devoted to [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), [madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) were totally devoted to their [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and [periyAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/20/periyazhwar/) respectively.

[![Azhwars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars-1024x235.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Azhwars.jpg)

[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)

[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) sung many pAsurams (verses) in glorification of [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). These pAsurams total up to 4000 verses approximately and are thus called 4000 dhivya prabandham. dhivya means divine and prabandham means literature (that which captures [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) himself). They brought out the essence of vEdham/vEdhAntham in simple and chaste thamizh. The whole purpose of these dhivya prabandhams is to uplift the [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s by transmitting true knowledge. Several hundreds of years after the time of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), many [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) starting with [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/), centered with [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and ending with [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) appeared and preached the divine message of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). While less intelligent people considered[AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) pAsurams as simple thamizh songs, the most intelligent [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) established that these pAsurams bring out the ultimate philosophy of [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) being the means (to be uplifted from this material world) and the goal (to be situated in ones true nature of eternal service to [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) in paramapadham – spiritual world). Our [pUrvAchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) fully relished the dhivya prabandhams and centered their life around learning them, teaching them and living by those pAsurams.

[![azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)[nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) with[madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) in either side

There was a dark period in the history where the dhivya prabandhams were lost in time after the time of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). Eventually, it was [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) who took lots of hardships to locate AzhwAr thirunagari which is the birth place of [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and he learnt all the 4000 dhivya prabandham with their meanings by the divine grace of [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/). [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) classified the 4000 dhivya prabandhams into 4 parts as we see today, taught them to his sishyas and brought out the importance of these dhivya prabandhams. He added kaNNinuN chiRu thAmbu into 4000 dhivya prabandhams in honour of[madhurakavi AzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) who showed unflinching devotion towards [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/).

[![Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Ramanuja_Sriperumbudur.jpg)

[SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)

[SrI rAmAnuja (emperumAnAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is considered as an incarnation of Adhi sEsha and who appeared a century later received the same through the guru paramparA by studying the same under various [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) per the desire of [yAmunAchArya](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/alavandhar/). He then spread the glories of [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and their works to all sections of the society and greatly facilitated the propagation of this SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam. It is because of his great contribution, this sampradhAyam was declared to be known as [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) dharsanam by [SrI ranganAtha](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) himself. Also, rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi which was sung in glorification of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) by [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/26/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar/) was added into 4000 dhivya prabandham by the [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) due to his greatness. This rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi is glorified as “prapanna gAyathri” – that which is to be recited compulsorily by all prapannas (ones who are surrendered) every day, just like how gAyathri manthram is to be recited by brAhmaNas everyday.

[![nampillai-goshti1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) kAlakshEpa (lecture) gOshti (assembly)

[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) is an important AchArya (coming in the parampArA after [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), [embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/), [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/) and [nanjIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)) who should be mentioned at this juncture. He was living in SrIrangam and was the leader of SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam during his times. It was during his period in SrIrangam, the meanings of 4000 dhivya prabandham were given great importance. He was engaged in giving lectures everyday close to the sanctum sanctorium of [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – [SrI ranganAtha](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). It is explained that even [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) would stand up and try to peek through the window to hear his lectures. [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)‘s sishyas also greatly contributed to propagate the meanings of these dhivya prabandhams. [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) who is a sishya of[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) and also known as vyAkyAna chakkaravarthy (emperor among commentators) wrote commentaries for all dhivya prabandhams and his contribution is greatly hailed by our [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/). [vadakku thiruvIdhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/), who is another sishya of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), documented the lectures given by [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) on thiruvAimozhi and this document became to be known as eedu 36000 padi (the most cherished vyAkyAnam of thiruvAimozhi).

[![pillailokacharya-goshti](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokacharya-goshti.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/pillailokacharya-goshti.jpeg)piLLai lOkAchAryar kAlakshEpa gOshti

After [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)‘s time, [piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) leads the sath sampradhAyam and documents all the most confidential matters of dhivya prabandham in his rahasya granthams. These confidential matters were explained by various [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) at various times in various granthams.[piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) consolidated those and documented them in his 18 primary works. But towards the end of his life, tragedy struck SrIrangam in the form of mughal invaders who destroyed everything there.[piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) arranged for the safe journey of namperumAL (SrI ranganAtha – uthsavar) and escaped from the invaders from there along with namperumAL. Shortly in to the journey, he ascended to paramapadham due to the difficult journey through forests at such advanced age. Then came a lengthy period of suffering for the whole of SrIvaishNava community. After few decades, when peace prevailed and invaders were driven out, namperumAL eventually returned to SrIrangam.

[![srisailesa-thanian-small](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srisailesa-thanian-small.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srisailesa-thanian-small.jpg)[mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) kAlakshEpa gOshti – “srI sailEsa dhayApAthram” thanian submission

Finally, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) who is considered as an incarnation of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) himself, appeared in [AzhwAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/). He became a sishya of[thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) and learned all the esoteric meanings of vEdham, vEdhAntham and dhivya prabandhams from his own father and [thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/). Under the orders of[thiruvAimozhi piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) (his AchArya), he reached SrIrangam and spent the rest of his life in rejuvenating the sath sampradhAyam to its past glories. He personally searched for all the lost literature, studied them, recorded them in palm leaves with great difficulty and preserved them for future generations to come. Fittingly, in appreciating his great qualities and efforts, SrI ranganAtha himself listens to thiruvAimozhi kAlakshEpam from [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) for a whole year and at the end of the lecture series, he himself appears as a small boy and accepts [mAmunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/23/azhagiya-manavala-mamunigal/) as his AchArya and submits him the most glorious “SrISailESa dhayApAthram…” thaniyan. Subsequently, many AchAryas who came in various lineages taught and lived by these dhivya prabandhams.

Thus, [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ dhivya prabandhams which were focussed on the upliftment of [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)s which is to fulfill the desire of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) have been preserved by our [pUrvAchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) through the history. It is emphasised greatly that all SrIvaishNavas should learn the dhivya prabandhams, understand the meanings properly and live by them. Keeping this in mind, with the aim of translating all of 4000 dhivya prabandhams, we are starting humbly in this great endeavour. We have a great desire to complete this translation kainkaryam by 2017 May, when we will commemorate the 1000th year appearance day of [SrI rAmAnuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Initially we are starting with English translation but we would try to arrange for translation of these dhivya prabandhams in other languages as well.

It would be very useful to understand the validity and glories of AzhwArs and their dhivya prabhandhams. Please read the following articles which go through them in detail:

- part 1 –
  <http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2013/02/dhivya-prabhandha-pramanya-samarthanam-1.html>
- part 2 –
  <http://ponnadi.blogspot.com/2013/02/dhivya-prabhandha-pramanya-samarthanam-2.html>

With full dependence and faith on [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), we are planning to translate the dhivya prabandhams into simple English (and other languages too). We will provide word-by-word meaning for each pAsuram with specific highlights and important points from the vyAkyAnams. The website will be well organized and easily searchable. We would also attempt to add pictures wherever possible/applicable. With the blessings of [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), bhAgavathas and [AchAryas](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), we plan to do a faithful kainkaryam of translating these dhivya prabandhams which will be useful for many generations to come.

Though dhivya prabandham only indicates the thamizh pAsurams composed by [AzhwArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (and rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi of [thiruvarangaththu amudhanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/26/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar/)), in this website/initiative, we would also cover many of the thamizh/samskritham prabandhams which are composed by our [pUrvAchAryas](http://guruparamparai.koyil.org) in the “[Other Prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/others/)” section. We revere our AchAryas SrIsUkthis (divine compositions) greatly too and will also provide translation for the same as much as possible.

adiyen sarathy ramanuja dasan  
on behalf of dhivya prabandham translations team

pramEyam (goal) – [https://koyil.org](https://koyil.org/)  
pramANam (scriptures) – <http://granthams.koyil.org>  
pramAthA (preceptors) – <http://acharyas.koyil.org>  
SrIvaishNava education/kids portal – [http://pillai.koyil.org](https://pillai.koyil.org/)

## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – thaniyan
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

**thaniyan – divined by [kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/)**

***in ‘kattaLaik kalith thuRai’*** (name of a particular form of thamizh poetry)

*munnam thiruvAimozhippiLLai thAm upadhEsiththa nEr*  
*thannin padiyaith thaNavAdha sol maNavALamuni*  
*than anbudan sey upadhEsa raththinamAlai thannaith*  
*than nenju thannil tharippavar thALgaL charaN namakkE*

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-thaniyan)

**Word by word meaning:**

*munnam* – earlier  
*[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) thAm, upadhEsiththa* – he had divinely advised/instructed  
*nEr thannin* – the meanings of thathvam (true knowledge);  
*thaNavAdha* – he follows without fail, always thinks and follows  
*padiyai* – those ways,  
*maNavALa mAmuni* – (such ) [srI maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)  
*than* – out of his  
*anbudan* – love/kindness toward the well-being of the world,  
*sey* – divined  
*upadhEsa raththinamAlai* – the prabandham with such title (instructions put together to form a garland of precious stones), its exclusive meanings  
*tharippavar* – those who bear it  
*tham nenju thannil* – in their mind;  
*thALgaL* – such people’s divine feet,  
*charaN* – it is the place to surrender  
*namakku* – for us.

**Simple meaning:**

{This thaniyan is written by [kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/) who is a disciple of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). Remembering about [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s deep respect and affection towards his [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), [aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/) has started the thaniyan with the name of that [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), which would have very much pleased [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), which would have been the very goal of [aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/).}

[srI maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), due to his love and care towards the well-being of everyone in the world, divined to us the prabandham called upadhEsa raththina mAlai, based on the teachings earlier of his AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), which [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) always thinks about and follows. Those who make the extra-ordinary meanings of this prabandham to strongly stay in their mind – their divine feet is the place for us to be.

[![ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)[emperumAnAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) – [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)

[![koilannan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/koilannan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/koilannan.jpg)[kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/koyil-annan/)

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – avathArikai (Introduction)
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous page (thaniyan)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai-thaniyan/)

**vyAkyAna avathArikai (Introduction)**

[periya jIyAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is the one who,

- as said in ‘*pinnAnAr vaNangum sOdhi* \[thirunedunthANdakam – 10\]’,
  is followed by future generations,
- can be said that he is one of the nithyasUris who would naturally have
  (without having to strain the mind) subservience, such greatness,
- took shelter of the divine feet of [thiruvAimozhip
  piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/),
- as said in ‘*[thEvu
  maRRaRiyEn](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/)*
  \[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 2
  [(audio)](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/kanninunchiruththambu-2)\],
  was extremely enthusiastic in serving thiruvAimozhip piLLAi,
- due to his teachings became well versed in
  [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)
  and other prabandhams [and their
  meanings](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org) which are rahasyams, and
  stayed thankful,
- that same
  [piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)
  himself told – you hold as your support the divine feet of the one who
  is the central gem stone of the garland of [guru
  paramparai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/): that is
  [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)
  – and *because of that* he
  ([mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/))
  possessed extreme devotion toward
  [udaiyavar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s
  divine feet,
- having [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ and
  [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)’
  grace as the potent water for his growth,
- and so only is having in him, in collective form, the characteristics
  of
  [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/),
  [thirumangai
  AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/),
  [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)
  and others, and also of [srIman
  nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/),
  [yAmunAcharyar
  (ALavandhAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/alavandhar/),
  [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)
  and others,
- is enthusiastic at all times in well-being of the world’s people,
- due to his nature of considering his purpose as the well-being of
  others, he is having the greatness of including the meanings of
  invaluable rahasyams in his prabandhams,
- it can be said that on his qualities of subservience etc., there is no
  equal to [maNavALa
  mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) in the
  seven material worlds and in the other world, that is ubhaya vibhUthi,
- having the wealth of rangamangaLam and living in thiruvarangam as
  ‘*thiruvarangam thiruppathiyE iruppAga’,*
- and due to that is known everywhere as ‘**kOyil maNavALamamuni**’,

he is such a swami, isn’t it?**  **

[![mamunigal-srirangam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/mamunigal-srirangam.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/05/mamunigal-srirangam.jpg)*kOyil maNavALa mAmuni*

[jIyar, that is maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) who is having such great qualities, due to his noble kindness, because the incarnations of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) were in the past, as he said in ‘*theruLuRRa AzhvArgaL seermai aRivArAr aruLichcheyalai aRivArAr* \[upadhEsa rathinamAlai – 36\]’ (who would know (not many) the greatness of [Azhvars](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), and their [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), he saw that the greatness of incarnation of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), their words and deeds, were all becoming lesser known, and saw that during that time the devotees were having less knowledge (of sampradhAyam etc.), so he firmly decided – we shall bring out the details of purpose, etc., of incarnation of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), what their prabandhams are, and about those who know well both of these, that is, [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) – their teachings and actions, starting with all these details, and through that let us get these people to attain the higher plane, and decided that if it is done just by teachings only then it may not be useful for the future generations, as he wanted current and future generations to know these, he then announces such great details through this prabandham as an upadhEsa raththinamAlai, that is, based on the lineage of teachings of prior [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), like a garland; so the name of this dhivya prabandham is upadhEsa raththinamAlai.

[![Azhvars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)

Since this prabandham announces the greatness of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), and their dhivya prabandhams, it is great among the prabandhams. What is announced in this prabandham is about what thirumanthram says – not being subservient to others but being subservient to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) only, holding [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) only as the support, and being enjoyable only by [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – about those having these three qualities. So the base of this prabandham is thirumanthram.

Those who live according to the meanings of thirumanthram is explained in detail in ‘*payilum sudaroLi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.7\]’, ‘*nedumArkkadimai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.10\]’. Following along the same lines is the prabandham ‘[*kaNNinuN chiruth thAmbu*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/)’. Following along the same lines is the prabandham ‘[*rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/)’. The ways of these two prabandhams is explained in this prabandham, since it shows the glory of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). So this prabandham is the ultimate stage in the ultimate stage.

[![srivaishna-guruparamparai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)

Now, an analysis of the reason/justification for this prabandham to follow the thirunakshathrams (birth stars) of the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) among the noble ones mentioned in this prabandham is:

As [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) wished to get the quality of being an AchAryan, he provided [bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) and abhaya pradhAnam (shelter/refuge) and he is considered as the first guru; to save the samsAris, what He incarnates in other sects in stars such as rOhiNi, punarvasu (punarpUsam), what in the months of chaithra (chiththirai), bhadra (purattAsi), etc., what in places like vada (north) mathurA, ayOdhyA that are near the rivers yamunA and sarayU; starting with these the details are mentioned in ithihAsam etc.; In the same vain, here too, the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who incarnated to save the people, and got unblemished knowledge due to His causeless mercy, their birth stars and months which are great ones like sravaNa (thiruvONam), etc., and months of ashvina (aippasi) etc., in places like kAnchi that are talked as equivalent of ayOdhyA, mathurA, and near their places are rivers like kAviri (cauvEry) – all these are indicated in those ithihAsams as ‘*kalaukalu bhavishyanthi*’(would incarnate in kali yugam),and as ‘*kvachith kvachith* \[bhAgavatham 11-5.38\]*’* (in there and there (places));

moreover, due to the greatness of getting unblemished knowledge [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) were immersed in devotion and performed saraNAgathy (surrender), due to His wish they incarnated as 10 of them as an aspect of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and with full of devotion; as He is present in the [dhivya dhEsams](https://koyil.org/index.php/dhivya-dhesams/) in [archA form](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/archavathara-anubhavam.html) out of his love, they have also taken the befitting form, and are having dharsan of Him; and are giving dharsan to others; due to our connection with them, they are able to make us reach the destiny;

so these [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ thirunakshathrams also can be celebrated equally;

Now, starting from ‘*AzhvAr thirumagaLAr ANdAL* \[[upadhEsa raththinamAlai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)\]’, since the other three ([ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/), [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html), and [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) are subservient to the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), and since they are much more glorious than other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), it goes well to enumerate these nobles ones’ incarnation details along with the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). Since [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) understand and celebrate the glory of the aforementioned, they too are celebrated.

Now, the prabandham talks about the glories of those who are in the first stage of devotion like ‘*vERAga Eththi iruppAr* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi 18\]’ (those who praise [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) in amazing distinguished ways), that is, devotion towards [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/); and about the glories of those who are in the pinnacle stage of devotion like ‘*maRRavaraich chARRi iruppAr* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi 18\]’(~ those who depend on devotees), that is, devotion towards AchAryan, and about the greatness of their prabandhams, and about the ways of the rahasya granthams which provide the essence of the above two categories, and about the anushtAnams (deeds/actions) explained in such granthams, and ways of being firmly positioned under the divine feet of AchAryan, that is, charama parva nishtai; this prabandham also explains how those who are involved in the prabandham reached the goal of srIvaikuNtam by the grace of those who spread the path of prapaththi by advices and corresponding actions;

and so this prabandham completes the exclusive meanings, which are shown firmly, and by advising others; and by talking about the glory of this [guru paramparai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/), the head of gurus that is [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) helps by making everyone have connection with the [guru paramparai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/) to reach the ultimate state.

– – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous page (avathArikai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai-introduction/)

**pAsuram – 1**

*enthai thiruvAimozhip piLLai innaruLAl*  
*vandha upadhEsa mArkkaththaich chindhai seidhu*  
*pinnavarum kaRka upadhEsamAyp pEsuginREn*  
*manniya seer veNpAvil vaiththu* 1

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-01)

**Word by word meaning**

*enthai* – my master  
*thiruvAimozhip piLLai* – that is, [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)  
*in(iya) aruLAl* – by his sweet/kind distinguished grace,  
*vandha* – what I got (from him)  
*upadhEsa mArkkaththai* – (is) the history of (AchAryas’) teachings;  
*chindhai seidhu* – in thinking of them,  
*pEsuginREn* – I am talking about them  
*upadhEsamAi* – as advice/instructions,  
*vaiththu* – as constructed (in the form of)  
*manniya* – distinguished/well known  
*seer* – greatness  
*veNpAvil* – of vEnpA, a form of thamizh poetry,  
*pinnavarum* – for the generations after me  
*kaRka* – to learn/think/follow.

**vyAkyAnam**

First pAsuram in this – he is taking a vow to convince the minds of those who listen – I shall bring out in the form of a prabandham the exclusive meanings that came in the lineage of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/full-list/) through the grace of my AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)’s teachings, for the future generations to know and attain the goal; by starting with, **‘*enthai thiruvAimozhip piLLai’****.*

That is, he having the name of [thirumalai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), due to his complete devotion to [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) (prabandham), got the name of [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) as known throughout the country. [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) thought about the same and said too as ‘*thirumalai AzhvAr thiruvAimozhip piLLai* \[Arththi prabandham – 21)”. The auspicious meanings the he gave can be fully trusted {thiruvAi?}.

***innaruLAl* –** [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) tries for my revival (ujjeevanam), due to his causeless mercy (nirhEthuka krupai),

[![pillailokacharyar-nayanar-thiruvaimozhipillai-mamunigal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/pillailokacharyar-nayanar-thiruvaimozhipillai-mamunigal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/pillailokacharyar-nayanar-thiruvaimozhipillai-mamunigal.jpg)*[piLLai lOkAcharyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/pillai-lokachryar/), [nAyanAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nayanar/), [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)*

***vandha upadhEsa mArkkaththai*** – the history of the advice/instructions he gave by coming to do that; combine this phrase with the phrase that comes later, *‘upadhEsamAi pEsuginREn’* (saying/passing on/repeating) those advice/instructions). This is following the words/path of what [pUrvAchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) said (sudhdha sampradhAyam – pure lineage), and not saying whatever came to mind and insisting that to be the truth, as [mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says in a later pAsuram ‘*than nenjil thORRinathE solli, idhu suththa upadhEsa**para vArththai** enbar* \[71\]*’*.

So based on the three aforementioned phrases (of the pAsuram?), the association for which he was the target, completeness of true knowledge, and completeness of kindness, are his ([mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s) shelter.

***enthai thiruvAimozhip piLLai innaruLAl vandha* –** As said in ‘*thAyAith thanthaiyAi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.3.2\]’, and ‘*annaiyAi aththanAi* \[[kaNNinUNchiruththAmbu – 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-4-nanmaiyal/)\]’, he is present as my mother and head. As being present as my father, like how one would squirt out into the floor the excessive breast milk, he as a father showed excessive kindness towards me. Like said in *‘eyiRRidai maN koNda enthai irAppagal Odhuviththu ennai* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi – 5.2.3\]*’* (~ emperumAn as a father taught me all the time), thinking about the ways that came in the lineage, through the blessings of his natural father-figure [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), is how [mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is doing this upadhEsam (advice/instructions).

That is, as said in ‘*vivasvAn manavE prAha manur ikshvAkavE abravIth – Evam paramparA prAptha* \[[bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 4-1\]’ (~ sUryan taught vaivasvatha manu; manu taught his son ikshvAku), as the pristine way of knowledge (parisudhdha gyAna mArgam) that came in the lineage, is being considered about.

***mArkkaththaich chinthai seidhu*** – think about the ways/history

***pinnavarum kaRka –*** for the future generation that is going to follow his ways, for them to learn to be in the correct ways; for them to learn, properly as said in ‘*munnOr mozhindha muRai thappAmal kEttup pinnOrndhu* \[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 71\] (properly learn what the previous AchAryas have said, and follow/repeat) ’.

That is, as said in ‘*neRi uLLi uraiththa* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.3.5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruvaimozhi-1-3-5-pinakkara-aruvagai/)\] (~ thought through the correct ways/vEdhas and then explained it), everything that [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), who knows everything, says, are like ‘*sollum avidu suruthiyAm* \[[gyAna sAram – 40](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/05/gyana-saram-40-alli-malar-pavaikku/)\]’ (~whatever is said is the vEdhas), that is, they are of higher reference (pramANa thamam), and are to be reasons for future generations to trust, learn, and follow; he has thought through that and divined this prabandham for us.

{now, the word ‘pEsuginREn’ (saying) is combined with other words of the pAsuram in different interesting ways below, and it brings out the salient thoughts of maNavALa [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) as he set out to write this prabandham}

***upadhEsamAip pEsuginREn –*** {am saying these as advice} (this prabandham has got) it is the weight of meanings of the topic; this prabandham talks in the range – from those interested in surrendering, up to those who are interested in gaining the acceptance of an [AchAryan](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) which is the ultimate state; these are the topics that it talks about as advice, isn’t it?

When advising the distinguished meanings, as ‘*pinnavarum karka upadhEsamAyp pEsuginrEn’,* unlike how [thiruvAimozhip piLLAi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) taught him one-on-one (OrAN vazhi), he is saying that he is enriching through this prabandham for all the sentient people to learn and attain the ultimate goal.

***sindhai seidhu pEsuginREn* –** {am saying these after thinking through} His – ‘*yadhvi manasA dhyAyathi thadh vAchA vadhathi* \[thaiththrIyam AraNyakam 1.23\]’ (what he meditates/thinks in his mind, he says that) – is this prabandham.

***pEsuginREn manniya seer veNpAvil vaiththu –*** {am saying these in the form of great veNpA form of thamizh poetry} when doing that (prabandham/advice), he did so in veNpA (thamizh poetry form); that is, there are many poetry forms for thamizh, like veNpa, kaliththuRai, etc. Out of this, the last prabandham (in 4000) that is rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi is based on kaliththurai; this prabandham is based on the metric of veNpA which is simpler for learning – that is how [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) who loves thamizh has divined this prabandham; he is advising only so that others could learn; veNpA is easy to learn in a couple of practices, that simple this form is.

To explain about the adjective ‘seer’ for the vENpA – its greatness is like said in ‘*pugazh malindha pA* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-1/)\]’; this is also full of greatness. As said in ‘*eNNarum seer poigai munnOr* \[30\]*’,* this greatness of this prabandham goes well with their (AzhvArs’) greatness; to match that greatness, this prabandham is in the great veNpA.

***pEsuginREn –*** {saying} The meaning said in ‘*pEsumaLavanRidhu* \[periya thirumozhi 2.4.9\]’, not being able to tolerate the wrong ways of everyone, I am saying it openly to bring it out in the open; you may listen or avoid, but I would not be able to survive without saying it (as advice/instructions). For those who surrendered, as said in ‘*prOvAchathAm thathvathO brahmavidhyAm* \[muNdakOpanishath 1.2.13\]’ (knowledge about brahmam should be taught as is), I am saying the meanings that have to be said – so he is doing this without expecting any request from us – that is the greatness of his kindness isn’t it?

By this we conclude that, like when sarvEsvaran gave [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) unblemished knowledge ([mayarvaRA madhinalam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)), [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) in turn gave that to the village, country, and world for them to be like him, and made them get unblemished knowledge and survive; here [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) also is advising the knowledge he got due to [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/)’s grace, and letting us reach the destiny.

– – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – २
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (enthai thiruvAimozhip piLLai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai-1/)

**pAsuram – 2**

*kaRROrgaL thAm ugappar kalvi thannil Asai uLLOr*  
*peRROm ena ugandhu pinbu kaRpar – maRROrgaL*  
*mAchcharyaththAl igazhil vandhadhen nenjE igazhgai*  
*AchcharyamO thAnavarkku* 2

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-02)

**Word by word meaning:**

kaRROrgaL thAm – those having the knowledge by education  
ugappar – will be happy;  
Asai uLLOr – those who wish  
kalvi thannil – to get the education  
ugandhu – would be happy  
pinbu – and then  
kaRpar – would learn / practice;  
maRROrgaL – others / (uninterested ones),  
mAchchariyaththAl – due to jealousy,  
igazhil – if they find faults / ridicule  
en – what  
vandhadhu – bad would be there?  
AchchariyamO – would it be a surprise (no)  
thAnavarkku – if demoniacal personalities  
igazhgai – find faults in other things?

[![maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup.jpg)*[maNavALamAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) as giving darshan at thiruvaheendhrapuram*

**vyAkyAnam**

He asks in his mind, “dhEvarIr (your highness) divined ‘*pinnavarum kaRka upadhEsamAip pEsuginREn manniya seer veNpAvil vaiththu* \[[pAsuram 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai-1/)\]’ (that I am saying it as an advice using veNpA poetry form, for future generation to learn and follow), but those who are immersed in jealousy would criticize this effort wouldn’t they?”; and then he calms down his mind by saying that there is no harm done, and such behaviour of them is nothing to be surprised about.

***kaRROrgaL thAm ugappar –*** As said in ‘*aRiyak kaRRu vallAr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.5.11\]’ (~ those who learn and understand well), such [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) would be happy, saying, Ah! he is advising through this prabandham what we wanted to advise; Or the meaning for the phrase can be said as: those who learned this prabandham through their AchAryan (will be happy);

next it talks about the nature of those who, unlike such learned people, are interested in now learning and understanding this:

***kalvi thannil Asai uLLOr peRROm ena ugandhu pinbu kaRpar*** – When we would have had to learn with great efforts from those who have learned and understood, now we are getting very easily through this prabandham! – and so the people who are very interested in learning this would say and become happy like they got a big wealth, by getting this, *(pinbu kaRpar)* and they would learn well from those who have learned and understood well, and be satisfied.

**maRROrgal etc. –** different from the aforementioned two kinds of people – Others;

They are: ‘*aRindhavar pAl chenRu sErudhal (seRidhal) seyyA\[dha\] thee manaththar* ([gyAna sAram – 27](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/gyana-saram-27-neri-ariyadharum/)\]’ (bad-hearted ones who would not go to and learn from the learned);

***mAchchariyaththAl igazhil –*** if they find faults due to jealousy.. jealousy is – as said in ‘*piRar minukkam poRAmai* \[Arththi prabandham – 55\], others’ jealousy is shown in real; that is, if they cannot tolerate the growth/greatness of others and if they find fault and ridicule/spurn;

***vandhadhu en nenjE*** – Oh mind! as you are fully in congruence with the one ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) who possesses all the glories, there is no worry/problem (if they find faults); since they are ‘*manakkuRRa mAndhar* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-5/)\]’ (~people whose mind is faulty), if they ridicule, then that would be a praise is what we think isn’t it?

{This 2^(nd) pAsuram is very similar to the [5th pAsuram of rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-5/) where [amudhanar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/26/thiruvarangathu-amudhanar/) first tries to back out thinking about those others who would find faults with the prabandham }

Still if they would ridicule shouldn’t we stop (the prabandham),
