***igazhgai AchchariyamO thAnavarkku –*** *for* those who would grow plump when they ridicule (happy to be ridiculing others), it is not a surprize if they ridicule (our prabandham). So it is according to their nature;

From this, we conclude that the liking and disliking of good and the bad people respectively both would add to the greatness of the prabandham.

– – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ३
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (kaRROrgaL thAm ugappar)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-2/)

**pAsuram – 3  **

*AzhvArgaL vAzhi aruLichcheyal vAzhi*  
*thAzhvAdhumil kuravar thAm vAzhi – Ezh pArum*  
*uyya avargaL uraiththavaigaL thAm vAzhi*  
*seyya maRai thannudanE sErndhu* 3

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-03)

**Word by word meaning**

*AzhvArgaL* – the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*vAzhi* – shall live forever;  
*aruLichcheyal* – [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that they divined  
*vAzhi* – shall live forever;  
*il* – not having  
*Adhu thAzhvum* – any lows  
*kuravar thAm* – that is, [pUrvAchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)  
*vAzhi* – shall live forever;  
*Ezh pArum* – all those in all the seven worlds,  
*uyya* – for them to reach the destiny (ujjeevanam)  
*avargaL* – those [pUrvAchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) (preceptors)  
*uraiththavaigaL thAm* – divined exclusive and sacred meanings ([vyAkyAna rahasyams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/));  
*sErndhu* – together with (those [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)),  
*seyya* – the virtuous/pure  
*maRai thannudanE* – that is vEdhas,  
*vAzhi* – shall live forever.

**vyAkyAnam**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-2/) after getting convinced that the insult of those Others is a praise only, as he continued on divining the prabandham, for the badness that might come from the adversaries to be removed, he who is agreeable performs mangaLAsAsanam to those related to [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), and for the [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) created by them, starting with ‘*AzhvArgaL vAzhi’.*

This pAsuram serves as a summary of the pAsurams that follow in this prabandham. That is, about the glories of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), the glories of [aruLichcheyal (prabandhams)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), the glories of those who spread about them/these, that is, the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), and the glories of the [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) divined by those [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), are what this prabandham (upadhEsa raththinamAlai) shows us. So this pAsuram can be considered as ‘*uLLathukkellAm churukkAi* \[upadhEsa raththina mAlai 19\]’, that is, it can be said that the summary of this prabandham is this pAsuram.

[![Azhvars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)

[![srivaishna-guruparamparai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)

***AzhvArgaL vAzhi –*** they are – after getting ‘*mayarvaRa madhi nalam* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\]’, they are being ‘*theruLuRRa AzhvArgaL* \[upadhEsa raththina mAlai 36\]’, ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) having divine knowledge), that is [nammAzhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) et al. For such noble ones, he is doing mangaLAsAsanam to avoid the touch of blemishes of the birth, and for them to live well forever; singing pallANdu to the ones who are earnest in singing pallANdu, is the work of mahAmunis; he is too maNavALa*mAmuni*.

‘*vAzhi satakOpan, vAzhi parakAlan* \[iyal sARRu\]’ is how those who love these [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) would say.

***aruLichcheyal vAzhi* –** aruLichcheyal are – by the grace of [sarvEsavaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) to them, they showed grace/mercy and divined the ones that can be the identity for the four vEdhas and their angams (subs); that is [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and other [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/). He is doing mangaLAsAsanam that these distinguished [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) should continue in vogue forever without having shortcomings of place, time, or author.

Would say, ‘*vAzhi satakOpan ittath thamizhp pAvisai* \[iyal sARRu\]’ (lovely thamizh pAsuram of [satakOpan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) shall live forever), and ‘*vAzhi parakAlan eNNil thamizhp pAvisai* \[iyal sARRu\]’.

***thAzhvAdhum il kuravar*** ***–*** Next, since those who are always discussing and thinking about the meanings of these ([prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), that is the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), are also to be blessed, so he is doing mangaLAsAsanam to them; the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) are – ‘*aruL peRRa nAthamuni* *mudhalAna nam dhEsikar*\[36\]’, that is, our [Acharyas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) starting from [nAthamuni](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/), [yAmunAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/alavandhar/), and [ethirAjar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/); now by ‘*thAzhvAdhum il’,* that is, not having any deficiency, means, being enthusiastic/interested in [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) only. Deficiency is, spending time in kAvyam (other stories), listening to the speeches which are not in any way about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), etc. Not having that (deficiency) is, spending time only in purANas, etc., that involve [bhagavAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s glories. By ‘*Adhumil*’ it means, as said in ‘*theedhil anthAdhi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.2.11\]’, (pAsuram that does not have anything bad), not contains any other stories but only interested in talking about [bhagavAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – such is the aruLichcheyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) – them spending time only in that, and considering it as the only benefit for us;

In the vyAkyAnam of periya thirumozhi 5.8.7, when explaining the word ‘*oruvan*’ (~the unique person) – it says: ‘*muRpada dhvayaththaik kaRRu, pOdhu pOkkum aruLich cheyalilEyAy, (nam)piLLaiyaip pOlE iruppAn oruvan*’ (~ (he) learned dhvayam’s meanings, and is spending time in [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), a glorious person like [nampiLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nampillai/));

seeing such AchArya’s vaibhavam, [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) understanding their greatness is the person doing mangaLAsAsanam to them, like ‘*indaLaththilE thAmarai pUththAr pole indha vibhUthiyil ivargaL silarE’* (like a lotus blossoming in an incense stand (hot/dry?), in a world like this, these ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) have incarnated!).

‘*vAzhi ethirAsan* \[Arththi prabandham – 1\]*’*, and ‘*vAzhi ulagAsiriyan* \[[mumukshuppadi](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2013/10/aippasi-anubhavam-pillai-lokacharyar-mumukshuppadi.html) thaniyan\]’ ([piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/) shall live forever), are the ways of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s words.

***Ezh pArum uyya avargaL uraiththavaigaL thAm vAzhi*** – that is, the [AchAryAs](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)’ [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) are such that they would help the people of this world of seven parts surrounded on both sides by water, to reach the goal; as said in ‘*ulagu uyya umbargaLum kEttuyya* \[iyal sARRu\], their vyAkyAnam helps all the worlds.

When doing that,

***seyya maRai thannudanE sErndhu*** – dhEvareers (all your highness) who are well versed in all the sAsthram, created the [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) whose greatness is such that all its meanings are given based on the sAsthram. Or, the noble meanings of your [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) are such that the sAsthras could follow it too – as said in ‘*vidhayachcha vaidhikA: sthvadheeya kambheera manOnusAriNa:* \[sthOthra rathnam – 20\]’ (even the commands of vEdhas are of the nature of following the deep/profound intellect of your devotees).

*‘seyya mArai thannudanE sErndhu avargaL uraiththavaigaL thAm vAzhi**’*** (along with the virtuous vEdhas, what the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) have spoken ([vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) shall live forever) is the way of blessing them when seeing their greatness.

[![Hinduscriptures](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Hinduscriptures.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Hinduscriptures.jpg)

*Courtesy: <https://ramanan50.wordpress.com/2014/05/31/hindu-scriptures-list/>
(Dec 03 2015)*

**seyya maRai** – vEdham shows its meanings to the righteous, and hides to the others; after joining the [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), the vEdhas have become virtuous. That is, ‘*alpa shruthar kalakkina shruthi nan gnyAnaththuRai sErndhu, theLivuRRu, Azh poruLai aRiviththadhu* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 71\], by the pristine meanings provided by [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) is how one could see the deep/true meanings of vEdhas.

Thus he performed mangaLAsAsanam that the blemishes of kali yuga should not touch those ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) who understand and follow the distinguished references (pramANams), and should live forever, without any blemishes, etc.

It is said, ‘*pramANancha pramEyancha pramAthAachcha sAthvikA: \|
jayanthu kshapithArishtam saha sarvathra sarvadhA* \[srIbhAshya srutha prakAsikA thaniyan – 8\]’ (the one that is the reason for true knowledge (reference/pramANam), and what is identified by pramANam ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), and those who get the knowledge through the pramANam (preceptors/[AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) – let the inauspicious aspects be destroyed, and victory to them together, at all places and at all times).

– – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ४
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvArgaL vAzhi)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)

**pAsuram 4**

*poigaiyAr bhUthaththAr pEyAr pugazh mazhisai*  
*ayyan aruL mAran sEralarkOn – thuyya patta*  
*nAthan anbar thAL thULi naRpANan naRkaliyan*  
*eedhivar thORRaththu adaivAm ingu 4*

[pAsuram 4](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-04)

**Word by word meaning**

*poigaiyAr –* [poigai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
*bhUthaththAr* – [bhUthaththAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
*pEyAr* – [pEyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
*pugazh* – famous  
*mazhisai ayyan* – [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)  
*aruL* – having mercy/kindness  
*mARan* – [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)  
*sEralarkOn* – [kulasEkaraAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)  
*thuyya* – pure  
*pattanAthan* – [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)  
*anbar thAL thULi* – [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)  
*nan* – having the goodness  
*pANan* – [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)  
*nal* – good  
*kaliyan* – [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)  
*eedhu* – this thus said  
*adaivu Am* – is the order of  
*ivar* – their  
*thORRaththu* – incarnations  
*ingu* – in this world.

**vyAkyAnam**

In the prabandham starting with ‘*AzhvArgaL vAzhi* \[[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)\]’, what he listed, he wished to show about them one by one, and as he had mentioned the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) first, here he is showing the order in which they incarnated, starting the pAsuram with – ‘*poigaiyAr’.*

That is, as he was born in the lotus flower in the pond, that is being his identity (poigai – pond), and as said in ‘*varuththum puRa iruL mARRa* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/09/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-8/)\] (~(incarnated) to remove the troubles of darkness in mind from things seen), that is our [**poigai** Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/);

[![PoigaiAzhvAr_thirukkachchi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/PoigaiAzhvAr_thirukkachchi.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/PoigaiAzhvAr_thirukkachchi.png)*poigai AzhvAr as divining in his avathAra sthalam*

As said in ‘*mAdhavan **bhUtham*** \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.2.2\]’, he having the glory, who lighted ‘*gyAnach chudar viLakku* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi – 1\]’ (lighting of lamp that is true knowledge); that is, [bhUthaththAzhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/);

[![bhuthathAzhvar_thirukkadal_mallai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/bhuthathAzhvar_thirukkadal_mallai-637x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/bhuthathAzhvar_thirukkadal_mallai.jpg)

Is interested only in enjoying [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), not paying attention to the ways of the material world, (and so) saying like in ‘*yAnum Or pEyan* \[perumAL thirumozhi 3.8\]’, which name is his identity, and who is ‘*kOvaluL mAmalarAL thannodu mAyanaik kaNdamai kAttum thamizhth thalaivan* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi
-10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-10/)\]*’* that is he who showed him having the vision of pirAtti and [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) (in idai kazhi thirukkOvalUr); that is, **pEyAr** ([pEyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/));

[![mayilai_peyazhvar_at_thiruvallikkeni (Large)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mayilai_peyazhvar_at_thiruvallikkeni-Large-680x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mayilai_peyazhvar_at_thiruvallikkeni-Large.jpg)*mayilai pEyazhvAr, during a visit to thiruvallikkENi*

***pugazh mazhisai ayyan*** – As said in ‘*idam koNda kIrththi mazhisaikku iRaivan* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-11/)\] ’ the head of [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/) which is also known as mahIsAra kshEthram, that is [thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/).

[![thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited.png)*thirumazhisaip pirAn at thirumazhisai*

***aruL mARan –*** As said in ‘*pAdinAn aruL kaNdIr ivvulaginil mikkadhE* \[[kaNNinuNchiruththAmbu – 8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiru-thambu-8-arul-kondadum/)\]*’*, he is very kind, that is being his identity, that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/).

[![Azhvar_AzhvarThirunagari_VaikasiUthsavam_IMG_6413-Edited](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Azhvar_AzhvarThirunagari_VaikasiUthsavam_IMG_6413-Edited.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Azhvar_AzhvarThirunagari_VaikasiUthsavam_IMG_6413-Edited.jpg)*nammAzhvAr at AzhvAr thirunagari*

***sEralarkOn –*** As said in ‘*chEran kulasEkaran* \[perumAL thirumozhi thaniyan\]’, he is the head of the clan of chEra kings, and he liked to be born as bird and plants (to be in [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)‘s abode in thirumalai), that is [kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/);

[![kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809.jpg)*kulasEkarapperumAL at thiruvanjikkaLam*

***thuyya patta nAthan –*** Having the purity of doing mangaLAsAsanam (pallANdu) to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and assuming the state of cowherd, and as said in ‘*vEdhAntha vizhup poruLin mEl irundha viLakkai vittu chiththan viriththana* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 4.3.11\]’, he established greatness and so is having the identity of head of the learned, that is patta nAthan, which is [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html);

[![srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)*periyAzhvAr at [srIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/)*

**anbar thAL thULi –** {anbar -\> thoNdar, thAL -\> adi, thULi -\> podi } As he said in ‘*thuLavath thoNdAya thol seerth thoNdaradippodi* \[thirumAlai 45\], he thought that the (first) birth of being a brAhmaNa with the haughtiness thinking that is of higher birth would cause suffering, and so preferred being the dust of the feet of the bhAgavathAs who do not have such egos, and that itself being his identity, that is **srI** [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/);

[![Mandangudi Thondaradipodi Azhwar-003](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mandangudi-Thondaradipodi-Azhwar-003-768x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mandangudi-Thondaradipodi-Azhwar-003.jpg)*thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr at thirumaNdankudi*

**naR pANan –** As he said in ‘*adiyArkku ennai Atpaduththa vimalan* \[amalanAdhipirAn – 1\], he having the goodness of having nature of birth that is amicable to being subservient / lowness;  
such head of the prabandham, that is pAN perumAL ([thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)).  
{  
Here the vyAkyAnam words reflect what is said in srIvachana bhUshaNam;  
**Here:** *thadhIya dhAsyaththukku anuguNamAna janma sidhdhamAna naichchiyaththai nanmaiyAga udaiyarAi*;

[![thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj.jpg)*thiruppANAzhvAr at uraiyUr*

**In srI vachana bhUshaNam:** *naichchiyam janma sidhdham; AgaiyAl uthkrushta janmamE srEshtam*  
}

**naR kaliyan –** As he said in ‘*nin thiruvettezhuththum kaRRu nAn uRRadhum un adiyArkku adimai* \[periya thirumozhi – 8.10.3\] (~ what I became after learning the manthra of eight words is being subservient to your devotees); and in ‘*adiyavargaL tham adiyAn’* \[periya thirumozhi – 2.6.10\]’, involved in the pinnacle of subservience, that is, to the devotees, like thinking that being subservient to the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) is his identity, having such goodness, and due to robbing things including conch (arugAzhi) (from [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) and so is identified as ‘kaliyan’ (having such strength), that is , [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/);

[![kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar (Large)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large-1024x680.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large.jpg)*thirumangai AzhvAr at thiruvAli thirunagari*

So, this concludes about them who are having such distinguished greatness, the order in which they incarnated in this world; like saying ‘*kAN perum thORRam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.6.9\]’, and ‘*AvirbhUtham* \[vishNu purANam 5.3.1\]’, they incarnated with distinction.

– – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ५
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (poigaiyAr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-4/)

**pAsuram – 5**

*anthamizhAl naRkaligaL AyndhurRaiththa AzhvArgaL*  
*intha ulagil iruL neenga – vandhu udhiththa*  
*mAthangaL nALgaL thammai maNNulagOr thAm aRiya*  
*eethenRu solluvOm yAm*  5

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-05)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*am* – (in the) beautiful  
*thamizhAl* – language of thamizh,  
*AzhvArgaL* – [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*Ayndhu* – researched  
nal – good  
*kalaigaL* – vEdhas  
*uraiththa* – and divined (the [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), for )  
*iruL* – the darkness that is ignorance  
*indha ulagil* – in this world  
*neenga* – to be destroyed;  
*solluvOm* – (adiyEn – I) shall say  
*eedhu enRu* – these are the  
*mAthangaL* – months, and  
*nALgaL thammai* – thirunakshathrams (auspicious star days)  
*vandhu udhiththa* – in which they came and incarnated,  
*maN ulagOr thAm aRiya* – for the people in this world to know.

**vyAkyAnam**

Then, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) says that I shall divine the months and star days of incarnation of these [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), for everyone to know.

[![azhwars-sriperumbuthur-with-sEnai-mudhaliyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/azhwars-sriperumbuthur-with-sEnai-mudhaliyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/azhwars-sriperumbuthur-with-sEnai-mudhaliyar.jpg)[ANdAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/andal/), [sEnai mudhaliyAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/vishwaksenar/) and [AzhwArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) – [srIperumbUthUr](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/) – pagal paththu uthsavam

[![mamunigal-sriperumbuthur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mamunigal-sriperumbuthur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mamunigal-sriperumbuthur.jpg)[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) – [srIperumbUthUr](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/)

***anthamizhAl naRkalaigaL Ayndhu uraiththa AzhvArgaL –*** Unlike vEdham which is in the form of samskrutham, which has got eligibility criteria to recite it, with having difficulty in trying to figure out the meanings of karma kANtam and brahma kANtam, prabandham is having the greatness of being of pure/simple thamizh, it is being easy for everyone, and is in the enjoyable thamizh language – that is the language in which they ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)) have divined it ([prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) after having researched and understood the vEdhas well, like said in ‘*paNNiya thamizh* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.7.13\] (~ created in thamizh)’.

*naRkalai* is – the unblemished vEdham that is the reference. [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) researched/thought through and divined its meanings in thamizh. So this is ‘*thirumAlavan kavi* \[thiruviruththam – 48\]’, that is, would talk only about the almighty who is [the husband of srIdhEvi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/).

The reason for [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), who are not touched by births, to incarnate here is the following as he explains:

***intha ulagil iruL neenga vandhu udhiththa* –** It is in this world where there is darkness; ‘*iruL tharumA gyAlam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.1\]. *That* world is ‘*athyarkanaladhIptham* \[mahAbhAratham vana parvam 164-18\]’, that is, brighter than the sun, fire, etc., and as said in ‘*sudaroLiyAy ninRa thannudaich chOthi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.10.5\]’ (~ srIvaikuNtam that is of light). So, those in paramapadham, as said in ‘*sUryakOti prathIkAsa*: \[lakshmI thanthram\]’ (bright as a crore of suns), and ‘*oLikkoNda sOdhiyamAy* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.3.10\]’ (having the bright light), and as said in ‘*sarvam hi paSya: paSyathi* \[chAndhOgya upanishath 26-2\]’ (sees everything directly, isn’t it?), they would be bright with knowledge/truth; So in that world there is no question of being blind to the truth, or, no darkness;

As said in ‘*pin ivvulaginil pEr iruL* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 1.8.10\]’, this world is material as the meaning of the word ‘*thamas*’. So we in this world take up the dirty body that hides us from [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s nature, and as said in ‘*aRivilA manisar* \[thirumAlai – 13\]’, we are without true knowledge; clarity in knowledge is required for us only. Only those caught in darkness would need the light of sun, etc. So he is saying in this pAsuram, ‘*indha ulagil iruL neenga vandhu udhiththa*’.

For removing the darkness of this world, don’t we need these kinds of suns: ‘*vandhE parAnkusAdhithyam* \[AzhvAr mukthakam\]’ (salute to the sun that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)), and ‘*kalayAmi kalidhvamsam kavimlOka dhivAkaram* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ (being one who removes the problems of kali yuga, being one who is a **sun** for the world, I meditate on such [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)), and ‘*rAmAnuja dhivAkara:* \[varavaramuni mukthakam – 6\] (sun that is [rAmAnujar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)); from their rising is how the darkness of ignorance was destroyed, and ‘thamas’ based illiteracy was destroyed, birth of reduction of sins (*pApa dhvAntha kshayam*): only in the presence of such vishNu devotees would the darkness that is spread everywhere would leave. This implicitly applies to other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) as well.

***vandhu udhiththa mAdhangaL, nALgaL thammai, maNNulagOr thAm aRiya eedhenRu solluvOm yAm –*** that is, like the the twelve ways suns each are in the month of chiththirai (ChithrA), etc. In the same way, [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) too incarnated in respective order, starting from the month of aippasi (asvina). ‘*vandhu udhiththa’* shows that they came from paramapadham and rose in this world.

Months (of their incarnations) are: seven months starting from the month of aippasi (asvina) through Ani (jyEshta);

Days are to be said as ‘*aththaththin paththA nAL* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 1.2.6\]’, and ‘*thirunAL thiruvONam* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 2.3.9\]’ (for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s star day of incarnation).

Here too it is starting from thiruvONam (sravaNa) till kEttai (jyEshta) the ten star days in between.

Only by learning about these that can create auspiciousness would one get the goal.

It is said, ‘*janmarkshE shravaNEpivA* \[dharma sAsthram\]’ (in the start of birth and in thiruvONam (sravaNa).

Since their incarnation is special related to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), similar to rOhiNi, punarpUsam (punarvasu), etc., their star days of incarnation are also for celebration and nurturing.

***maNNulagOr thAm aRiya*** *–* Like said in ‘*agal gyAlaththu avar aRiya* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.8.6\]’, there is no need to advise/educate those in the other world; as said in ‘*maNNil piRandhu … angu eNNam onRinRi irukkum Ezhai manisarkAL* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 4.6.7\]’ (~ Oh poor people, being born in this earth, and not having any thoughts about that world) – for people of this world only there is a need to advise/educate.

***maNNulagOr thAm aRiya* –** To those born in this earth, the devotees who do not have the true knowledge **–** for them to know (about the months and start days of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ incarnations) and celebrate, and who are not trying to know that this is the way to reach the goal, let me, who is very interested in it. shall explain to them without their requesting for the details – is how [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s oath is.

From this, it is shown that AchAryan’s ways is to teach us what we do not know.

– – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ६
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (anthamizhAl naRkalaigaL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-5/)

**pAsuram 6**

*aippasiyil ONam avittam sathayam ivai*  
*oppilavA nALgaL ulagaththIr – eppuviyum*  
*pEsu pugazhp poigaiyAr bhUthaththAr pEyAzhvAr*  
*thEsudanE thOnRu siRappAl* 6

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-06)

  
**Word by word meaning0**

ulagaththIr – Oh those of this world!  
pugazh – having the greatness  
eppuviyum – of people of all the worlds  
pEsu – talking/praising about  
poigaiyAr – [poigai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/),  
bhUthaththAr – [bhUthathAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/), and  
pEyAzhvAr – [peyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
thOnRu – coming to this world  
thEsudanE – with thEjas (brightness/majesty)  
(si)piRappAl – by incarnation,  
aippasiyil – [in the month of aippasi](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/aippasi-thula-masa-anubhavam.html), (and in the star days of)  
Onam – thiruvONam, and  
avittam –avittam, and  
sathayam –sathayam  
ivai – these,  
oppilavAm – are unparalleled  
nALgaL – star days.

**vyAkyAnam**

As per the vow in the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-5/), [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) wishes to start in orderly manner, and he first divines the ways of incarnations of [mudhal AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) (first three AzhvArs), by starting with ‘*aippasiyil Onam*’.

That is, [in the month of aippasi](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/aippasi-thula-masa-anubhavam.html), the star day of [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) which is thiruvONam, and then avittam, and sathayam, these three are unparalleled.

Oh you who do not know the propriety of conduct based on vEdhas, and have set your eyes on the life in this material world! Please celebrate the unparalleled days and reach the correct goal.

To talk about why those days are unparalleled,

***eppuviyum, etc –*** All those in all the worlds were saying ‘that! that!’ about the greatness in the [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) being born in flowers, and due to their brightness of knowledge they have the greatness of seeing [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) in their mind, having the greatness of ‘*nAttArOdu iyalvu ozhindhu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.2\]’ (~ not following the material ways of the people) they were moving to different places and were staying in a village in the night {thirukkOvalUr}, moreover, as said in ‘*thUvadivil pUmagaL pAr mangaiyOdu* \[periya thirumozhi 2.10.9\]’ and so on, the husband of srIdhEvi that is sarvEsvaran wanted to join the [AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) physically and so as said in ‘*pulavar nerukka ugandha perumAL’* (perumAn who was happy when pushed by poets), having the greatness of being able to make [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) happy by their closeness/pushing of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and so these are being praised by the world.

[![thirukovalur-perumal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirukovalur-perumal-756x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirukovalur-perumal.jpg)*thirukkOvalUr idai kazhi Ayan – srI dhEhaLeesa perumAL*

When asked who they are,

***poigaiyAr bhUthaththAr pEyAr*** *–* they are [poigai AzhvAr, bhUthaththAzhvAr, and pEyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/).

***thEsudanE thOnRu –*** (thEjas /brightness) they incarnated with the brightness which is their natural subservience to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/).

Since the wealth came due to that, those days are unparalleled.

As said in ‘*Azhiyankaip pErAyarkkALAm piRappu* \[periyA thiruvanthAdhi – 36\]’, it is the brightness of parama padham (srIvaikuNtam).

As said in ‘*karuvarangaththuL kidandhu kai thozhudhEn kaNdEn* \[mudhal thiruvanthAdhi – 6\], and in ‘*karukkOttiyuL kidandhu kai thozhudhEn kaNdEn* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi – 87\], and in ‘*karuvirundha nAL mudhalAk kAppu* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 92\], they are having natural subservience. So they are of extreme greatness.

(mAmunigaL) very much loves these star days, and he is loved by these [AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) – he is having such greatness. [![mudhal_azhwars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhal_azhwars-1024x720.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhal_azhwars.jpg)

Moreover, [in the month of aippasi](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/aippasi-thula-masa-anubhavam.html), that thiruvONam star day is [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)‘s star birthday, and also of the one who is the most excellent srIvaishNava who is ‘*krishNapAdhasya sUnu* \[[thathva thrayam thaniyan](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/thathva-thrayam.html)\], (the divine son of [vadakkuth thiruvIdhip piLLAi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)), that is – of [piLLai lOkAchAryar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/), so [varavaramuni Acharyar jIyar (maNavALa mAmunigaL)](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/11/archavathara-anubhavam-mamunigal.html) with great love, nurtured this day, and set about celebrating regularly with care – this is well known.

These star days also are three (of [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)) (muppuri Uttiya – where 3 great incidents happen on the same time/day/place)

As said in ‘*kriyAdhikArE ashtasAdhyAyE sravaNam cha AchvayangmAsE sarvapApa haramparam \|mathsya kUrma varAhANAm AvirbhAva dhinam smrutham* \[srI pAncharAthram\]’ (In the eighteenth chapter, it talks about the star day of thiruvONam in the month of aippasi, the incarnations by mathsya (fish), kUrma (tortoise/turtle), and varAha (boar), which would remove all the sins).

As said in ‘*hAritha: – mAsE bhAdhrapadhE chuklE dhvAdhashyAm vishNu dhaivathE* \| *adhithyAmdhayAth vishNurupEndhrO vAmanO vyaya:* ’ (in the month of purattasi, Sukla dhvAdhasi, [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) incarnated like a rising sun like an Indra, as vAmanan).

{So the star days of incarnations of these [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) are also special, unparalleled, and celebrated by all}

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ७
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (aippasiyil ONam)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-6/)

**pAsuram 7  **

*maRRuLLa AzhvArgaLukku munnE vandhu udhiththu*  
*naRRamizhAl nUl seidhu nAttai uyththa – peRRimaiyOr*  
*enRu mudhal AzhvArgaL ennum peyar ivarkku*  
*ninRadhu ulagaththE nighazhndhu * 7

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-07)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*munnE –* Before  
*maRRuLLa AzhvArgaLukku –* the other seven [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/),  
*vandhu –* (the first [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)) came to the earth  
*udhiththu* – and incarnated,  
*nal* – (and in) good  
*thamizhAl* – language thamizh  
*seidhu* – (they) divined (aruLich cheydhu)  
*nUl* – the dhivya prabandhams – mudhal thiruvanthAdhi, iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi, and mUnRAm thiruvanthAdhi  
*nAttai* *uyththa* – and made the people in the world reach the true goal (ujjIvikkumpadi);  
*peRRimaiyOr* *enRu* – due to their having such greatness  
*ivarkku* – these [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
*nigazhndhu* – are referred to with the  
*peyar* – divine name of  
*mudhalAzhvArgaL* *ennum* – mudhal AzhvArgaL (first/foremost [AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/))  
*ninRadhu* – which got well established  
*ulagaththu* – in the world.

**vyAkyAnam**

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining the reason for them getting the name of mudhalAzhvArgal, by starting with ‘*maRRuLLa AzhvAgaL’*.

Out of the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), these [three mudhalAzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) incarnated before the other seven [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/).

The first [three AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) are supreme like the praNavam (Om). They incarnated between the end of dhvApara yuga and beginning of kali yuga {several years pass between two yugams }. To indicate that too they are called as mudhalAzhvArgaL.

[![mudhal_azhwars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhal_azhwars-1024x720.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhal_azhwars.jpg)*mudhalAzhvArs*

[thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) also incarnated during similar times, and the rest of the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) incarnated during kali yuga, starting from the beginning of the yuga.

Now,

***naRRamizhAl nuL seidhu*** is, in the best language that is thamizh, very distinguished from other prabandhams, is their creation of dhivya prabandhams that is thamizh vEdham. They are thiruvanthAdhis of, ‘*vaiyam thagaLi* \[mudhal thiruvanthAdhi\]’, ‘*anbE thagaLi* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi\]’, and ‘*thiruk kaNdEN* \[mUnRAm thiruvanthAdhi\]’ .

The prabandhams and their thamizh are of the nature that can be celebrated as said in ‘*senchoR kavaigAL* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.7.1\]’, and ‘*senthamizh pAduvAr* \[periya thirumozhi 2.8.2\]’, and ‘*inkavi pAdum parama kavigaLAl* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.9.6\]’.

They themselves valued it saying ‘*perum thamizhan nallEn peridhu* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi – 74\]’.

Their greatness is such that they would celebrate their and others’ [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) about the thamizh and its formation.

With such greatness through their prabandhams, they removed the darkness (ignorance) in this world, and made people reach the true goal – due to such greatness they together got the name of ‘mudhalAzhvArgaL’ (first/foremost [AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)), as referred to by the world.

*peRRimai :* perumai – greatness/nobleness. Due to this, it shows their pre-eminence as said in ‘*janmanA vidhyAcha*’ (by birth and by education/knowledge).

– – – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ८
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (maRRuLLa AzhvArgaLukku)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-7/)

**pAsuram 8**

*pEdhai nenjE inRaip perumai aRindhilaiyO*  
*Edhu perumai inRaikku enRiyEl (en ennil) – OdhuginRen*  
*vAyththa pugazh mangaiyar kOn mAnilaththil vandhu udhiththa*  
*kArththikaiyil kArththikai nAL kAN 8*

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-08)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*nenjE* – Oh the mind,  
*pEdhai* – not having the true knowledge,  
*aRindhilaiyO – have you not known*  
*perumai* – the glory (vaibhavam) of  
*inRai* – this day?  
*enRiyEl* (en ennil) – If you ask  
*Edhu perumai* – what is the greatness  
*inRaikku* – of this day, then  
*OduginREn* – I shall say that to you; that is,  
*mangaiyar kOn* – [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)  
*vAyththa* – having fitting  
*pugazh* – glory  
*vandhu udhiththa* – came and divined his incarnation  
*mAnilaththil* – in this big world  
*kArththikaiyil* – in the month of kArththikai  
*kArththikai nAL* – in the star day of kruththikAi;  
*kAN* – you learn about this.

[![kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar (Large)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large-1024x680.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large.jpg)*thirumangai AzhvAr – thiruvAli thirunagari*

**vyAkyAnam**

Then [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining as a question and answer to his mind regarding the glory of [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)’s incarnation day of thirukkArththikai divine star day, starting this with *‘pEdhai nenjE’.*

Unlike the earlier pAsuram where [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) said ‘*eedhu ivar thORRaththu adaivAm* \[[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-4/)\] which was in the order of incarnations of [Azhvars](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), from this pAsuram [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is presenting in the order of months in which various [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) incarnated. For the sentients, this also would be a sequence to keep in their mind. It is convenient too to go in the order of months.

***pEdhai nenjE inRaip perumai aRindhilaiyO –*** Oh the ignorant mind which thinks the other days as equivalent to this special day! The reason of our reaching the true goal that is enabled by this star day is something you could reflect upon, but are you not aware of this important day?

***Edhu perumai inRaikku enRiyEl (en ennil)* –** If you ask ‘What is the greatness of this day compared to the other days? Should you who know its greatness not divine it?’, then

***OdhuginREn –*** I, who has understood, shall preach that to you (the mind) who has not understood it.

***vAiththa pugazh , etc. –*** As said in ‘*manRil mali pugazh mangai mannan* \[periya thirumozhi 11.2.10\]’, he having the glory that matches his svarUpam (nature), the king of thirumangai, incarnated in this great world in the month of kArththikai , in the star day of kArththikai – you note this – is what I am preaching you.

The glory of his is – as said in ‘*mAyOnai vAL valiyAl manthiram koL* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ (he got the rahasyam that is thirumanthram from mAyOn ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) using his strength of his sword);

It continues as ‘*manthiram koL *mangaiyar* kOn* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ (one who got the thirumanthram, he is the king of thirumangai). It is the gain of thirumanthram that is the reason for the glory of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/).

vAyththa – obtained/got.

It is ‘*vAyththa thirumanthiram* \[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 26\]’ (~ the great thirumanthram is available (for us)).

Or, the place ‘mangai’ *got* the glory due to this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)’s incarnation.

***mangaiyar kOn mAnilaththil vandhu udhiththa kArththikaiyil kArththikai nAL kAN* –** Such [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) the ruler of thirumangai, incarnated in the month of kArththikai in the star day of kArththikai, to remove the ‘thamas’ that is darkness (ignorance) from this world that is said as ‘*iruL tharumA gyAlam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.1\]’ (~ material world that creates darkness) – learn this.

Since in ‘*kalayAmi kali dhvamsam kavim lOka dhivAkaram* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ it is referring to [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) as a (rising) sun, here [he (maNavALa mAmunigaL)](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is also using the word ‘*vandhu udhiththa’* (rise/rose) to describe the incarnation of [thirumangai Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/).

In this way he had manifested (AvirbhAvam), I have understood this greatness and am preaching this to you (the mind), and you who did not know this, shall now learn and support/follow it.

This [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) , as said in ‘*nejukku iruL kadi dhIpam* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ (~light that removes the darkness in our mind), incarnated to remove the darkness through his prabandham which is like *‘dheiva nan mAlai* \[periya thirumozhi 1.1.10\] (~ beautiful garland for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)). So, this day has come for us to celebrate with light (dheepam), and propitiation (ArAdhanA) (kArththikai dheepam)!

We should say as ‘*kurvANa: kArthikE mAsi vishNOr dhIpam hi mandhirE* \[vishNu dharmOththara purANam\]’ (light the lamps in [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) temples during the month of kArththikai), and ‘*vishNvAlayEshu kArththikyAm dhIpa dhAnam karOthiya:* \[vishNu dharmOththara purANam \]’ (In [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) temples, lamps are donated during the month of kArththikai).

Such day matches the glory of the phrase ‘*inRaip perumai’* (that is, matches the glory of the day due to [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)’s incarnation), as said in this pAsuram.

– – – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ९
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (pEdhai nenjE)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-8/)

**pAsuram – 9**

*mARan paNiththa thamizh maRaikku mangaiyarkOn*  
*ARangam kURa avadhariththa – veeRudaiya*  
*kArththikaiyil kArththikai nAL inRenRu kAdhalippAr*  
*vAyththa malarth thALgaL nenjE vAzhththu.* 9

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-09)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*mAran* – [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)  
*paNiththa* – divined (aruLich cheydha)  
*thamizh maRaikku* – dhrAvida vEdhas, that are the four prabandhams, thiruviruththam, periya thiruvanthAdhi, thiruvAsiriyam, and [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) ;  
(for these prabandhams),  
*mangaiyar kOn* – [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)  
*ARu angam* – (created) its six parts, that are the six prabandhams – periya thirumozhi, thirukkuRunthAndakam, thirunedunthANdakam, [thiruvezhukURRirukkai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/04/thiruvezhukurrirukkai/), siRiya thirumadal, and periya thirumadal;  
*kURa* – to divine them (aruLich cheyya)  
*avadhariththa* – [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) performed divine incarnation  
*veeRu udaiya* – in the great  
*kArththikaiyil* – month of kArththikai  
*kArththikai nAL* – in the star day of kruththikA;  
*kAdhalippAr* – (those who) would love and  
*inRu enRu* – say that (that star day) is this day (today),  
*nenjE* – Oh the mind!  
*vAzhththu* – you shall praise  
*vAyththa malar* – the compact/fit lotus flower like  
*thALgaL* – divine feet (of theirs).

**vyAkyAnam**

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining to his mind to praise the divine feet of those who always love the thirukkarththikai month, thirukkarththikai star day for it being the day [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) came here for divining six [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) which are the six parts of the four vEdhas.

***mARan paNiththa thamizh maRaikku* –** unlike the samskrutha vEdham that is following itself as self-existent, the greatness of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) is that it incarnated from nammAzhvAr.

Like saying ‘*vEdha:prAchEthasAdhAseeth* \[rAmAyaNam dhyAna slOkam – 16\]*’* (vEdham (rAmAyaNam) was created by vAlmIki), by saying ‘*thamizh maRai*’, it implies vEdham made in thamizh.

[bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/) too divined:

‘*thagam ha threen giri rUpAn vigyAthAniva dharsayAmchkAra \|*  
*thEshAgam hyEkaikasmAn mushtimAdhadhE sahOvAcha \|*  
*bhardhvAjEthryA manthrya \| vEdhA vA yEthE \|*  
*ananthA vai vEdhA – namO vAchE yAchOdhithA yAchAnudhithA thasyai*  
*vAchE namO vAchE – svam samskrutha dhrAvida vEdhasUkthai: –*  
*dhrAvideem brahma samhithAm* \[kAtakam\]

(~ bharathvAjar said to athri – these three vEdhas are of innumerable length. It cannot be said completely)

(in case of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/),) [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) makes [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) divine them, and thus [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) divined the prabandhams;

[![Nammazhwar-kanchi-2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Nammazhwar-kanchi-2.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Nammazhwar-kanchi-2.jpg)*mARan – at (dhEvap) perumAL kOil, kAncheepuram*

***mangaiyar kOn ARangam kURa avadhariththa –*** So, for these prabandhams of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) which are equivalent to four vEdhas**,** [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) incarnated to provide the six parts related to vEdhas, in the form of six prabandhams. For the prabandhams thiruviruththam etc., of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), the six prabandhams periya thirumozhi etc., of [thirumagai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) represent its six parts; these can be said as thamizh parts for the thamizh vEdham. This is very well established in AchArya hrudhayam.

[![thirumangai-azhwar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirumangai-azhwar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirumangai-azhwar.jpg)*thirumangai AzhvAr with kumudhavalli nAchchiyAr – (thiruvAli) thirunagari*

***vIRudaiya kArththikaiyil kArththikai nAL* –** In this way the incarnation of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) who knows the true meanings of vEdhas and its parts (angams) is the reason for kArththikai month’s kArththikai day being glorious compared to other non-special days. [He](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) is famously referred in the phrase ‘*parAnkusa parakAlA yathivarAdhigaL*’ (“[nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/), [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and other Azhvar AchAryas”).

[He](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) himself divined too – ‘*um adiyArOdu okka eNNi irundheer adiyEnai* \[periya thirumozhi 4.9.6\] (~ You thought of me to be same as your devotees); (you are thinking of me to be same as your innumerable other devotees; you are thinking of me to be same as seethA pirAtti who said she would wait for a month to see you, whereas here I am who cannot be separated from you even for a second, and you act like you don’t know the difference between me and your other devotees, dear indhaLUr swami!);

Matching this theme is [his](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) star birth day too { that is, there is a huge difference between this day and other days};

Moreover, *‘thAn ugandha UrellAm than thAL pAdi* \[thirunedunthAntakam – 6\]*’* (praising the divine feet of [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) in all the dhivya dhEsams where He is present out of his love) – this greatness of praising in all [dhivya dhEsams](https://koyil.org/) is applicable to this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) (as he went in person to so many dhivya dhEsams to do mangaLAsAsanam).

In this way, due to [his](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) glory, the importance also came to this day –

***kArththikaiyil kArththikai nAL inRu enRu kAdhalippAr* –** They (certain devotees) would think, among these insignificant days, there is this wonderful day that is available for us! For them this is also a ‘*madhi niRaindha nannAL* \[[thiruppAvai – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-01-margazhi-thingal/)\] (Oh what a day! We got this wonderful day to meet krishNan!)., and would always be thinking about its greatness, and will live with increasing love for it.

They are those like ‘*kuRaiyal pirAn adik keezh viLLAdha anban irAmAnusan* \[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 2\] ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is ever having the devotion toward the divine feet of [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)).

[![emperumAnAr-thirumangai AzhwAr](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/emperumAnAr-thirumangai-AzhwAr.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/emperumAnAr-thirumangai-AzhwAr.jpg)*thirumangai AzhvAr and one who loves kArthikai’s kArthikai – emperumAnAr*

Their divine feet is available to us –

***vAyththa malarth thALgaL nenjE vAzhththu –*** Oh mind! Since they (such devotees) are our lords, do mangaLAsAsanam that the existing devotion should continue forever, without straying – devotion towards their divine feet that is infinitely beautiful and is as per their svarUpam (nature) – is what you need to pray and praise, to keep to your nature (svarUpam) (of subservience).

That should be similar to what is said in ‘*pOndhadhu en nenju* \[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 100\] (~ the golden bee that is my mind, flew into the divine feet of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)).

It is to be said – ‘*inbuRum thoNdar sevvadi Eththi vAzhum en nenjamE* \[perumAL thirumozhi 2-4\]’ (~my mind would live praising the beautiful feet of the devotees).

**vAyththa** – what we got; well set

***malarth thALgaL –*** divine feet that are like flowers.

By this, our nature is to serve and do good to those who are subservient to AchAryan.

It was talked about with joy by noble and elderly srIvaishNavas, that he who is having the divine name of thiruk kali kanRi dhAsar, who is well-versed in the beautiful thamizh, and who preaches the meanings of all of the [four thousdand dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), that is lOkAcharyar, which is [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), and his divine lineage/family would celebrate with great love the divine incarnation day of [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/).

[![nampillai-goshti1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)*nampiLLai and disciples during his kAlakshEpam (discourse)*

[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) celebrates that day due to his love towards [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)’s divine feet; his lineage/family celebrates the day due to their love for [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) whose divine incarnation day is that same day too.

– – – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १०
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mARan paNiththa)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-9/)

**pAsuram 10**

*kArththigaiyil rOhiNi nAL kANmin inRu kAsiniyIr*  
*vAyththa pugazhp pANar vandhu udhippAl – AththiyargaL*  
*anbudanE thAn amalanAdhipirAn kaRRadhar pin*  
*nangudanE koNdAdum nAL* 10

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-10)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*pANar* –[thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)  
*vayththa* – having apt (porundhiya)  
*pugazh* – glory, (pugazh)  
*vandhu udhippAl* – because of [his](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) coming here and incarnating,  
*AththiyargaL* – those having Arththi (interest/love)  
*anbudanE* – would, with love  
*kaRRu* – learn and practice  
*amalanAdhipirAn* – the prabandham amalanAdhipirAn,  
*adhaRkup pin* – and after that  
*koNdAdum* – would celebrate  
*nangudanE* – well  
*nAL* – that the day is  
*inRu* – today;  
*kAsiniyIr* – Oh those on this earth!  
*kANmin* – notice that it is  
*kArththikaiyil* – the month of kArththikai  
*rOhiNi* – and star day of rOhiNi.

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, since after the star day of kArththikai it is rOhiNi, and since the month of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) is also of kArththikai, for that sequence, and since the day of rOhiNi in kArththikai month is when [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) incarnated, it is loved by those who accept the vEdhas (Asthika) and is celebrated, says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/).

***kArththikaiyil rOhiNi nAL kAnmin inRu kAsiniyeer*** – [He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) advised to his mind in the previous pAsuram, and in this again he is advising to the common man of the world (loukikar), with the wish in his mind that they (we) would be agreeable and go along with him.

***rOhiNi nAL* –** is the star day that krishNan incarnated. This [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) is having his mind attracted to that krishNan, “*kOvalanAi veNNai uNda vAyan en uLLam kavarndhAnai* \[amalanAdhipirAn – 10\]” (as a cowherd, ‘mouth person’ having the butter he ate; one who stole my heart..). So, [his](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) star day also became that itself.

Not only that, [thirukkOttiyUr nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/) from whom the meanings of charama slOkam started to spread, also incarnated in rOhiNi star day in the month of vaikAsi (v*aisAkha*). As is said of him ‘*uRiyil veNNaiyOdu iyaluNda oruvanaip pOl avadhariththAr*’ (incarnated like one who along with butter from the sling, ate the iyal (prabandham?) as well), so (since all three are related to krishNan), this is of muppuri (all three auspicious events happening in similar fashion).

When is this triple special day?

***inRu kANmin* –** it is today, see this, you all!

Not some other day, like said in ‘*ayam mAsa:*’ (ayOdhyA kANtam 3-4), it is today!

[He (maNavALa mAmunigaL)](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is having extreme love, that even though it (incarnation?) was in the past, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is saying it as present day. Like one would show huge stash of money, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is showing it as if it is in the front, saying**,** see this (day)!

***kAsiniyeer –*** showing it not for one or two persons, but like said in ‘*yadhi kaschin mumukshu: syAth*’ (if there is any mumukshu present..), due to his love, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is preaching to the whole country.

Would you not explain the reason for this day’s greatness?

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) replies: ***vAyththa pugazhp pANar vandhu udhippAl*** (due to incarnation of [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) who is having apt glory) – *vAyththa pugazh* is – glory that matches the svarUpam (nature); that is, having the humbleness that is required to match being naturally subservient, is present in him as part of [his](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) birth (in fifth varNam), and so ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) making srI lOka sAranga muni carry [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) by head as his vAhanam (vehicle/carrier), and accepted [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) – having such glory.

It is said – ‘*pAriyalum pugazh pAN perumAL* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-11/)\]’ (~ his glory and auspicious quality have spread in the world, such [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)).

***pANar vandhu udhippAl –*** Similar to what is said in ‘*Ethath sAma gAyan nAsthE* \[thaiththiriya upanishath – bruguvalli – 10) (he is reciting/singing sAma vEdham) which is the action of mukthas (those in parama padham), here [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) is doing the services with his pAN type songs to [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/); and doing that is his identity.

[![thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppANAzhvAr-uraiyUr-Nov-2015-Bharathwaj.jpg)*thiruppANAzhvAr at uRaiyUr during his yearly star day (thirunakshathram day)!*

***vandhu udhippAl* –** ([periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) is *‘aNdarkOn aNi arangan* \[amalanAdhipirAn – 10\]’ (~ king of the mukthas, and is here the beautiful [ranganAthan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), so for singing about Him, one of them from there has incarnated here, so it seems;

So it is said ‘***AththiyargaL koNdAdum nAL’*** (day that is celebrated by those who believe/accept the vEdhas etc.) – those people are – like lOka sAranga mahAmuni, they cherish [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who is in the archA form (statue) and whose truth can be understood (pramEya bhUthar), and cherish the best in pramANam (reference) amalanAdhipirAn which is in beautiful/pure thamizh which was created because of knowing Him, which is the prabandham of [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/), be well versed in it, and respect [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) who remembers his humble status , avoid what is seen in him just on the outside, but be with limitless love towards the [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/), be in this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)’s feet like said in ‘*pAttinAl kaNdu vAzhum pANar thAL paravinOmE* \[amalanAdihpirAn thaniyan\]’;

***anbudanE thAn amalanAdhipirAn kaRRadhar pin* –** As said about [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) in ‘*seeriya nAn maRaich chemporuL senthamizhAl aLiththa* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-11/)\]’, [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) gave the essence of the four vEdhas in virtuous thamizh, that is praNavam (Om) having three letters (a, u, ma) by placing those as first letter of the first three pAsurams *(**a**malanAdhipirAn, **u**vandha uLLaththanAi, **m**andhi pAi)*, and he sang about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who is talked about by that praNavam when standing under the vimAnam (roof of sanctum sanctorum) that stands for praNavam, and was immersed in Him singing about starting from His divine feet up to His divine head – thinking of all of these glories of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/), learn in proper way of letting AchAryan recite and repeat after him; after that –

**nangudanE koNdAdum nAL –** they would be trustful of such pramANams, be Asthikas, be motivated by its instructions, think about them as helpful for the well-being, and celebrate that day (of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)’s incarnation).

So [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) says (to us) – you too be Asthika, and trust my words, and establish these in your mind.

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – ११
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (kArththikaiyil rOgiNi nAL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-10/)

**pAsuram 11**

*manniya seer mArgazhiyil kEttai inRu mAnilaththeer*  
*en idhanukku ERRam enil uraikkEn – thunnu pugazh*  
*mAmaRaiyOn thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr piRappAl*  
*nAnmaRaiyOr koNdAdum nAL.* 11

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-11)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*mAnilaththeer –* Oh who are in this big world!  
*inRu* – this today  
*manniya* – is the well established  
*seer* – glorious  
*mArgazhiyil* – month of mArgazhi (mArgashIrsha)  
*kEttai* – and star of kEttai (jyEshta).  
*en ennil* – If you asked what  
*ERRam* – is the glory  
*idhanukku* – of this day,  
*uraikkiREn* (uraikkEn) – I shall tell that to you;  
It is,  
*thunnu* – fittingly  
*pugazh* – excellent,  
*mA* – and glorious,  
*maRaiyOn* – and most distinguished brAhmaNa,  
that is, *[thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)*’s,  
*piRappAl* – incarnation, and because of that  
*nAn maRaiyOr* – those who know the four vEdhas  
*koNdAdum* – celebrate  
*nAL* – this day.

**vyAkyAnam**

[srI thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)’s incarnation day that is mArgazhi (mArgashIrsha) month’s kEttai (jyEshta) star day, is the day celebrated by parama vaidhikas (those who are expert followers of vEdhas), so advises [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) to others.

***manniya seer, etc –*** Fullness of glory for the month of mArgazhi is – ‘*mAsAnAm mArgaseershOham* \[[bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 10.35\]’ (In the months, I am the mArgazhi), so it is a vaishNava month, ‘*mArgazhith thingaL madhi niRaindha nannAL* \[[thiruppAvai – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-01-margazhi-thingal/)\]’, that is having the greatness of [ANdAL](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-andal-anubhavam.html)’s incarnation in that month, also thiru adhyayana uthsavam starts during this month.

Moreover, through the prabandham of ‘*[thiruppaLLiyezhuchchi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppalliyezhuchchi/)*’, [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) wakes up [periya perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), so this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)’s incarnation is the greatness *for* this month.

Also, ***manniya seer* –** this month is like an adjective to his star day kEttai, like how that month is the best of months, this could be said as, the best of star days is kEttai.

Like said as ‘*viprANAm gyAnathOsrEshtam’* (best in knowledge, among the brAmhaNa), [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) who is having the glory of gyAnam (knowledge) being incarnated in this month/day is the glory for this month/day.

Since [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) is absolutely glorious as a thoNdaradippodi (~ devoted to His devotees), his incarnation day also would be glorious isn’t it? Like so the day that helps be among [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and his devotees is this wonderful day!

***mAnilaththIr* –** Since [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) whose identity is subservience to His devotees, due to his incarnation this earth is having such connection; Oh those who are in such earth!

***en idhanukku ERRam enil uraikkEn –*** If you asked, ‘When there are other star days in this month, what is the greatness of this star day?’, then listen to me explaining about that as I have known about its greatness.

***thunnu pugazh mAmaRaiyOn – etc. –*** That is, [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) is having the greatness of ‘*thuLapath thoNdAya thol seer* \[thirumAlai – 45\]’ (~ greatness/subservience of making thiruththuzhAi (thuLasi) garland (for [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/))), and ‘*kaRRinam mEyththa endhai kazhaliNaikkeezh – uRRa thirumAlai pAdum seer* \[thirumAlai thaniyan\]’ (~ being able to create/sing about/under divine feet of my father that is [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who herded the cows) – having immersed in such character due to doing these kainkaryams.

This [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) is ‘*mikka seerth thoNdar* \[periya thirumozhi 11.1.9\]*’* (~ a srIvaishNava, ananyaprayOjanar (not asking for anything else from [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/))*,* isn’t it?

Also he makes ‘*seyyum pasum thuLabath thozhil mAlai* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 13](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-13/)\]’ (makes garland of thiruththuzhAi that becomes bright by the touch of [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)’s hand), isn’t it?

This is how his ‘*aham sarvam karishyAmi’* is. \[ayOdhyA kAntam 31-25\]’ (iLaiya perumAL saying, ‘I will do every kainkaryam (in the forest)). It is this that is his rich glory. It is same as said in ‘*mali pugazh vAnavar* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.2.11\]’ (rich glory of nithyasUris).

***mAmaRaiyOn*** – Reason for all this is that he is distinguished among the brAhmaNas who are involved in finding the meanings of vEdhas. As said in ‘*vaidhikarE, meyppadiyAl un thiruvadich chUdum thagaimaiyinAr* \[thiruviruththam – 94\]’ (vaidhikAs are by true ways keep your divine feet in their head), since he is a great vaidhika and is having tenacity/devotion in kainkaryam. It is this that is his well established glory.

***mAmaRaiyOn, thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr –*** [He](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) got this name because the inner meaning of vEdhas, that is, being subservient to His devotees as said in ‘*mikka vEdhiyar vEdhaththin ut poruL* \[[kaNNinuNchiruththAmbu – 9](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiruth-thambu-9-mikka-vedhiyar/)\]’. This is the way in which he affectionately lives by.

‘*nambikku anbar thalai meedhu adippodi* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 153\]’ (dust of the feet of devotees on his head), is how the glory of [him](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) who does according to what the devotees wish him to do (*itta vazhakku).*

***AzhvAr piRappAl* –** It is his birth that is a (distinguished) birth; birth of rest are lowly only (due to karma?). Even though he thought of his birth as lowly when saying ‘*en seivAn thOnRinEnE* \[thirumAlai – 26\] ( (have not done anything good related to [emperuman](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) why have I born?), he is divining so since he has born as an [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/).

As said in ‘*srushtasthvam vana vAsAya* \[ayOdhyA kAntam – 40-5\]’ (You have born only to be living in the forest) {, this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) is born for serving other devotees only?}.

***nAnmaRaiyOr koNdAdum nAL* –** As he is being in this way, the vaidhikas similar to him who have understood the inner meanings of vEdham enthusiastically celebrate this day.

[![thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr - with emperumAnAr and maNavALa mAmunigaL](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thoNdaradippodi-AzhvAr-with-emperumAnAr-and-maNavALa-mAmunigaL-1024x684.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thoNdaradippodi-AzhvAr-with-emperumAnAr-and-maNavALa-mAmunigaL.jpeg)*thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr with those (emperumAnAr and mAmunigaL) who celebrate this day of his incarnation  *

***mAmaRaiyOr –*** They are understanding and celebrating, which is matching with their birth.

So,

***mAnilaththIr* –** Oh! the people of this world, you also understand the greatness of this day, nurture it, and reach the true goal (ujjIviyungOL), is the meaning.

Further to this, this mArgazhi’s kEttai is also having the superiority that it is the day of incarnation of he who loved periya kOyil (srIrangam) and [periya perumAL (srI ranganAthan)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and who is having the eminence/honour of being an AchAryan of the lOkaguru ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) – that is [periya nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/periya-nambi/).

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १२
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (manniya seer mArgazhiyil)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-11/)

**pAsuram – 12**

*thaiyil magam inRu thAraNiyIr ERRam indhath*  
*thaiyil magaththukkuch chARRuginREn – thuyya madhi*  
*peRRa mazhisaip pirAn piRandha nAL enRu*  
*naRRavargaL koNdAdum nAL* 12

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-12)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*thAraNiyIr* – Oh the residents of this earth!  
*inRu* – this today  
*thaiyil magam* – is thai month (pushya/paushal thaisya/pausa), magam star day (magha).  
*chARRuginREn* – I shall say  
*ERRam* – (about the) glory of
