*indhath thaiyil magaththukku* – this thai month, magam star day:  
*peRRa* – having  
*thuyya* – pure/virtuous  
*madhi* – knowledge, that is,  
*mazhisaip pirAn* – [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)  
*piRantha* – divined his incarnation  
*nAL enRu* – is this day –  
*nal thavargaL* – those having good asceticism / penances  
*koNdAdum* – would say this, and praise/celebrate  
*nAL* – the day.

**vyAkyAnam**

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining for the people of the earth to know about [thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s incarnation in the month of thai (pushya/paushal thaisya), in the star day of magam (makha).

***thaiyil magam inRu thAraNiyIr* –** Having the greatness as said in ‘*thai oru thingaLum* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi 1.1\]’, today is magam star day in pushya (thai) month.

Oh those in this world! As said in ‘*EkAm dharaNimAchrithau* \[yudhdha kAntam 5.10\]’ (we are in the same earth)’, you are having the fortune to be born in the world where thirumazhisaip pirAn incarnated.

***ERRam indhath thaiyil magaththukkuch chARRuginREn –*** What? Only **mAsi** (magha) magam (magha) is considered the grand star day; what is great about **thai** (pausa) magam (magha)? If you asked so, then listen to me as I explain its greatness for it to become popular in the whole world.

Saying that these are the greatness, by showing the following –

***thuyya madhi peRRa, etc*** – that is, having pure/virtuous knowledge by the grace of [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) got unblemished knowledge (*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* \[[thiruvAimozi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\]), [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) the head of the place [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/), incarnated on this day – is so celebrated by the ascetics.

***thuyya madhi –*** His knowledge (given by [emperumAn](http://emperumAn-pirAtti%20-%20https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) is enjoyed by himself too, as [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) says ‘*en madhikku viNNellAm uNdO vilai* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 51\]’ (is there any price for my knowledge?)

Purity of mind is – Not having the blemish of mind that considers other demi gods as superior/desired. This is said in ‘*mananaga malam aRak kazhuvi* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.3.8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/thiruvaimozhi-1-3-8-nalum-ninradu/)\]’.

[![thirumazhisai_azhwar_thirumazhisai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirumazhisai_azhwar_thirumazhisai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/thirumazhisai_azhwar_thirumazhisai.jpg)*thirimazhisai AzhvAr at thirumazhisai*

This is said very clearly by [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) in various of his pAsurams such as the following.

‘*thAdhulAvu konRai mAlai thunnu senchadaich chivan nIdhiyAl vaNangu pAdha* \[thiruchchanda viruththam – 9\]’ (One wearing konRai flowers, and having dense red hairlocks that is rudhran would properly prostrate – Oh you (emperumAn) having such divine feet!)

From ‘*pOdhil mangai bhUthalak kizhaththi dhEvi*’ to ‘*vEdha nUl OdhuginRadhu uNmai alladhu illai maRRu uraikkilE*’ \[thiruchchandha viruththam 72 to 88\], (~ srIdhEVi and bhUdhEvi are your consorts; the son from his lotus nAbhi is His son; one having half his body as the woman and having bull as his vehicle is emperumAn’s grandson; saying about this (parathvam) in any other way is falsity),

‘*uLLa nOygaL thIr marundhu vAnavarkku aLiththa em vaLLalArai anRi maRRor dheivam nAn madhippanE* \[thiruchchandha viruththam – 88\]
(Instead of the most generous emperumAn who gave nectar to the dhEvas to cure their problems, would I consider the other demi-gods as anything worthy?)

Starting with ‘*pAr migundha*’ – to – ‘*seer migundha ninnalAl Or dheivam nAn madhippanE* \[thiruchchandha viruththam – 89\]’, (Instead of you (emperumAn) who performed so many wonders to get pANdavas win over the dhuryOdhanA’s group, would I go to any demi-gods?)

Starting from ‘*nAnmuganai nArAyaNan padaiththAn nAnmuganum thAn mugamAi sankaranaith thAn padaiththAn*’ – to – ‘*pidhiru manamilEn pingyakan thannOdu edhirvan avan enakku nErAn*’ \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi 1 to 84\], (nArAyaNan created brahmA, and he in turn created Sankara (shows that emperumAn is the god who is the root of all creations), (I do not have the mind that sickens by going into worldly matters; even though I may be equal in knowledge to paramaSivan, he would not equal me as I am forever a servant of emperumAn)

‘*kallAdhavar ilangai kattazhiththa kAkuththan allAl oru dheivam yAnilEn* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 53\], (He who destroyed lankApuri that was inhabited by the ignorant/bad rAkshasas, that is srI rAman – I would not consider any one other than Him as a god)

‘*ini aRindhEn eesarkkum nAnmugarkkum dheivam ini aRindhEn emperumAn unnai* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 96\], (I have understood very clearly now (*ini aRindhEn ini aRindhEn*), that you are the god of brahmA and rudhran)

and so in all his prabandhams, in the start, middle/in-between, and in the end (which signifies that it is important), without any hesitation, like [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) is referred to as ‘*uRaiyil idAdhavar*’ (not putting the sword back in its holder, that is, [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) does not mince his words), he has clearly divined to us what is important and what is not, isn’t it?

***mazhisaip pirAn piRandha nAL enRu –*** in this way [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) is having divine knowledge; such is his birth – two births in one (after getting the true knowledge is the new birth).

**nAl thavargaL koNdAdum nAL –** Since this AzhAr is son of a rishi, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is saying ‘day that good sages/ascetics celebrate’, as [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s birth day.

Birth of others is like ‘*anRu nAn piRandhilEn* \[thiruchchandha viruththam – 64\]’ (that physical birth of me was not the real birth (since did not gain true knowledge)).

‘*piRandha pin maRandhilEn* \[thiruchchandha viruththam – 64\]’ is how this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s divine birth is which is when getting true knowledge of our relationship with [emperumAn](http://emperumAn-pirAtti%20-%20https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – after that have not forgetten about it)

***piRandha nAL enRu –*** That day is such that it would be celebrated with prapaththi (surrender) by those who have gained the true knowledge.

(thavam -\> surrendering to [emperumAn](http://emperumAn-pirAtti%20-%20https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/); nal thavam (good thavam) -\> subservient to his devotees.)

thavam -\> prapaththi. It is to be said, *‘thasmAn nyAsam EshAm thapasAm athirikthamahu:* \[thaiththiriyOpanishath nArAyaNa valli 24-50\]’ (so this saraNAgathy is said to be above the other means like sathyam, etc.) , and ‘*sArvE thava neRi* \[thiruvAimozhi 10.4\]’ ().

So surrendering and ‘*vErAga Eththi* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 18\]’ (praising/being immersed in [emperumAn](http://emperumAn-pirAtti%20-%20https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s exclusive aspects), is how this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s ‘thapas’, that is prapaththi is.

*nal thavam* (nal thavargaL) -\> AcharyAbhimAna nishtA (being most dear to AchAryan); it is to be said ‘*maRRavaraich chArththi (chARRi) iruppAr thavam* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 18\] (ways of srIvaishNavas who are subservient to other srIvaishNavas (would win the ways of those immersed in praising [emperumAn](http://emperumAn-pirAtti%20-%20https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))).

Having such ‘*nal thavam*’ are – [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s disciples like kaNikaNNar, and perumpuliyUr adigaL.

By this it is concluded that for those having attachment in AchAryAbhimAnam, this day is to be specially nurtured.

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १३
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (thaiyil magam inRu)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-12/)

**pAsuram 13**

*mAsip punarpUsam kANmin inRu maNNulagIr*  
*thEsu iththivasaththukku Edhennil – pEuginREn*  
*kolli nagark kOn kulasEkaran piRappAl*  
*nallavargaL koNdAdum nAL* 13

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-13)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*maNNulagIr –* Oh residents of this earth!  
kANmin – Realize that  
inRu – today  
mAsi – is the month of mAsi (magha)  
punarpUsam – and star day of punarpUsam (punarvasu);  
(E) edhu ennil – if asked what is the  
thEsu – grand value  
ith thivasaththukku – of this day,  
pEsuginRen – I shall tell you about that; that is,  
kolli nagark kOn – he who is the head of the place kolli,  
kulasEkaran – that is, [kulasEkara AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/),  
pirappAL – due to his incarnation  
nAL – on this day,  
nallavargaL – noble people  
koNdAdum – celebrate (it).

**vyAkyAnam**

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining the enrichment of knowledge of the ignorant ones, about the greatness of [srI kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) who divined his incarnation during mAsi (magha) punarpUsam (punarvasu).

***mAsip punarpUsam kANmin inRu maNNulagIr*** – As said in ‘*mAsi munnAL* (nAchchiyAr thirumozhi – 1.1), it can be considered as having greatness that is not present in any other day – that is mAsi (magha) month’s star day of punarpUsam (punarvasu), Oh see that those in this world – that day is today for you all!

***inRu*** – The one that occurred in the past and will in the future is appearing as today for him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) due to his regard/fondness.

***mAsip punarpUsam –*** It was in chiththirai month punarvasu star day that chakravarththy thirumagan (srI rAman) divined His incarnation. *‘ellai il seerth dhayarathan than maganAith thOnRiRRu adhu mudhalAth than ulagam pukkathIRA* \[perumAL thirumozhi 10.10\]*’ –* (From His incarnation as a son of dhasarathan of limitless fame, till the time when He returned to paramapadham, that is, [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) gave us the summary of srI rAmAyaNam), is how this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) lets us know about rAman’s glory; and his star day also has become the same.

Like how those born in the lineage of kings should have a grand star day, this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s incarnation is having such connection with [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/).

[![kulasekarazhwar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/kulasekarazhwar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/kulasekarazhwar.jpg)*srI kulasEkarap perumAL*

***maN ulagIr*** – Oh the ones in this earth who are involved in the enjoyments of this world, and not paying attention to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and his devotees! Avoid your distractions and listen to the meanings I am talking about. Those in the other world are best in their true knowledge. Having less knowledge and as said in ‘*uNdiyE udaiyE ugandhu* \[perumAL thirumozhi 3-4\] going eagerly after food only, clothes only (and other comforts only) and being ‘*mAranAr varivenchilaikku At cheydhu* \[perumAl thirumozhi 3-3\]*’* (Surrendering to the beautiful bad arrow of manmatha and enjoying this material world), — for such people as you only is it required for me to advise.

{notice how the vyAkyAthA ([piLLailOkam jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/08/pillai-lokam-jiyar/)) is using the respective AzhvAr’s prabandham itself to show the meanings of [upadhEsa raththina mAlai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)}

If you asked, ‘For your highness to advise us regarding this, what is great about this day?’, then –

***pEsuginREn* etc. –** As [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) said about himself in ‘kolli kAvalan kUdal nAyakan kOzhik kOn kulasEkaran \[perumAL thirumozhi 2.10\] (king of the place of kolli, of madhurai, and uRaiyUr, that is [kulasEkaran](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)), such chEra king, is [kulasEkara AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/); the day got its significance due to his incarnation, and due to that (we) are able to get relation of the good; [kulasEkaran](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s birth is not of body but of life/[AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/) – he said ‘*UnERu selvaththu udal piRavi yAn vENdEn* \[perumAL thirumozhi 4-1\] (I who has realized the good from the bad, would not want the birth in the body that grows rich in meat everyday, etc.).

The king [kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) wished to be an animal or a plant living in thirumalai (thiruppathi)

– are how his his likes and dislikes are set.

Being amicable to be subservient (to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and his devotees) – that is a birth; this is as said in ‘*Azhi am kaip pEr Ayarkku ALAm piRappu* \[periya thiruvanthAdhi – 79\]’, and having ‘(un) *viNNAttuth thEsu’* (regardless of the kind of birth in this world, if one has the devotion toward [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), then such birth would be having the greatness/luster of your other \[higher\] world).

In this way, due to this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s incarnation that is amicable to subservience, this day gets its luster.

So this day is –

***nallavargaL koNdAdum nAL –*** (celebrated by noble ones); they are ‘*kolli kAvalan sol padhikkum kalaik kavi pAdum periyavar* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 14](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-14/)\]’ (the noble ones who recite the pAsurams of [kulasEkara Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) as an outlet of their love for him);

*nallavargaL* – they take care of others’ spiritual wellness like of their own.

*nAL* – a day is one that is celebrated by such people.

This [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/), as said in ‘*ellaiyil adimaith thiRaththinil enRu mEvu manaththanAm* \[perumAL thirumozhi 2.10\]’ (([kulasEkara AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)) having the mind of being at most subservient, (to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)’s devotees’ devotees’ …)), is of such goodness, and due to that, for them he had put his hand inside the pot of snake (to prove those devotees’ innocence when they were blamed for a lost jewel in [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s palace) – having such greatness of character;

This day is nurtured and celebrated by those srIvaishNavas who have lost themselves to such quality of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) and are good to his lotus feet.

Now,

[srI kulasEkara AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) wanted to be some animal or plant or, ANYthing in the hills of thirumalai (thiruppathi), as he said in :

‘*inbamarum selvamum ivvarasum yAn vENdEN* \[perumAL thirumozhi 4.1\] (I do not want the wealth that would go into enjoying various things, and I do not want this kingdom that enables them),

and in –

‘*uruppasi than am poR kalai algul peRRAlum AdhariyEn* \[perumAL thirumozhi 4.3\] (Would not want it even if I got the beautiful decorated parts of UrvaSi (consort of indhra who is the king of dhEvas)),

– Thus this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) wishes to be something, anything in the hills of thirumalai and with such wishes he serves [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/).

Similarly,

[srI gOvindhap perumAL (embAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) too is described in the same way, as said in ‘*thruNIkrutha virinjchAthi nirankusa vibhUthaya:* \[varavaramuni mukthakam – 7\]’ (gives no importance to those like brahmA, and is having the greatness in the worlds), ignores all lowly affairs,

and as said in ‘*hrudhi nArAyaNam pasyan nAbhyagachchathrahassadhA yassarvadhArathEchchApi gOvindham tham upAsmahE* \[[embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) thaniyan, guruparamparA prabhAvam – 528\]’ ([He](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) who is always seeing [nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), and was not able to see any place as private for happiness with his wife, we worship such [gOvindhar (embAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/)), and so for other enjoyments [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) is of the view that there is no dark and private place (since he sees [nArAyaNAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)’s brightness everywhere),

so, for this [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) also the punarpUsam (punarvasu) has become the star day of his incarnation.

[![embar_madhuramangalam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/embar_madhuramangalam.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/embar_madhuramangalam.jpg)*embAr – [madhuramangalam](http://madhuramangalam.koyil.org)*

As said in ‘*arasamarndhAn adi sUdum* \[perumAL thirumozhi 10.7\]*’* (falling at the feet of [srI rAma pirAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is seated with majesty in his throne), like this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) who seeks the feet of [srI rAman](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/), [embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) too is like a shadow of [rAmAnujar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine feet.

In the case of distaste for other demi gods, he ([embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/)) matches [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/).

[embAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/07/embar/) too is of two births in one (brAhmaNa).

Due to all of these reasons, this pAsuram says about the greatness of this star day being of *muppuri* (three auspicious things happening in a similar way).

– – – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १४
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mAsip punarpUsam kANmin)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-13/)

**pAsuram 14**

*ERAr vaikAsi visAkaththin ERRaththaip*  
*pArOr aRiyap pagarkinREn – seerArum*  
*vEdham thamizh seydha meyyan ezhil kurugai*  
*nAthan avadhariththa nAL* 14

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-14)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*Ar* – filled with  
*Er* – beauty  
*vaikAsi* – (is the) month of vaikAsi  
*visAkaththin* – star day of visAkam;  
*pArOr* – (For) those in the earth  
*aRiya* – to know  
*ERRaththai* – its glory,  
*pagarginREn* – I shall say (about it; that is),  
*Arum* – filled with  
*seer* – glory  
*vEdham – that is vEdhas*  
*seydha* – is divined  
*thamizh* – in thamizh language  
*meyyan* – (by the one who is) truthful  
*ezhil* – (who is the) beautiful  
*kurugai* – [thirukkurugUr](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/)’s  
*nAthan* – master, that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/);  
*avadhariththa* – (it is his) divine incarnation  
*nAL* – day.

**vyAkyAnam**

He who is having other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) as his parts, who divined the popularity of meanings of vEdhAnthams through [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), who is the head of [(AzhvAr) thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/), that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) – for everyone in the earth to know this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s incarnation day of visAka star, I shall divine about it in an exclusive way, says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/).

***ErAr* etc. –** In the pAsurams till now he had divined about the months in the calendar order, now since there is no incarnation of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) in the month of panguni, and even though in the month after that which is chiththirai there are incarnations of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), since he is currently listing the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ incarnation details, he has skipped them and is starting here with ‘*ErAr vaikAsi’*.

vaikAsi having beauty is about – Since it is mAdhava month (spring) it is having the period of blossoming flowers. The place of incarnation is rich in ‘*koththalar pozhil* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.7.1\] (groves full of flowers in bunches), and in ‘*kuyil ninRAr pozhil* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 10](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiruth-thambu-11-anban-thannai/)\] (cuckoos joyfully singing near the groves), so it is said as ‘*ErAr vaikAsi visAkam’*.

*‘ErAr*’ (full of beauty) is also an adjective for visAkam. Then it is to be decorated as ‘*thiru visAgath thirunAL*’ (auspicious day of visAkam). In all the [dhivya dhEsams](https://koyil.org/index.php/dhivya-dhesams/) it is celebrated with consuming milk and fruits. That is, ‘*pAl mAngAi*’.

About such day’s greatness –

***pArOr aRiyap pagarginREn –*** (saying for everyone in the world to know) – I shall talk about the glory of vaikAsi visAkam that is [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s incarnation day, for everyone around. His ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s) love is making [him](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) talk to ensure that there is no one who would not love about this (day).

Now it talks about the reason for all these –

***seerArum, etc* –** Greatness for vEdham are – not created by anyone {so no bias, etc.}, always existing {eternal – available at all times}, and faultless {so can be followed} – and so it having the wealth of being the ultimate reference/authority. [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) too said ‘*sudar migu suruthiyuL* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.7](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/04/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-7-thidavisumbu-erivali/)\]’ (abundantly radiant vEdham (being self-evident/reference)). It is also about the second part of vEdham which talk about nature, form, and qualities of [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) referred as para brahmam who is the [husband of lakshmI](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). It is to be said, ‘*yaSruthEruththaram bhAgam chakrE thrAvida bhAshAyA* \[parAnkusa ashtakam – 7\]’ (he ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) who created in thamizh the second part of vEdham that is upanishath).

***vEdam thamizh seidha –*** Creating it in thamizh is – as said in ‘*eidharkku ariya maRaigaLai Ayiram in thamizhAl seidharkku ulagil varum satakOpanai* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 18\]*’* ([satakOpan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who incarnated and created in sweet thamizh one thousand pAsurams that represent the hard vEdhas), vEdhas have limitations for learning, it is not possible for all sentient ones to learn and reach the true goal.

[nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) provided its meanings in detail in sweet thamizh for everyone to be able learn and use it and reach the true goal. It is to be said ‘*vERu onRum nAn aRiyEn vEdham thamizh seidha mARan satakOpan* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-thaniyans/)\], and ‘*arumaRaigaL anthAdhi seydhAn* \[[thiruvAimozhi thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-thaniyans-invocation/)\], to say the same.

***meyyan*** – All that was divined are based on vEdham so we have the faith in it.

***ezhil kurugai nAthan –*** As saying ‘*kurugUrch chatakOpan’*, ([satakOpan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) of kurugUr), for all these the reason is being born in that place (kurugUr that is AzhvAr thirunagari). Even though there is one [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) named ‘*Adhip pirAn’* there, everything happens there under the mastership of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) only. Even though he is the paran and [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) is the jIvan, it is [Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s leadership that He is establishing there. As said in ‘*nalan idai Urdhi paNNi vIdum peRuththith than mUvulagum tharun oru nAyagam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.10.11\]*’* ((benefit of learning this padhikam would be that He would) make one be involved in subservience to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and His devotees, will give mOksham, and make one like a head of all His three worlds) {such is [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), that he makes this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) as the head}.

[![nammazhvar_painting](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/nammazhvar_painting.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/nammazhvar_painting.png)

***ezhil kurugai –*** (beautiful kurugai ([AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/))) – Having the decorations of a city. That is, like ‘*kunRam pol maNi mAdam* ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.10.1) (having buildings tall like a collection of mountains), ‘*mAdalar pozhil* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.4.11\]’ (dotted by blossoming groves), ‘*sErth thada* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 1.2.11\]’ (having dense set of ponds), and ‘*Er vaLam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.1.11\] (having fertile/abundant paddy etc., fields)’. It is also said as ‘*kattezhil then kurugUr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.6.11\]*’* (kurugUr having the beauty of protective walls).

As said in ‘*jagathAbharanam vakuLAbharanar*’, [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) is like a jewel for the world, and the beauty to this place can also be due to his incarnation there.

Or,

***ezhil*** – (beauty) – is like a adjective to [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), and can also be about the beauty that came due to his srIvaishNava decorations – gyAna, bhakthi, vairAgyam.

***ezhil kurugai nAthan avadhariththa nAL*** – As said in ‘*Urum nAdum ulagamum thannaip pOl* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.7.2\]’ (he ([AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) can make the place, country, and the world to always babble [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s name and other things), such [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) ‘s day of incarnation.

[AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who can show the way for the people in the samsAram (material world) to attain true goal, incarnated; similarly this great day among all the different days has come for us.

So due to his extreme kindness, [maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) has revealed this precious secret for us.

– – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १५
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (ErAr vaikAsi)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-14/)

**pAsuram – 15**

*uNdO vaikAsi visAkaththukku oppu oru nAL*  
*uNdO satakOparkku oppu oruvar – uNdO*  
*thiruvAimozhikku oppu then kurugaikku uNdO*  
*oru pAr thanil okkum Ur*
15

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-15)

**Word by word meaning**

*vaikAsi visAkaththukku* – For the visAka star day of vaikAsi month  
*uNdO* – is there  
*oru nAL* – any day that is  
*oppu* – equal;  
*satakOparkku* – for [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)  
*uNdO* – is there  
*oruvar* – any one who is  
*oppu* – equal;  
*thiruvAimozhikku* – for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) prabandham  
*uNdO* – is there a prabandham  
*pAr thanil* – in the earth that is  
*oppu* – equal;  
*then kurugaikku* – for [AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/) that is on the south  
*uNdO* – is there  
*oru Ur* – any place that is  
*okkum* – equal;

No is the answer.

**vyAkyAnam**

He is involving in the abundant experience of talking to himself about the place, time, and the [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) divined by the [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) whom he mentioned in [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-14/).

***uNdo vaikAsi visAkaththukku oppu oru nAL –*** Is there any day that can equal this divine vaikAsi day that is born to do mangaLAsAsanam, for [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) and all his abodes to grow well? The day of birth of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) as said in ‘*nee pirandha thiru nannAL* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 23.8\]*’* (the auspicious good day You were born) – can even that equal the day of incarnation of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who is said as ‘*krushNa thrushNA thathvam* \[srI rangarAja sthavam, pUrva sathakam – 6\] ([AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) could be said to be in the form of love for krishNan)?

There, in krishNan’s birth, only some people here and there like akrUrar, mAlAkArar, kUni, chinthayanthI, or a few such only were reformed to be amicable. Here [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)‘s birth is such that, as [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) said starting with ‘*thAnaham dhvishatha: krUrAn*’ to ‘*kshipAmi’* \[[bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) 16-19\] (~ I punish those who disrespect my devotees by pushing them into asura births), even those whom [He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) would reject, it is the day of incarnation of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who would create interest in such people toward [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) such that they too cannot bear the separation from Him – as [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) said in ‘*nin kaN vEtkai ezhuvippanE* \[thiruviruththam – 16\]’ (~will motivate to be thirsty for You). { that is the greatness here compared to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)‘s incarnation}.

***uNdO satakOparkku oppu oruvar*** – Starting from his incarnation, he was a remover of bad/ignorant minds of such people; having true depth of knowledge – such is the glory of knowledge of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/); even if inquired in all the worlds do we hear anyone equaling him?

What with food, water, etc., what with ripe fruits, etc., what with ‘*appAl mudhalAi ninRa aLappariya Aramudhu* \[thirunedunthANtakam – 14\]’ {here it may mean food that is like nectar} – the samsAris are involved in sustaining, growing, and enjoying with these things; starting from such kind of people, can they ever be compared to this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who is of the type ‘*nAttArOdu iyal(vu) ozhindhu nAraNanai naNNi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.2\]’ (~ connections with the people of the (material) place got removed, and got [nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)), and ‘*ellAm kaNNan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.6.1\]’ (~ food, water, everything is krishNan for me), and such [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) cannot be equaled by even the nithyasUris.

[![Nammazhwar-2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Nammazhwar-2.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Nammazhwar-2.jpg)

‘nainAr’ (as referred by the commentator) ([azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nAyanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/)) divined too – other than nithyasUris (that is, like rishis) “*pala sAdhana dhEvathAntharangaLil ivargaL ninaivu pEchchilE thOnRumpadi irukkum* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 62\]” (compared to maharishis whose speeches would indicate that the goal is to reach [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), or that karma/gyAna/bhakthi are the means, or that it is acceptable to pray to the demi-gods, [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s speech is that bhagavath kainkaryam is the goal, that [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) is the means, and that even forgetfully we should not pray to demi-gods; so they cannot be compared to [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)).

Or, for nithyasUris, that place is like ‘*theLi visumbu thirunAdu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.7.5\] (~ radiant, in knowledge) such that it is amicable for them to enjoy [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) all the time. Here, this place is like ‘*viNNuLAr perumARkkadimai seyvAraiyum seRum aym pulan ivai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 7.1.6\]’ (~ the five senses would trouble even those who are subservient to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)). Such ‘*iruL tharumA gyAlam* \[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 72\] (this world that feeds ignorance), would not make it easy to enjoy [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/).

In such a birth, there is only [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who spends time only in enjoying [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). Isn’t that why it is ‘*sudhurlabha*:’ ([bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/)) {*Or oruvar uNdAgil aththanai kAN* – upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 55}.

– As said in “*mARuLadhO immaNNin misai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.4.9\]” (Is there anyone matching me in this world?), and

– “*iniyAvar nigar agal vAnaththE* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.5.8\]” (who would equal me even in that other big world (~when I have been given opportunity to sing [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) on [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))).

So [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) himself divined by his words that there is no equal in both this world and the other world, isn’t it?

When asked: So in this way, if we say [satakOpan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), he is meant as above everyone, this mahAthmA incarnated and is worshiped by the whole world, and if there is no equal to him or to his grand star day**,**

then is there anything equal to his words that is [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and for the place of his incarnation?

Even that is also not there, says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), as:

*uNdO thiruvAimozhikku oppu then kurugaikku uNdO oru pAr thannil okkum Ur.*

*uNdO thiruvAimozhikku oppu –* [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who is ‘*thirumAlAl aruLap peRRa* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.8.11)’ (given unblemished knowledge (*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* ([thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/))) by [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), and ‘*thirumAlavan kavi* \[thiruviruththam – 48\]’ – his experience of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) did not contain itself like said in ‘*suzhi pattOdum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.10.5\] (like a flood with a vortex), like said in ‘*avAvil anthAdhigaLAl ivai Ayiramum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.10.11\]’ (the thousand pAsurams in anthAdhi style, that came out of devotion) the [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) got caught in [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s bhakthi and it incarnated.

Can the words that came out of dharma, strength, knowledge, happiness, etc., match the words of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) that is out of devotion and is essence of [nAlAyira dhivya prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)?

Other words are like the sound of sea waves (no meaning/use). So, as said in ‘*aruL koNdu Ayiram in thamizh pAdinAn* \[[kaNNinuNchiruththAmbu –
8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiru-thambu-8-arul-kondadum/)\] (~ he sang one thousand sweet pAsurams in beautiful thamizh due to his mercy), this [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) that incarnated due to his kindness/mercy would not be having any equals.

***then kurugaikku uNdO oru pAr thanil okkum Ur*** – Like how there is none equal to [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) in this world or the other world, this place (of his incarnation) also does not have any place that equals it.

*Tree in AzhvAr thirunagarI (kurugai) where nammAzhvAr stayed*

Even if searched in eighteen worlds, is there any place that equals kurugai vaLampathi? Even if it is there (srIvaikuNtam), it is more like saying together ‘*thirunAdu vAzhi then kurugai vAzhi* \[iyal sARRu\]’ (long live srIvaikuNtam long live then kurugai). Shall have to say ‘*thirunagarikku oppAriyuNdO’.*

It is too divined as ‘*ARRil thuRaiyil Uril uLLa vaishamyam vAchAmagOcharam* \[AchArya hrudhayam 80\]’ (~ can’t be said in words the difference between this place and the others).

***then kurugai*** – This place is a jewel for the (difficult?) samsAram, as said in ‘*nallAr palar vAzhum* *kurugUr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.2.11\]’, and as ‘*sayap pugazhAr palar vAzhum thadam kurugUr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.1.11\]’ – such is the grand [kurugUr](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/) that is [srI nagarI (AzhvAr thirunagarI)](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/) (wealthy city), isn’t it?

Also, it is meant as this place is in the southern direction.

Thus [maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divined about this divine star day, about [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) who incarnated, about [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), and [thirunagarI](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/), after considering their unequaled greatness.

This visAka star day is of significance in ikshvAku dynasty as said by noble people, and this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) also got the same star day of incarnation and greatness as said in ‘*rushImjushAmahE* \[parAnkusa ashtakam – 3\] (we prostrate before satakOpa muni).

– – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १६
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (uNdO vaikAsi)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-15/)

**pAsuram 16**

*inRaip perumai aRindhilaiyO Ezhai nenjE*  
*inRaikku en ERRam enil uraikkEn – nanRi punai*  
*pallANdu pAdiya nam pattar pirAn vandhu udhiththa*  
*nal Anilyil sOdhi nAL*
16

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-16)

**Word by word meaning**

*Ezhai* – (Oh) the ignorant  
*nenjE* – mind!  
*aRindhilaiyO* – Do you not know  
*inRai* – today’s  
*perumai* – greatness;  
*enil* – If you are asking  
*ERRam en* – what is the greatness  
*inRaikku* – of today,  
*uraikkEn* – I shall tell you;  
*nal* – (It is) the good  
*Aniyil* – Ani month (vaiSAka)  
*sOdhi nAL* – svAthi star day (in which)  
*nam* – our  
*pattar pirAn* – [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)  
*vandhu udhiththa* – incarnated,  
*pAdiya* – (and who) divined the song of  
*pallANdu* – [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) (prabandham)  
*punai* – that is having / made of  
*nanRi* – goodness.

**vyAkyAnam**

Furthermore, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining to his mind about the greatness of Ani month (vaiSAka) svAthi star day in which [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) incarnated, divined [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) through which to revive the world, and having the greatness of referred to as ‘*AzhvArgaL ellAraiyum pOl allar periyAzhvAr* (srI vachana bhUshaNam – 251) ([periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) is not like any [other AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (in the sense that [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) sang [pallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) (long live) to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), compared to other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who were usually pleading [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) to take them to SrI vaikuNtam; and more));

And so [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) wishes to divine in a big way using five pAsurams about this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s greatness.

***inRaip perumai aRindhilaiyO Ezhai nenjE –***

**Oh my mind you who without knowing the difference between the star days mentioned earlier and this star day, and who is fond of those other star days!**

If comparing him to them it is ‘*parvatha paramANuvOttai vAsi* \[[thiruppallANdu vyAkyAna avathArikai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)?\]’ (Difference between a mountain and a small atom/particle), then should you not be knowing that such difference is there in his star day also? Reason for ignorance is your poverty (of knowledge);

If so, if you asked what is the excellence of today, then hear what I say as I know its excellence very well.

***nanRi punai etc. –*** That is, alas, the subject who is always wished well by the ever active nithyasUris who fear for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s safety (even) in the place where time is immaterial (SrI vaikuNtam), has divined his appearance here with his soft beautiful auspicious divine body (dhivya mangaLa thirumEni), as target of the eyes, in this place where kali (yuga) is ruling and where there are offending enemies – so becoming very sad, [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) took the bells from the elephant’s back (as he was sitting on it as arranged by the king for proving the superiority of [SrIman nArAyaNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) as the one and only one to go to, to escape from this material world), and setting the tune he sang [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) to add glory to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) – such [bhatta nAthar](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) (head of the learned) who is our head incarnated such that the Ani (vaiSAka) month’s svAthi star gained the greatness that is not present for any other (star days).

So, learn the greatness of this day which is wonderful in every which way, and become fond of it.

***nanRi punai* –** (nanRi -\> goodness) (punai -\> put/tie together); Goodness put together in his [pallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/). Goodness put together on [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) by his [pallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/). It is to be said, ‘*thAn mangaLam AdhalAl* \[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 19\] (auspicious ([thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)))**,** and ‘*pallANdu enRu kAppu idum* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 15](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-15/)\] (([periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who puts together protection (mangaLASAsanam) to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) through [pallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)).

***pattar pirAn*** – (head of the learned) – by this it has talked about the way he established the supremacy of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and destroyed placement of that in others.

[![pallandu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/pallandu-1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/pallandu-1.jpg)

***pallANdu pAdiya –*** by this it has talked about the way of his care for the divine beautiful body of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/).

By this, it is clear that [Isvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)’s (one who controls) svarUpam (nature) etc., are under the control of this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १७
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (inRaip perumai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-16)

**pAsuram 17**

*mAnilaththil mun nam periyAzhvAr vandhu udhiththa*  
*Ani thannil sOthi enRAl Adharikkum – gyAniyar(u)kku*  
*opporuvar (oppOr) illai ivvulagu thanil enRu nenjE*  
*eppozhudhum (eppOdhum) sindhiththu iru.*
17

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-17)

**Word by word meaning**

*mAnilaththil* – In the big earth  
*mun* – earlier,  
***nam* – our**  
[*periyAzhvAr*](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)  
*vandhu udhiththa* – came and incarnated  
*Ani thannil* – in the month of Ani  
*sOthi* – and star day of svAthi;  
*enRal* – regarding this,  
*gyAniyarkku* – the learned ones  
*Adharikkum* – would be very fond of it; and  
*ivvulagu thannil* – in this world  
*oruvar illai enRu* – there is no one  
*oppu* – equal (to such learned ones);  
*nenjE* – Oh the mind!  
*eppozhudum* – at any time  
*iru* – be  
*sindhiththu* – reflecting upon (their greatness) (*mananam*).

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, through the unparalleled greatness of the learned ones who are fond of it when talking about this day, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining the greatness of this day.

***mAnilaththil munnam periyAzhvAr vandhu udhiththa –*** His incarnation in this big world, as being the cause of our true being (*saththai*, etc); his incarnation was being equal to the one who incarnates ([emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)).

[![srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)*periyAzhvAr*

*nam periyAzhvAr* and *nam pattar pirAn,* is the way of desire of his ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s) mind.

*vandhu udhiththa –* His incarnation such that not only his true being, but our true being also he made happen by the way of managaLASAsanam through his singing of [pallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/); and making his yAthrai as our yAthrai as well, is his ways;

***Ani thannil sOthi enRAl Adharikkum*** – It is the reason of this *mangaLASAsanparar* (one who wishes well for [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) that we nurture this day. Among other star days, when considering this jyEshta month svAthi star day due to the incarnation of this superior one, the learned ones pile on to celebrate it – there is no equal to them.

***Adharikkum gyAniyarkku** –* Would the uninterested ignorant ones who do not celebrate this be equal to these learned ones? The use of knowledge is to know it and celebrate it – isn’t it?

***oppu oruvarillai ivvulagu thanil –*** Even if searched in this big world, there is no one equal to the eminent ones who understand the difference of the *mangaLASAsanaparar*. If present it is only in that world (SrI vaikuNtam); there they are of nature fit for their divine knowledge; so they are the ones who celebrate those who understand the difference of the *mangaLASasanaparar.* Since this is so, there is no one equal to these (aforementioned) learned ones here.

***enRu nenjE eppozhudhum sindhiththu iru*** – Oh my mind who knows the greatness of the bhAgavathas (devotees)! Always reflect upon what I have said, considering this as something (of importance). Do not hallucinate that you would get that which would not be gotten (the equals of such learned ones?). By this it is established that – like how there is no equal to this [Azhvar](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html), there is no equal to these learned ones as well.

Like this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html), who in the matter of ‘*gyAnach chudar* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi – 2.8.5\]’ (([emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) having the light of knowledge (manifested by itself / that is not easy to understand by any knowledgeable ones fully)), had bathed (*neerAttal* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi – 2-4\], decorated with flowers (*pUchchUttal* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 2-7\]), and applied protections (*kAppidal* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 2-8\]);

In the same way, [periya thirumalai nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/01/periya-thirumalai-nambi/) too was serving the [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) at thirumalai, as said in ‘*sumandhu mAmalar neer sudar thUpam koNdu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.3.7\] ((worship [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) with) flowers, water, light, and incense)’, in the matter of ‘*ezhil koL* *sOdhi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.3.1\] (the beautiful light ([emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) who is visible for everyone (unlike the one in SrI vaikuNtam and kshIrAbdhi/thiruppArkkadal))’, at all times that is ‘*ozhivil kAlam ellAm* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.3.1\];

and, this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s sOthi star day itself came after that for this AchAryan;

[![periya-thirumalai-nambi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periya-thirumalai-nambi-897x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periya-thirumalai-nambi.jpg)*periya thirumalai nambi*

Not only that, as said in ‘*thUNAi adhanOdu ariyAy vandhu thOnRi* \[periya thirumozhi 1.10.5\] (came and appeared from within the pillar)’, as can be said as ‘*jvalantham* \[nrusimha manthram\]’ (emits/form of – light), this AchAryan’s [thiruvArAdhana](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/07/srivaishnava-thiruvaaraadhanam.html) emperumAn is also of sOthi star day.

svAthi star day is of the group of dhEvas in the form of light. Also, as said in ‘*thrEthAyAm AdhikalpE kilakamalayukE mAdhavE mAsipakshE SuklE sAdhyE cha yOgE vaNijasukaraNE bhUthathidhyAm marudhbhE \| mandhE vArE pradhOshE kanakakaSipu samhArahEthOrjanithvA*’ **(**In thrEthA yugam, previous kalpam, kilakamala yugam, vaikAsi month Sukla paksham, sAdhya yOgam, vaNija karaNam, saturday, pradhOsham He was born to kill hiraNya kaSipu**)**, it describes the incarnation of narasimhar in the star day of svAthi.

So this day is also of muppuri (three auspicious happenings at the same time) by incarnations of narasimhar, [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html), and [periya thirumalai nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/01/periya-thirumalai-nambi/).

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – १८
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mAnilaththil mun)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-17)

**pAsuram 18**

*mangaLAsAsanaththil maRRuLLa AzhvArgaL*  
*thangaL Arvaththu aLavu thAN anRi – pongum*  
*parivAlE villipuththUr pattar pirAn peRRAn*  
*periyAzhvAr ennum peyar* 18

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-18-new)

**Word by word meaning**

mangaLAsAsanaththil *–* In doing mangaLASAsanam (wishing long live)  
*maRRuLLa AzhvArgaL thangaL* – the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*Arvaththu aLavu thAn anRi* – limited by their love, unlike that,  
*pongum* – increasing/overflowing  
*parivAlE* – affection  
*villipuththUr* – one who incarnated in [SrIvillipuththur](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/)  
*pattar pirAn* – head of the learned  
*peRRAr(n)* – is having/got  
*periyAzhvAr ennum peyar* – the divine name of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)

**vyAkyAnam**

Considering the difference between other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) in doing mangaLASAsanam he got the name of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) – and through this he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining about the greatness, starting with *‘mangaLAsAsanaththil’.*

That is, when it comes to mangaLASAsanam, unlike other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ level of devotion, due to the abundant/increased affection towards [bhagavAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who is identified as belonging to [SrIvillipuththur](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/), got the divine name of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

mangaLAsAsanam is – due to the tenderness/delicateness of that one (that is, [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), even at the expense of destruction of self, he ([AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)) would wish to create greatness for Him. svarUpam (nature) is to create greatness for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) isn’t it? It was divined as ‘*SEshikku athisayaththai viLaikkai SEshabhUthanukku svarUpa lAbhamum prApyamum* \[mumukshuppadi – 177\] (Creating greatness for the master is the nature and destiny of the servant).

Getting ‘*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\]’ (unblemished knowledge) etc., are same among them, but when it comes to mangaLASAsanam, this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s depth in it makes a difference.

***AzhvArgaL thangaL Arvam*** – As said in ‘*adhanil periya en avA* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) 10.10.10\]*’*, ones desires are so big, asking for everything of [sentient](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/), [non-sentient](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/09/thathva-thrayam-achith-what-is-matter/) and (even) [Isvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/); and it is this desire to be destroyed is what they (the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)) wished for.

Their interest is like said in ‘*abhinivEsam pOvadhu anubhavaththAlE* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 293\]’, (~ their rush of devotion gets under control after getting the divine experience)

and ‘*saththA samrudhdhigaL dharsana anubhava kainkaryangaLAlE* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 257\]’ ((the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’) being/living is based on being able to see [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), getting that experience, and doing kainkaryam to Him).

So this happens only once in a while for these [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/).

In this way they wished for their getting the completeness, of Him;, whereas for [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) it is about Him getting the completeness, which he sustains based on his mangaLASAsanam. This is the higher level of devotion of this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

***pongum parivAlE*** – Due to the ever multiplying affection; that is, as said in ‘*anbE perugum* \[periya thiruvanthAdhi – 8\] (In your matter my love is ever increasing), and ‘*enthan aLavanRAl yAnudaiya anbu’* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi – 100\] (the love adiyEn have got for you does not stay within me), and ‘*snEhOmE parama:* \[SrI rAmAyaNam uththara kAndam – 40-16\] (I have got only affection more for you), not stopping at surrendering to Him but his love (flood) is crossing the shores.

It is similarly said in *‘sOrAdha kAdhal perun chuzhippAl thollai mAlai onRum pArAdhu avanaip pallANdu enRu kAppidum pAnmaiyan thAL* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 15](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-15/)\]*’*.

His love matches that of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s love; the love of one who is supreme is matched by this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s devotion.

Now, it is talking about the greatness of the divine name that came from the greatness of such devotion.

[![perialwar1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perialwar1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perialwar1.jpg)*periyAzhwAr as divining in SrIvillipuththUr*

***villipuththUr pattar pirAn peRRAn periyAzhvAr ennum peyar*** – The whole reason for saying this name for him, is his birth in this place isn’t it? Similar to saying, ‘*ArAdha kAdhal kurugUrch chatakOpan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) 2.1.11\]*’* (uncontrollable love [kurugUrch chatakOpan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) – (this says it along with the place where [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) was born)).

*villipuththUr pattar pirAn –* It says his village, lineage, and occupation respectively.

His identity is ‘*villipuththUr udaiyAn*’. Also saying ‘*vishNu chiththan*’, and ‘*kOyilil vAzhum vaittaNavan* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 5.1.3\] (~ am a SrIvaishNavan who is always in the temple)’, he is like ‘*vishNunA vyapadhEshtavya:*’ (should say by the name of [vishNu](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) – everything is that for this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

*pattar pirAn peRRAn periyAzhvAr ennum peyar –* after getting the fame/name by establishing the supremacy of [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), since he performed mangaLASAsanam due to worrying about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s delicate divine body, this is the name he got.

Since mangaLASAsanam is done by him all the time every day, this divine name got established fully for him.

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – १९
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mangaLAsAsanaththil)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-18)

**pAsuram – 19**

*kOdhilavAm AzhvArgaL kURu kalaikkellAm*  
*Adhi thiruppallANdu Anadhuvum – vEdhaththukku*  
*Om ennum adhu pOl uLLadhukkellAm surukkAyth*  
*thAn mangalamAdhalAl*
19

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-19)

**Word by word meaning**

*kalaikku ellAm* – Among all the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/),  
*kOdhu ilavAm* – (all of which are) non-blemished  
*AzhvArgaL kURu* – which are divined by [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/),  
[*thiruppallANdu*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/),  
*Anadhuvum* – is arranged  
*Adhi* – as the first;  
*Om ennumadhu pOl* – Like Om is recited (first)  
*vEdhaththukku* – for the vEdhas,  
*thAn* – that [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)  
*surukku Ay* – is as the summary/essence  
*uLLadhukku* *ellAm* – for all the other [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)  
*mangalam AdhalAl* – because it is the auspicious mangaLASAsanam.

**vyAkyAnam**

Now he (maNavALa mAmunigaL) is divining about the greatness of this with an example through this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s dhivya prabandham that is [thirupallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)’s placement as the first of all [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), by starting with ‘*kOdhilavAm*’.

Mistake *(kOdhu)* in a poem is – talking about some other story. That is not present here. For these [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), starting with ‘*rAmAyaNam, nArAyaNa kathai* \[AchArya hrudhayam 63\]’ author of AchArya hrudhayam ([azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nAyanAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/)) has established showing that this problem exists in those (rAmAyaNa, etc), and does not exist in the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/);

Or, when ‘no mistakes’ is taken as an adjective for [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) (*kOdhilavAm AzhvArgaL*), they don’t have the mistake of even a hint of trying some other means on their own for reaching him which in turn would prevent getting [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s grace, nor do they have any less haste in wishing to reach [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). These [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are having love without any mistakes.

[![Azhvars](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/Azhvars.gif)

**AzhvArgaL kURu kalaikkellAm –** For the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) divined by the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who do not have any blemishes and so can be referenced (pramANam), and all of them speak the same in unison, and their [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) are ‘*gyAnak kalaigaL* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.9.8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/thiruvaimozhi-1-9-8-navinul-ninru/)\]’ (pAsurams based on their (faultless) knowledge), and are sAsthras about ‘*adhyAthma vidhyai* \[vEdhArththa sangraham\]’ (“jIva paramAthma”).

– for all such [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) …

***Adhi thiruppallANdu Anadhuvum* –** this ([thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)) is foremost among all the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/); like how:

***vEdhaththukku, etc. –*** As said in, ‘*praNavAdhyAs thathA vEdhA: – OngkAra prabhavA vEdhA:* \[lakvathri samruthi 1.9\]’ (All vEdhas include praNavam as first; vEdhas came from praNavam), and ‘*vAngmayam praNavam sarvam* \[vishNu dharmam – 67.6\]’ (All the four vEdhas came from brahmA’s face),

(so) praNavam is the essence of all the vEdhas;

starting from ‘*OngkArach chAdhA sabdhachcha* \[Word that is Om\]*’*, it says ‘*thasmAnmAnggaLikAvubhou* \[so the two auspicious\]’, and ‘*a ithi bhagavathO nArAyaNasya pradhamAbhidhAnam \| kimnAma mangaLam na krutham* \[What mangaLam has not been done when he has started with ‘a’ (first part of praNavam (a-u-m)), that is the first divine name of bhagavAn [nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)\]’ (mahA bhAshyam kaiyadam-1\], is having auspicious ways in the beginning,

Like how ‘*yadhvEdhadhau svara: prOktha:* \[thaiththiriyOpanishath nArAyaNavalli 10-24\]’ (the sound that is recited first for vEdham) , the praNavam is in the beginning of vEdhas, [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) too (is recited first in [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/));

Like said in ‘*prApyasya brahmaNO rUpam* \[hArItha smruthi 8-141\]’, etc., (nature of the goal ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))), all of their meaning is about [artha panchakam](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/artha-panchakam.html) (five aspects of it – nature of [emperumAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), nature of [individual soul](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/), way to reach Him, activity/goal of individual soul after reaching [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and hurdles that stop souls from reaching the goal); since these are divined in his prabandham ([thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)), and starting from ‘*pallANdu pallANdu* ([thiruppallANdu – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-1-pallandu/))’, through ‘*sUzhndhu irundhu Eththuvar pallaNdE* \[[thiruppallaNdu
-12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruppallandu-12-pallandu-enru/)\]’ it is mangaLASAsanam everywhere,

like so, since it is having the quality of being the essence, and being auspicious, there is no issue in this also being the first of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

Some more – Like how thirumanthram that is having praNavam in the beginning is important for reaching [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) which is its explanation is also acceptable to be the first (of [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)).

Not only that, for all the other [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) which talk about the greatness of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), this prabandham ([thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)) is present in the beginning and in the end, and so protects the [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

This protection is as said in ‘*brahmaNa: praNava kuryAdhAdhAvanthE cha sarvadha \| sravanthyanOngkrutham pUrvam parasthAchcha visIryathE* \[dharma sAsthram\]’ (It is special, that to begin with, for brahmam in all states/stages, in the beginning and end, praNavam is pronounced).

[![periyazhwar-srivilliputhur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-srivilliputhur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-srivilliputhur.jpg)*periyAzhvAr – [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/)*

With this, it is concluded that like how this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) is foremost among the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), [his prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) also is foremost about the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

– – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – २०
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (kOdhilavAm AzhvArgaL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-19)

**pAsuram 20**

*uNdO thiruppallANdukku oppadhOr kalai thAn*  
*uNdO periyAzhvArkku oppu uruvar – thaN thamizh nUl*  
*seydhu aruLum AzhvArgaL thammil avar sey kalaiyil*  
*paidhal nenjE nee uNarndhu pAr* 20

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-20)

**Word by word meaning**

*uNdO* – Is there  
*oppadhu* – an equal  
*Or kalai thAn* – prabandham  
*thiruppallANdukku* – for [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)  
*uNdO* – is there?  
*oppu oruvar* – an equal person  
*periyAzhvArkku* – for [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)?  
(Is there an equal)  
*AzhvArgaL thammil* – among [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*seydhu aruLum* – who divined  
*nUl* – prabandhams  
*thaN thamizh* – (in) sweet thamizh (*eerath thamizh*),  
*kalaiyil* – and among the prabandhams  
*avar* – (that) those [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*sey* – divined,  
*paidhal nenjE –* Oh childish mind!  
*nee* – you  
*uNarndhu pAr* – try to know.

**vyAkyAnam**

Further more, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining about the greatness of this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) and also his [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) due to there being no equal for them, starting with *‘uNdO thiruppallANdukku’.*

[![maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/maNavALa_mAmunigaL_thiruvaheendhrapuram-closup.jpg)*maNavALa mAmunigaL – thiruvaheendhrapuram*

For this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) which is focused only on doing mangaLASasanam, is there an equal in other [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that are focused on experiencing [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and be immersed in that**?**

Difference is that ‘*pallANdum paramAthmanaich chUzhndhu irundhu Eththuvar pallANdE* \[[thiruppallANdu – 12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruppallandu-12-pallandu-enru/)\]’ (would be around [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) for ever and do mangaLASasanam to Him),

(as compared to the following where it is about one’s experiencing of and immersed in the matter of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) only)

‘*AyiraththuL ivaiyum Or paththum vallAr URRin kaN nuN maNal pOl urugA niRpar neerAyE* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.8.11\]’ (Like the fine sand near a spring, their mind (who learn this) would melt (for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))), and in

‘*onbadhOdu onRukkum mUvulagum urugumE* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.5.11\]’ (Those in all the three world would melt),

– is how the difference of this prabandham ([thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)) is compared to these other [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

***uNdO periyAzhvArkku oppu oruvar –*** Can he ([periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)) who sustains himself by doing mangaLASAsanam to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s beauty etc., be equaled by other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who are (only) immersed in such beauty, etc., of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)?

Starting from ‘*adiyOmOdum* \[[thiruppallANdu – 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-2-adiyomodum/)\]’ (we and you shall live forever), through ‘*pAncha chanyamum pallANdE* \[[thiruppallANdu
-2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-2-adiyomodum/)\] (including the disc and the conch shall live forever), such is the state of this [Azhvar](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html), and can he be equaled by the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who say ‘*adiyEn innam thaLarvEnO* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – 6.9.3\]’ (even though I am having your relationship would I still be here and suffer (due to separation from you)),

‘*chinthai kalangith thirumAl enRu azhaippan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.8.10\]” ((Thinking whether I would be able to reach and live with you) with my worried mind I would call your divine name out (thirumAl)), and “*chakkaraththu aNNalE enRu thAzhndha(u) kaNNeer thathumba* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.7.10\]” (Saying that you mesmerized me by showing your disc and conch, would drop tears due to not getting your experience now), etc., where they get immersed in every which way they related to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) – so he ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) (of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/))) cannot equal this [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) isn’t it? This is applicable for other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) as well.
