***thaN thamizh nUl seydhu aruLum AzhvArgaL thammil uNdO periyAzhvArkku oppu oruvar –*** The other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) through the grace of [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) had divined their [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) in sweet thamizh, can they equal [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who by nature cannot sustain himself without doing mangaLASAsanam to [emperuman](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)?

***avar sei kalaiyil thiruppallANdukkum oppadhu Or kalai thAn uNdO –*** As they wished by His grace their sustenance and growth (of experience with [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), can they equal [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who wishes well for the growth of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)?

kalai -\> dhrAvida [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/); their [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) are in thamizh that talk about [brahmam](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/).

Among these, about the greatness of this [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) –

***paidhal nenjE nee uNarndhu pAr*** – (Oh the childish mind you try to know whether those are equal to this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)) – Get out of your dumbness and using your true nature of having wisdom analyze the difference in greatness of this.

Since in the aspect of getting‘ ‘*mayarvaRa mathinalam’* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\] (unblemished knowledge) and divining [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) based on that is same among all of the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)**,** Oh the ignorant mind which thinks that due to this the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) are equal to [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) and his [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/)!

At least now, since you have the ability to understand the huge difference between these, think properly and analyze it. Then only you can understand their huge difference.

– – – – – –


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – २१
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (uNdO thiruppallANdukku)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-20)

**pAsuram 21**

*AzhvAr thirumagaLAr ANdAL madhurakavi*  
*AzhvAr ethirAsarAm ivargaL – vAzhvAga*  
*vandhu udhiththa mAthangAL nALgaL thammin vAsiyaiyum*  
*indha ulagOrkku uraippOm yAm* 21

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-21)

**Word by word meaning**

*AzhvAr* – [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s  
*thirumagaLAr* – divine daughter, that is,  
*ANdAL* – [sUdikkoduththa nAchchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/), and  
*[madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html)*, and  
*ethirAsar* – [SrI bhAshyakArar (emperumAnAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/),  
*Am ivargaL* – so these three,  
*vAzhvu Aga* – for the people of this world to gain the true goal,  
*vandhu udhiththa* – they came and divined their incarnation,  
*yAm* – we  
*uraippOm* – shall say  
*indha ulagOrkku* – to those in this world (about the)  
*vAsiyaiyum* – greatness of those  
*mAthangaL* – months  
*nALgaL thammin* – and days (of incarnations).

**vyAkyAnam**

Thus in the last five pAsurams after [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) talked about this [AzhvAr’s (periyAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) greatness through the greatness of his birth star day, now as [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) had mentioned near the beginning of this prabandham as ‘*anthamizhAl naR kalaigaL Ayndhu uraiththa AzhvArgaL’* through ‘*vandhu udhiththa mAthangAL nALgaL thammai maNNulagOr thAm aRiya eedhu enRu solluvOm yAm’* \[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 5\], and as per that intention of going in the order of the months/start days, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) talked in detail about AzhvArs’ months and days of incarnation,

and now [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) vows to talk about the order of months and days of incarnations of [ANdAL](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-andal-anubhavam.html), [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html), and [ethirAsar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

***AzhvAr thirumagaLAr etc.* –** Since these three stayed firm in AchArya AbhimAnam (being cared by AchArya and fully dependant on AchArya), and are incarnations of pirAtti (bhUdhEvi), thiruvadi (garudAzhwAr), and thiruvananthAzhvAn (AdhiSEsha) respectively, they can be grouped together in this special way!

[![periyazhwar-andal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-andal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-andal.jpg)*AzhvAr thirumagaLAr ANdAL*

[ANdaL](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-andal-anubhavam.html): ‘*vittu chiththar thangaL thEvarai* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi – 10.10\]’ ( (if) [vishNu chiththar (periyAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) brings his lord (then we will be able to have His darshan)),

[madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html): ‘*thEvu maRRaRiyEn* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/)\]’ (do not know any other lord (than [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/))),

[![nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)*madhurakavi AzhvAr (with nammAzhvAr)*

and

[ethirAsar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/): ‘*adi paNindhu uyndha* \[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 1\]’ (reached the true goal having reached the divine feet of [mARan (nammAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/));

[![emperumAnAr-nammAzhwAr](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/emperumAnAr-nammAzhwAr.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/emperumAnAr-nammAzhwAr.jpg)*ethirAsar with nammAzhvAr*

These three belong to ‘*adi paNindhu uyndha*‘ (became glorious by taking shelter of AchArya) group.

As said in ‘*anantha: prathamam rUpam* \[nAradheeyam. yAdhavAdhri mahAthmiyam 1.32\]’ (thiruvananthAzhvAn first mUrththy), etc., and ‘*aheenAmeeSvar SrImAnAseeth rAmAnujO muni:* ’ (rAmAnujar is being the head of serpents). The greatness of other two is given in detail in *guruparamparA prabhAvam*. So [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divines the incarnation of these three.

***AzhvAr thirumagaLAr ANdAL*** – bhUmi pirAtti as [ANdAL](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-andal-anubhavam.html) incarnated as divine daughter of [periyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Like (seethA) pirAtti incarnating as janaka rAjan’s divine daughter. They incarnated, not from a womb (not based on karma), in vEndhar kulam (king’s lineage), and vEyar kulam ([periyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s clan).

***madhurakavi AzhvAr* –** [madhurkavi azhvar](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html) is ‘*then kurugUr nambikku anbanAi* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiruth-thambu-11-anban-thannai/)\]’ (devoted to [*then kurugUr nambi* (nammAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)), like how ‘*padaiththAn kavi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.9.10\]’ (([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) is) poet of [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) {That is, [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html) is to [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), what [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) is to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)}.

Unlike saying what ever came to mouth, he is like ‘*kurugUr nambi pAvin innisai pAdith thirivanE* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/)\] (will sing [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s pleasant pAsurams), having such delicateness of words. That is, ‘*nambi enRakkAl aNNikkum amudhu Urum en nAvukkE* \[[kaNNinuN chiruthhtAmbu – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-1-kanninun/)\]’ (~ saying the word [(then kurugUr) nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) would make nectar spring in my tongue).

***ethirAsar Am ivargaL*** – [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is the head of yathis (saints) .

In this way the three having such greatness –

***vAzhvAga vandhu udhiththa*** – Rose as a wealth for the world; they are the wealth for [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) who incarnated as the wealth for the world; and they are the wealth for sAthvikas (ones having tranquil nature / {SrIvaishNavas} ).

As said in ‘*vakuLAbharaNAnghriyugmam* \[parAnkusa ashtakam – 1\]’ (of divine feet of [nammazhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)), and ‘*mEvinEn avan ponnadi meymmaiyE* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/)\]’ (surrendered to his beautiful feet, and this is the truth), and ‘*mARan adi paNindhu uyndhavan* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-1/)\]’ (([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) surrendered unto AzhwAr’s feet and attained the true goal), they are like the divine feet of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/).

Not only that, as they have surrendered and be like a sandal on [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s divine feet, and so they are compared to the lines in the divine feet, and as the protection for the feet; so [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divined ‘*pon adiyE nanthamakkup pon* \[thiruvAimozhi nURRanthAdhi\]’ ([AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s beautiful feet is our wealth/beauty);

Apt living and reaching \[of the goal\] are by being a servant of that feet, isn’t it?

In this way the three of them incarnated as the wealth of SrIvaishNavam, for enriching SrI vaishNava SrI (wealth of SrIvaishNavam).

Their –

***mAdhangaL nALgaL thammil vAsiyaiyum*** – (months and days of incarnation; distinguished greatness of those days) – In this way as they incarnated for the world to get the life as the true existent being – the uniqueness of the months and days of their incarnation,

***indha ulagOrkku uraippOm yAm* –** For the ignorant and knowledgeable ones of this world to know well about the greatness of these star days, we who knows the unique differences/greatness of these days of incarnation of [ANdAL](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-andal-anubhavam.html) et al., shall talk about it to you whether you asked for it or not;

Isn’t it AchAryas’ ways to teach the sentient after seeing their humility as said in ‘*aRiyAdhana aRivikkai* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam
-14\] (teaching them what they are ignorant about).

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २२
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvAr thirumgaLAr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-21)

**pAsuram 22**

*inRO thiruvAdippUram emakkAga*  
*anRo ingu ANdAL avathariththAL – kunRAdha*  
*vAzhvAga(na) vaikuntha vAn pOkam thannai igazhndhu*  
*AzhvAr thirumagaLArAi           
* 22

[Liten](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-22)

**Word by word meaning**

*thiru AdippUram* – beautiful month of Adi’s pUram star (AsAdha, pUrva)  
*inRO* – is it today!  
*emakkAga anRO* – Isn’t it for us only,  
*vAzhvu Aga* – to have life  
*kunRAdha* – not having any shortcomings (of this material world),  
*igazhndhu* – (that she) left  
*vaikuntham* – SrI vaikuNtam of  
*vAn* – best  
*pOkam thannai* – comforts,  
*ANdAL* – (that is,) [sUdik koduththa nAchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)  
*avathariththAL* – had incarnated  
*ingu* – in this world  
*AzhvAr thirumagaLArAi* – as the divine daughter of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

**vyAkyAnam**

Out of the three mentioned in the previous pAsuram, [he (maNavALa mAmunigaL)](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) starts with talking about [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who is the best among them, using three pAsurams; in this pAsuram [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) melts by engagement of [his](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) experience, in the thought whether today is *thiru Adip pUram (AsAdha, pUrva)* when [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) divined her incarnation to help [him](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) reach the goal.

***inRO thiruvAdippUram*** – Is it today what is famously known as thiruvAdippUram? Is it today that we were granted such a day? If we got what is rare, then, doesn’t that become cause for enjoyment?

[He](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining the reason next.

***emakkAga anRO ingu ANdAL avathariththAL*** – Like when her baby falls in a well a mother would also jump in the same way to save it, ([she](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) incarnated to) take us out who have drowned in births (in this material world)? [She](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who is the mother for all beings has divined [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) incarnation here. Like said in “*kUpaththil vIzhum kuzhaviyudan kudhiththu avvApaththai nIkkum andha annaiyaip pOl* \[Arththip prabandham – 9\]” (like the mother who also falls into the water and removes the danger), and in “*kUpAntharmukthaputhram pathAthamanupathan mAthruvath”* (Like how a mother would jump in to save the baby that fell into the well), [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) who is completely knowledgeable is considering [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) incarnation as for [him](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/).

[![ANDALpainting](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/ANDALpainting.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/ANDALpainting.jpg)*SrI ANdAL*

Next it talks about the rarity of such incarnation, by ‘*kunRAdha’,* etc.

Unlike the experience of other places which are not complete/not without shortcomings, in SrI vaikuNtam there is no hindrance to any greatness where limitless [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) is to be enjoyed – discarding such enjoyment, here too ‘*pOkaththil vazhuvAdha pudhuvaiyar kOn kOthai* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi 8.10\]’ (As the daughter of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who enjoys [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) fully), [she](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) incarnated ‘*AzhvAr thirumagaLArAi* (as [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s divine daughter, her highness)’.

Like how a queen would give less importance to the flowery bed of the king and lie down holding her baby’s cradle, [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) too ignored the limitless enjoyment of paramapadham, and came incarnating here.

Isn’t this what creates sorrow in the mind of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)?

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २३
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvAr thirumagaLAr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-22)

**pAsuram 23**

*periyAzhvAr peN piLLaiyAy ANdAL piRandha*  
*thiruvAdip pUraththin seermai – oru nALaikku*  
*uNdO manamE uNarndhu pAr ANdALukku*  
*uNdAgil oppu itharkum uNdu* 23

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-23)

**Word by word meaning**

*uNdO* – Is there  
*seermai* – greatness  
*oru nALaikku* – in any other day (compared to)  
*thiru AdippUraththin* – the beautiful Adi month pUram star day  
*ANdAL* – (in which) [sUdik koduththa nAchchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)  
*piRandha* – divined her incarnation  
*periyAzhvAr* – (as) [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s  
*peN piLLaiyAy* – divine daughter;  
*manamE, uNarndhu pAr* – Oh mind! Analyze and become clear about this.  
*uNdAgil* – if there is  
*oppu* – an equal  
*ANdALukku* – for [sUdik koduththa nAchchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/), (then)  
*uNdu* – there would be an equal day  
*itharkum* – for this day too.

**vyAkyAnam**

Now as in this way she incarnated, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines the greatness of this star day through showing that there is no equal to this day, with ‘*periyAzhvAr peN piLLaiyAy’.*

It is the greatness of him ([AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)) who is the reason for [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) birth.

[periyAzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyazhwar/) who was having the main kainkaryam of making flower garlands, found her ([ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)) under a thiruththuzhAy (thuLasi) plant, and took her and gave her in the hands of his dhEviyAr (wife), and she was childless, she took this girl of someone else with a lot of affection; at that time, her breasts produced a lot of milk as said in ‘*van mulaigaL sOrndhu pAya* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 2.2.4\]’ ((as yaSOdha saying to krishNan) my beautiful breasts due to my love for you are producing milk which is pouring out). It is usually only for the mothers who delivered their babies that the milk would produce when they have their children. So it talks about her being their girl child.

*[![periyazhwar-andal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-andal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/periyazhwar-andal.jpg)periyAzhvAr’s divine daughter ANdAL*

***ANdAL piRandha*** – This is one (great) birth of [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) having greatness. nAchchiyAr who has got the worlds {bhUdhEvi} has come and incarnated in this world.

***piRandha –* ‘***nAnum piRandhamai poy anRE* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi – 10.4\]’ ((if chakkaravarththith thirumagan’s words are not truthful, then only) my birth would also be not truthful), is how she has talked (about [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) own birth).

The one who got (janakan) and the one who was born (sIthA pirAtti) also say ‘*mE pithA, me suthA* \[SrI rAmAyaNam – bhAla kAndam 73.27\]’ (my father, my daughter); in the same way [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) too said ‘*oru magaL thannai udaiyEn* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi – 3.8.4\]’ (am having only one daughter (though this is said in a different context)), and his daughter [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) too said ‘*pattar pirAn kOthai*’ ([periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html)’s daughter [gOdhA (AndAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)).

***piRandha thiruvAdippUraththin seermai*** – Because of birth only the greatness is present for this day. When said there isn’t any other day that are mentioned till now that has got this greatness, then if there is a question as to why not, then,

***manamE uNarndhu pAr* –** Oh the mind which has got the ability to analyse well, instead of giving a cursory look, you think deeply again and again about this day.

**ANdALukku uNdAgil oppu itharkum uNdu –** It there is an equal to [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who rules all the worlds, then there would be an equal to this day also.

About her it was said ‘*avargaLilum kAttil vinjina kshamA dhayAdhi guNangaLaiyum nAvAl thogaikka oNNAdha azhagaiyum udaiyaLAy*’ (~ having qualities such as forgiving and kind mind compared to those others, and having beauty that cannot be expressed in words) is how it is divined.

So the meaning is that like how there is no equal to [her](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/), there is no equal to her incarnation month and star day as well.

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २४
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (periyAzhvAr peN piLLaiyAy)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-23)

[![andal](https://guruparamparai.files.wordpress.com/2012/12/andal1.jpg?w=625)](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/12/16/andal/andal-2/)

**pAsuram – 24**

*anju kudikku oru santhathiyAy AzhvArgaL*  
*tham seyalai vinji niRkum thanmaiyaLAi – pinjAip*  
*pazhuththALai ANdALaip paththiyudan nALum*  
*vazhuththAi manamE magizhndhu.* 24

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-24)

  
**Word by word meaning**

*ANdALai* – [sUdik koduththAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/),  
*oru* – (who incarnated as an) unparalleled  
*santhathiyAy* – divine daughter  
*anju kudikku* – of the lineage of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who are afraid of the cruel world, and so do mangaLASasanam, (and who is)  
*vinji niRkum* – being of special state than  
*AzhvArgaL tham* – [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’  
*seyalai* – ways of gyAna (true knowledge) bhakthi (devotion) vairAgyam (steadfastness in following the principles of SrIvaishNavam), etc., (and who is)  
*thanmaiyaLAi* – having that nature,  
*pazhuththALai* – being very mature  
*pinju Ay* – when being very young,\`  
*manamE* – Oh the mind!  
*vazhuththAi* – you shall worship  
*nALum* – always  
*magizhndhu* – happily  
*paththiyudan* – with devotion.

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining to his mind to worship [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) happily, [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who has got more greatness compared to (other) [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), as in ‘*anju kudikku oru santhathiyAy’.*

That is, as said in ‘*santhAna bheejam kuru pANdavAnAm*’ (only son for the lineage of the pANdavas), like how parIkshith himself was the offspring for the five pANdavas,

[ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) too, for the lineage of prapannas that is [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), is being the one child as a divine daughter. As she is part of the clan of having true knowledge, she is referred by them as ‘*kula magaL kOthai’* (~ daughter of the lineage, [gOdhA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)).

Or, being an unmatched offspring of the lineage of [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) who at a much later time would do mangaLASAsanam by being afraid of some wonderful valor that [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) showed at a much earlier time. This is reflected in ‘*bhagavath yajaSramasthAna rakshaNa bhayAkula vamsajAthAm* \[jIyar nAyanAr who is [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s divine grandson in pUravAsaramam – his upadhEsa raththinamAlai slOkam
-24 ?\]’.

[ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) too starting with ‘*anRu ivvulagam ALandhAi adi pORRi*’, performed mangaLASAsanam at present, for the glorious deeds of the past of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), isn’t it? Reason for her doing mangaLASAsanam is the lineage of her birth, isn’t it?

This lineage is identified as ‘*anju(m) kudi’* (clan that is afraid (as shown above)), isn’t it?

***AzhArgaL tham seyalai vinji niRkum thanmaiyaLAi*** – that is, while matching her father [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) in doing manaLASAsanam, she is supreme compared to the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) in gyAnam (true knowledge), bhakthi (devotion), vairAgyam (steadfastness), etc.

Since she gets bhakthi as ‘family wealth’ (being in the lineage of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)), and in addition unlike the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ who have to pretend to be a woman in their various states of bhakthi, she can be herself (a female), and so she is having wonderful level of bhakthi compared to them.

That is, unlike [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who in their urge to get [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) had used means other than Him, like starting with things like doing nOnbu (vratham – austerity), taking madal (calling out emperumAn in public) etc., which would destroy ananyOpAyathvam of a devotee (not using anything other than Him as the means), [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) said towards kAma dhEvan (deity of love) – ‘*pEsuvadhu onRu uNdu ingu emperumAn* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi – 1.8\]*’* (addressing kAma dhEvan: now there is something I need to convey to you, who is my swAmy/master (to bless me as one who gets to caress the lotus feet of krishNan)), and ‘*unnaiyum umbiyaiyum thozhudhEn* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi 1.1\]’ (addressing kAma dhEvan: worshiping you and your brother sAman (please make me do kainkaryam to thiruvEnkatamudaiyAn/SrInivAsa)), and ‘*thozhudhu muppOdhumunnadi vaNangi* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi 1.9\]’ (again addressing kAma dhEvan: three times a day I surrender to you completely and prostrate unto your feet ( and am expecting you to help me do kainkaryam to krishNan)), – and so she was thinking of kAma dhEvan himself as the main deity, thus crossing the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ limit of using other means for getting [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)!

***pinjAyp pazhuththALai –*** That is, in the world when something ripens, as said in ‘*palasya kAraNam pushpam*’, it would have gone through the stages of flower, tender fruit, then unripe fruit, and after some days among these stages it becomes a ripe fruit, isn’t it? Unlike that, it is as if the tender fruit without becoming unripe fruit had become ripe fruit by itself, is how [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)’s ways are.

That is, instead of going through the stages of para bhakthi, para gyAnam, and parama bhakthi regarding devotion to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) as said in ‘*gyAnam kanindha nalam* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 66\] (~ knowledge ripening ultimately to parama bhakthi), when she was too young when typically knowledge would not be pronounced, that she ripened to reach parama bhakthi. That is, the natural bhakthi was present in her at that itself.

Like when she was *five* years old when usually knowledge is not pronounced, she compiled [thiruppAvai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/11/thiruppavai-english/).

If asking whether what someone who is five years old say would be significant, there are examples like [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s ‘*mulaiyO muzhu muRRum pOndhila* \[thiruviruththam – 60\] (too young that she is not even having enough of breast to distinguish from that of a boy (etc., but she still has bhakthi toward [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and talks about thiruvEnkatam, etc.,)), and more such examples.

And the knowledge of being devoted to devotees which the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) got at a last stage, she got it in the beginning stage itself. That is, in the padhigam (decad) of ‘*nedumARkadimai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.10\]’, it explained the greatness of them (devotees) as ‘*nanimAk kalavi inbamE nALum vAykka nangatkE* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.10.7\]*’* (wish to get always the togetherness with your devotees), and as ‘*thamargaL thamargaL thamargaLAm sathirE vAikka nangatkE* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.10.9\], (~ wish to get the opportunity to serve the devotees of devotees of devotees of you), that is the sweetness of the view of being together with [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s devotees was talked about (by [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) ;

also [(thirumangai) AzhvAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/) divined in the padhikam (decad) of ‘*kaN sOra vengkuruthi* \[periya thirumozhi 7.4\] he said ‘*tha(va)N sERai emperumAnukku adiyAr thammaik kaNdu enakku idhu kANeer en nenjum kaNNiNaiyum kaLikkumARE* \[periya thirumozhi 7.4.6\]’ (see here how my mind and my eyes are ecstatic after seeing the devotees of sAranAthap perumAL at the beautiful thiruchchERai dhivya dhESam), and ‘*thaN sERai emperumAn thALai nALum sindhippArkku en uLLam thEn Uri eppozhudhum thiththikkumE* \[7.4.5\]’ (Regarding the devotees who meditate on the divine feet of sAranAthap perumAL at the comfortable thiruchchERai, my mind produces nectar and it is very sweet for me),

Not taking that long (in to the prabandham to talk about the devotees), she did it in the beginning (of her prabandham) itself like in ‘*pOdhuveer pOdhuminO* \[[thiruppAvai – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-01-margazhi-thingal/)\]’ (said towards other gOpikAs (devotees): Oh you who are interested in bathing (krishNa anubhavam) please join), and ‘*ellArum pOndhArO* \[[thiruppAvai – 15](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-15-elle-ilam-kiliye/)\]’ (Have all the ones (devotees) who have to join (for going to krishNan) have come? (always including devotees for worshiping emperumAn)).

***ANdALai –*** Like in this way she being very matured (ripened), and having the greatness of the aforementioned qualities;

***paththiyudan nALum vazhuththAi manamE magizhndhu –*** Like how she is having unblemished bhakthi towards [bhagavAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), you (mind) have that bhakthi towards [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) and do mangaLASAsanam in the form of praise (sthuthi) every day – ‘*gOdhA thasyai nama idhamidham bhUyayEvAsthu bhUya:* \[[thiruppAvai thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-thaniyans-invocation/)\]’ (~ [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who is immersed in kaNNan, my similar reverence be placed toward [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) having such greatness, till eternity ), and also involve with affection in ‘*mangaiyum pallANdu* \[thiruppallANdu – 1\]’. It is as said in ‘*uRREn ugandhu paNi seidhu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.8.10\]’ (reached your divine feet and be able to do kainkaryam).

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २५
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (anju kudikkoru)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-24)

**pAsuram 25**

*ErAr madhurakavi ivvulagil vandhu udhiththa*  
*seerArum chiththiraiyil chiththirai nAL – pArulagil*  
*maRRuLLa AzhvArgaL vandhu udhiththa nALgaLilum*  
*uRRadhu emakku enRu nenjE Or.* 25

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-25)

**Word by word meaning**

*Er Ar* – Full of beauty (that is)  
*madhurakavi* – [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)  
*vandhu udhiththa* – came and divined his incarnation  
*iv ulagil* – in this world  
*seer Arum* – (in the) fully great  
*chiththiraiyil* – month of chiththirai (chaithra)  
*chiththirai nAL* – in the star day of chiththirai (chithrA);  
*emakku* – for us  
*uRRadhu* *enRu* – (this day is to be chosen because) it matches our svarUpam (true nature)  
*nALgaLilum* – than the divine star days of  
*maRRuLLa* – the other  
*AzhvArgaL* – ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*vandhu udhiththa* – who came and divined their incarnation  
*pAr ulagil* – in the earth;  
*nenjE* – Oh my mind  
*Or* – understand this.

**vyAkyAnam**

Out of the three mentioned earlier, considering the middle one that is [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/), he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines to his confidential mind that the chiththirai star day (chithrA) during vasantha (spring) season (month of chiththirai (chaithra)), which is the star day of this [AzhvAr,](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) is the one that would be apt for our svarUpam (true nature (of serving [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)’s devotees)), compared to other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)‘ divine star days.

***ErAr madhurakavi –*** he is – as said in ‘*avargaLaich chiriththiruppAr oruvar* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 409\]*’* (~ this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) who is always happy due to surrendering to [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) (a devotee), would be laughing at the other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who have surrendered to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) since they would be happy when [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) graces them and sad when [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) does not show up for them), such [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) is involved in AchArya abhimAnam (getting the love of AchAryan).

‘***Er***’ (beauty) for him is – ‘*AchAryavAn* \[chAndhOgya upanishath 6.14.2\]’ (one having the AchAryan only would understand the true entity), thus being the place of jewellery for the world. He is ‘*anbar adikku anbar* \[[gyAna sAram – 39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/04/gyana-saram-39-alagai-mulai-suvaitharkku/)\]’ (devotee of lotus feet of His devotees) isn’t it? As he is ‘*thilatham enath thirivAr* \[[gyAna sAram – 39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/04/gyana-saram-39-alagai-mulai-suvaitharkku/)\]’ (considers the devotees of krishnAn to be as holy as the thilakam that is smeared on one’s forehead), he is the devotee of ‘*jagathAbharaNar*’ (jewel that decorates the world) ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)), isn’t it?

‘**Er Ar’** is – having the completeness of: dependence on the will of AchAryan (AchArya parathanthran), such that [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) could also lead to that same nishtai (intent).

[![azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/azhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)*madhurakavi AzhvAr with nammAzhvAR – (dhEvap)perumAL kOyil (kAncheepuram)*

***ivvulagil vandhu udhiththa –*** such [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/), like how there is rise of aruNan before that of the sun, he incarnated before the sun that is *vakuLabhUshaNa bhAskarar* ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)).

**seerArum chiththiraiyil chiththirai nAL** *–* Since he having ‘*Er Ar*’ (complete beauty) incarnated, this day is also being ‘*seer Ar*’ (complete greatness). Since he is being SrImAn (having (true) wealth {AchArya abhimAnam}), the month of his incarnation also matched ‘*chaithra: SrImAn ayam mAsa:* (SrI rAmAyaNam – ayodhyA kANdam – 3.4\] (~this month of chiththirai is very best).

***seer Arum*** – can be applied as adjective for both the chiththirais {month and star day / or, as quoted in SrI rAmAyaNam above, and for [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)}.

As said in ‘*chiththA nakshathram bhavathi* \[thaiththirIya upanishath\]’ (chiththirai star day happened), this star day is celebrated by Sruthi as well.

This day is an important uthsavam day in kOyil (srIrangam) as *gajEndhra mOksham* (elephant) *(thiruvURal uthsavam).*

This [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) is a mahAthmA as said in ‘*periyavar seerai* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 18\]’ ([madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)’s qualities such as knowledge etc).

In this way, it is having the greatness that is not present for any other day – such star day.

***pArulagil maRRuLLa AzhvArgaL vandhu udhiththa nALgaLilum –*** In this world, as said in ‘*uNda pOdhu oru vArththaiyum uNNAtha pOdhu oru vArththaiyum solluvAr paththup pEr* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 408\] (other [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who have surrendered to [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) would be happy and praise Him and His related items when [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) graces them, and be sad and say the opposite about them when [emperumAn](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) does not show up for them) –

– compared to the months and days of incarnation of such ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/),

for removing the darkness in this world (*indha ulagil iruL neenga vandhu udhiththa mAdhangaL nALgaL* (upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 5\]) –

***uRRadhu emakku enRu nenjE Or*** – (the divine star day of incarnation of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)) is apt for our svarUpam (true nature) which is like ‘*madhurakavi soRpadiyE nilaiyAgap peRROm* \[Arththip prabandham – 55\] (have got the state of the words/ways of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) (doing service to AchAryan)). It is said ‘*uRRadhum un adiyArkku adimai* \[periya thirumozhi 8.10.3\] (~ (what I learned from thirumanthram is that I am a servant of your devotees).

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २६
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (ErAr madhurakavi)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-25/)

**pAsuram 26**

*vAyththa thirumanthiraththin maththimamAm padham pOl*  
*seerththa madhurakavi sey kalaiyai – Arththa pugazh*  
*AriyargaL thAngaL aruLichchyal naduvE*  
*sErviththAr thARpariyam thErndhu.* 26

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-26)

  
**Word by word meaning  **

*maththimam Am padham pOl* – Like the ‘nama’ word in the middle  
*thirumanthiranththin* – of thirumanthram  
*vAyththa* – that is corresponding to our true nature (svarUpa anurUpam),  
*madhurakavi* – [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)  
*seerththa* – who is full of greatness  
*sey* – divined  
*kalaiyai* – the prabandham that is [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/);  
*AriyargaL thAngaL* – [pUrvAcharyas (preceptors)](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)  
*Arththa* – (who are) full of  
*pugazh* – glory  
*thErndhu* – understood  
*thARpariyam* – its purpose/meaning/essence  
*sErviththAr* – and added it to be  
*aruLichcheyal naduvE* – in the center of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) divined by [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/).

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining with an example about how [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) who research about the meanings of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), had researched the greatness of meanings of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)’s [dhivya prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) and established it to be in the mid part of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) (when looking in the order of full recital of the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), with *‘vAiththa thirumanthiraththin maththimamAm padham pOl’.*

This thirumanthram ‘***vAyththa*’** is that it is complete in words and meanings, and so is according to our true nature. It is said too that ‘*Sarvam ashtAksharAnthassadham* \[hArItha smruthi – 3.45\]’ (everything is present in this thirumanthram that is of eight letters) – such is the greatness of thirumanthram.

As the etymology/origin for the word manthram is ‘*manthrAram thrAya ithi manthra:*’ (since it protects the one that deliberates on it, it is called manthram), thirumanthram uplifts from samsAram (life in the material world) those who inquire/deliberate on it. This is as divined in the divine saying (*aruLichcheydhu aruLi*) of ‘*samsAra nivarththakamAna periya thirumanthram* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam 315\]’. The same is said in ‘*sathyassamsAra nAsanam*’ (samsAram is destroyed immediately).

***maththimamAm padham pOl*** – Like the middle word which is present in it (thirumanthram) that is namas. That word (nama:) removes the hurdles regarding: svarUpam (true nature of self), upAyam (means), and purushArththam (goal), and tells us about what is svarUpam, upAyam, and purusArththam; also, as said in ‘*sidhdhE thadheeya sEshathvE sarvArththAs sambhavanthi hi*’ (by being servants of devotees all good are created isn’t it?), this manthram includes servitude to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s devotees. It is the meaning of this word that is according to our true nature.

This ([prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)) is also like this word (nama:) of thirumanthram.

Along the same lines, [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) too, as said in ‘*thadhiyAnAm akrEsara:*’ (is foremost among devotees) in relation to [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) (who is such a devotee), had divined about [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) as being the head, protector, true destiny, etc., in his prabandham that is [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/).

***seerththa madhurakavi sey kalaiyai*** – commendable prabandham [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) of this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/), which he said as ‘*madhurakavi sonna sol* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiruth-thambu-11-anban-thannai/)\]’ (~ words said by madhurakavi), ***sErviththAr*** – placed such prabandham (to be in the middle).

***seerththa madhurakavi –*** also says about him having the honor of not knowing any other master.

***seerththa sey kalaiyai –*** More than *prathama parvam* related (first state, i.e.,subservient to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), it is charama parvam related (last state, that is, subservient to AchAryan/devotee); such [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) would be having much greatness isn’t it? This [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) includes the greatness of holding the inner meaning of vEdhas as said in ‘*mikka vEdhiyar vEdhaththin uL poruL* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiru-thambu-8-arul-kondadum/)\]’ (inner meanings of vEdham recited by the learned vaidhikas). This [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) has got the greatness of ‘*avar pAsuram koNdu ivvarththam aRudhi idak kadavOm* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 409\]’ (shall show the meaning (of *charama parvam)* using the prabandham of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)).

Also, to the divine feet of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), [SrI nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) had repeated this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) 12000 times, and due to that [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s mind was soothed, and so all the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) became available, isn’t it? It is the greatness of this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) that that is attributed due to this too.

[![thiruppuLiyAzhwAr](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppuLiyAzhwAr.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thiruppuLiyAzhwAr.jpg)*thiruppuLi AzhvAr where nAthamunigaL recited kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu 12000 times*

In this way this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) which is having the greatness of conveying the inner meaning, that is [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)’s prabandham of [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/), they included this in the middle of beautiful [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

***Arththa pugazh AriyargaL thAngaL*** – [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) who follow the way of preceptors, determined the ways of [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) (being dependent on AchAryan), and they have the glory that came due to researching the meanings of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/);

***Arththa pugazh*** is ‘*Arndha pugazh’* similar to what is said in ‘*Arndha pugazh achchuthan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – 3.5.11\]’ (full of glory).

[![nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/nammazhwar-madhurakavi-nathamuni.jpg)*Acharyan nAthamunigaL with madhurakavi AzhvAr and nammAzhvAr*

Since this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) gives the meanings expressed in pathikams like ‘*payilum sudar oLi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3-7\]’, and ‘*nedumARku adimai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8-10\], the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) researched its greatness in meanings; like how when constructing a garland one would set a central gem store in the middle, due to which the whole garland would brighten up/become meaningful, they included [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) in the middle of other [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) such that those [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) became meaningful/useful.

This is like how the ‘*nama:*’ word in the middle brightens up the manthram, this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) being in the middle brightens up the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

Like how this [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)’s star day of incarnation, that is chiththirai month’s chiththirai star day is in the middle of thamizh months and is being bright among other months**,** [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) ‘s prabandham of [kaNNinun chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) is in the middle of [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)

and would enrich those other [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) too.

When considering this [prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) as equivalent to the middle word ‘*nama:*’ of thirumanthram, then it would be possible to think of all the [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) placed before this as giving the meaning of the word prior to *nama:* in thirumanthram *(praNavam)*, and [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) placed after this as giving the meaning of the word after *nama:* (that is, nArAyaNa).

To explain that, *‘vEdhaththukku Om ennum adhu pOl* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 19](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-19/)\] (like praNavam for vEdham) starting from [*thiruppallANdu*](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) up to the prabandham before [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) are of the meaning of praNavam, *[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/)* standing for the meaning of *nama:,* and after that, starting from ‘*nArAyaNA ennum nAmam* \[periya thirumozhi 1.1\]’, till the thirumadals that include ‘*nArAyaNa O maNivaNNa nAgaNaiyAy vArAy en Ar idarai neekkAi’* are of the meaning of *‘nArAyaNa’,* and of the meaning of ‘*Aya*’ of thirumanthram, which signifies that which is related to kainkaryam.

chiththirai month’s chiththirai star day is the incarnation day of [thirumalai ananthAzhvAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/31/ananthazhwan/) too who is a follower of the words of AchAryan, isn’t it? That is why he got the dhAsya name of madhurakavi dhAsan.

– – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २७
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (vAiththa thirumanthiraththin)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-26/)

**pAsuram 27**

*inRu ulageer chiththiraiyil Eyndha thiruvAdhirai nAL*  
*enRaiyinum inRu idhanukku ERRam en thAn – enRavarkkuch*  
*chARRuginREn kENmin ethirAsar tham piRappAl*  
*nARRisaiyum koNdAdum nAL.
27*

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-27)

**Word by word meaning**

*ulagIr* – Oh the people in this world!  
*inRu* – today is  
Eyntha – a day aptly set  
*chiththiraiyil* – in the month of chiththirai (chaithra)  
*thiruvAdhirai nAL* – and of star day thiruvAdhirai (ArdhrA).  
*enRavarkku* – For those who asked  
*en thAn* – what could be  
*ERRam* – the greatness  
*inRu ithanukku* – of today’s day  
*enRaiyinum* – compared to any other day,  
*saRRuginREn* – I am saying  
*kEL(N)min* – (so) listen;  
that is,  
*nAL* – it is the day  
*nAl thisaiyum* – that those in all four directions  
*koNdAdum* – celebrate  
*ethirAsar tham* – [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s  
*piRappAl* – divine incarnation.

**vyAkyAnam**

Now starting with this pAsuram, he ([maNavALA mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines in three pAsurams about he who is having the greatness distinct from [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), who is their servant, and who is the head of the others, that is [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/); in this pAsuram, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is mercifully conveying in the form of question and answer about the greatness of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine incarnation day of chiththirai (chaithra) month’s thiruvAdhirai (ArdhrA) star day.

***inRu ulageer chiththiraiyil Eyntha thiruvAdhirai nAL*** – [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) too, like [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), for everyone in the world to reach the true goal, is addressing them as ‘*inRu ulageer*’. {recall [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s great thirukkOshtiyUr incident}.

Like said in ‘*chaithra: SrimAn ayam mAsa:* \[SrI rAmAyaNam – ayOdhyA kANdam – 3.4\]’ (this chiththirai month is accepted/nurtured by everyone).

***inRu* –** saying this shows that its greatness is of importance to him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)).

***chiththiraiyil Eyntha thiruvAdhirai nAL*** – The thiruvAdhirai star day in chiththirai month is the time that when [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) incarnated, it could pour flowers and to indicate good times ahead.

***Eyntha thiruvAdhirai –*** thiruvAdhirai that goes well with our svarUpam (true nature). It is such a great month and star day, and it is available for us! perumAL who is SrImAn that is rAman incarnated in this SrImAn month (month having such wealth), and perumAL’s star day is close to [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s star day. He ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) too is referred to as ‘*seemAn iLaiyAzhvAr* \[[emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) nAL pAttu – verse which glorifies the day of his birth\]’. [SrI rAma](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and [rAmanuja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) got the divine star days that are before and after, as thiruvAdhirai and punarpUsam.

In these ways this star day is being wonderful compared to other days, is the answer to those who asked what is great about this day. Based on that, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is saying ‘*sARRuginRen*’ (I shall tell you).

***sARRuginREn*** – Whether you would appreciate it or not, I will do my duty. For [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/)’s victory SrI jAmbavAn, mAhArAjar (sugreevan) were sounding the drums; in the same way I ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) am sounding the drum and letting it be known in all the worlds about the divine star day of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is ‘*vAmanan seelan* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 40\]’ (having greatness equal to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who took vAmana avathAram {who spanned all the worlds}).

***kENmin*** – Listen to [this devotee](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s words without fail. No need to come closer, fall at the divine feet, and listen in privacy; just listen with your ears open from wherever you are, that is all.

When asked – If so, can you not convey the secret of the incarnation? He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) says ***ethirAsar tham piRappAl.*** Since it is the incarnation of the head of yathis (mendicants), it would be celebrated by the learned in all four directions.

**pUrvAchAryas divined the use of general term ‘thiru nakshathram’ to imply the star day of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).**

***ethirAsar tham piRappu*** – This incarnation of yathi kula nAthan (head of yathis, that is, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) is having more greatness even than yadhu kula nAthan (head of cowherds) that is [krishNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)’s incarnation. For that incarnation the use was to sit on the chariot and explain everything to one person that is arjuna to make him get clarity. The use of this incarnation is for getting those in the whole world to get to the true destiny by him saying a few words.

[![emperumanar_with_sishyas](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/emperumanar_with_sishyas-1024x768.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/emperumanar_with_sishyas.jpg)*emperumAnAr with Sishyas*

Now he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is showing to all directions about those who have understood the greatness of and cherish this incarnation day.

***nAl thisaiyum koNdAdum nAL*** – As he is having the greatness as said in ‘*thisai anaiththum ERum kuNanai* \[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 46\]’ (having divine qualities that have spread in all directions), and ‘*thikku uRRa keerththi rAmAnusanai* \[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 26\]’ (emperumAnAr having complete fame in all directions), [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)‘s divine star day would also be protected from all sides.

{It is to be noticed that in [rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) it is said that emperumAnAr’s greatness is known by people in all directions, and maNavALa mAmunigaL has used a matching phrase of ‘*nAl thisaiyum koNdAdum*‘ here, and the vyAkyAtha (commentator) piLLai lOkam jIyar of this pAsuram has unearthed this connection for us }

Those in these directions are all having the connection with [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). So there is no place where there is no connection with [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). So understand that this is celebrated by everyone, and you also nurture this, is the theme (of this pAsuram).

– – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २८
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (inRulageer chiththiraiyil)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-27/)

**pAsuram 28**

*AzhvArgaL thANgaL avathariththa nALgaLilum*  
*vAzhvAna nAL namakku maNNulageer – Ezh pArum*  
*uyya ethirAsar udhiththaruLum chiththiraiyil*  
*seyya thiruvAdhirai*
28

[pAsuram 28](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-28)

**Word by word meaning**

*nALgaLilum* – Compared to the divine star days  
*AzhvArgaL thAngaL* – in which all the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*avathariththa* – graced their incarnation,  
*maNNulageer* – Oh those in this earth!  
*namakku* – for us,  
*vAzhvAna* – that can give us true life  
*nAL* – is the divine star day  
*ethirAsar* – (in which) [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
*udhiththu aruLum* – graces by incarnating  
*chiththiraiyil* – in the month of chiththirai (chaithra),  
*seyya* – in the beautiful  
*thiruvAdhirai* – star day of thiruvAdhirai (ArdhrA),  
*Ezh pArum* – for those in all the seven worlds  
*uyya* – to attain true goal.

**vyAkyAnam**

For all the people in the world to attain true goal, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) graced his incarnation; such divine star day is a huge wealth compared to the divine star days and months of all [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), for all kinds of people to know.

***AzhvArgaL thAngaL avathariththa nALgaLilum*** – Having the quality of being given unblemished knowledge (*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1\]](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)) by [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), due to which through their [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) they were able to correct the village, country, and the world; that is, they had incarnated to help the world.

Compared to such divine days of their incarnations,

***vAzhvAna nAL namakku maN ulageer*** – (better day for us, Oh the people of this earth) – that is, as said in ‘*mangaiyarALi parAnkusa munnavar vAzhvu muLaiththidu nAL* \[Arththi prabandham – 32\]’, the day of incarnation of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) helps enrich those of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), so it would be a more important day for us for us to attain true nature and proper being;

Or,

***vAzhvAna nAL namakku maN ulageer* –** Unlike you (the people of the earth) who are after material wealth etc., and who would be away from this (star day?), we who consider them as immaterial (like giving no importance like how one would ignore some grass), and have surrendered to [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s divine feet *(rAmAnuja padhAmboja samASrayaNa SAlina:)*, and saying ‘*thanthai nal thAy thAram thanayar perum selvam en thanakku neeyE ethirAsA* \[Arththi prabandham – 3\]’ (Father, good mother, wife, brothers, huge wealth is all you for me [ethirAsA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)), we consider him as all the wealth, so the divine star day of his incarnation also is a big wealth for us.

That is, instead of it (the day) being the *reason* for our true living, it in itself is our true living.

***maN ulageer*** – As said in ‘*AvirabhUdhbhUmau* \[varavaramuni mukthakam – 6\]’ (appeared on the earth), and the same is said in ‘*maNNin thalaththu udhiththu* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 95\]’, Oh the people of this earth who have born in the world where such [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) incarnated – you are having such a fortune! You also be considering this always as your true life.

Now, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining what this day is, as ‘***Ezh pArum uyya ethirAsar udhiththu aruLum chiththiraiyil seyya thiruvAdhirai’.***

That is, as said in ‘*uNmai nal gyAnam uraiththa* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 73\]’ (emperumAnAr who preaches the true knowledge), due to his advice/preaching and giving knowledge, those in all the worlds became true being, and reached the true goal – such [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is the head of yathis, divined his incarnation in chiththirai month and beautiful thiruvAdhirai. So –

***vAzhvAna nAL namakku maNNulageer Ezh pArum uyya*** – here ‘*pAr’* being earth, and ‘*Ezh pAr’* being earth that is the head of seven dhvIpams (islands). By this, it thinks about all the worlds. Like said in ‘*anaiththulagum vAzhap piRantha* \[Arththip prabandham – 41\] (~born for all the worlds to live the true one).

People of all the worlds getting the true life due to his incarnation is: as said in ‘*thadhuparyapi bAdharAyaNas sambhavAth* \[SrI bashyam 1.3-25\]’ (after this it becomes/happens like this, says bAdharAyaNa), which implies that worship of brahmam happens in the other worlds as well, and any doubts in sAsthras which mandates such things are cleared very well by [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) through SrI bAshyam, as said in ‘*thaththuva nUl kUzh aRRadhu* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 65\]*’* (SAsthras that convey the truth in existence became clear of doubts and were able to convey the correct meanings), and so they learned without any doubts and got the true life.

Even though this is for matters related to those in the earth, it also helps those in the divine worlds.

When he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) had divined his visit to SAradha peetam, sarasvathi had asked him about her doubts and got them clarified, and as said in ‘*sankai keduththu ANda thavarAsA* \[periya thirumozhi thaniyan (related to [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/))\]’ (~ clarified the doubts and ruled us), she celebrated him, showed the grantham ‘*bhOdhAyana vruththi*’, and later when SrI bAshayam grantham was graced to her she had kept SrI bAshayam on her head, is all well known isn’t it?

If all learned sarasvathi who is the wife of brahmA who is the head of all the dhEvas and who lives in sathya lOkam, would do something like this, then it goes without saying that those in all the worlds also would also celebrate this.

Or, as said in ‘*sa bhrAthuch charaNau gAd(h)am nipIdya raghunandhana: \| sIthA muvAchAthiyasA rAghavancha mahAvratham* \[SrI rAmAyaNam ayOdhyA kANdam 31.2\]’ (famed and key of clan of raghu, that is iLaiyaperumAL (lakshmANan), fell fully at his elder brother’s feet, holding them by both hands, in the presence of [sIthA pirAtti](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/), pleaded as follows to [SrI rAma](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) who is staunch in accepting refuge and saving them), and so the head of nithya sUris that is iLaiyaperumAL (lakshmaNan) had started as a request for doing kainkaryam (service)

– such ways was followed as it is by his reincarnation that is [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), as he said ‘*SrIman! nArAyaNa! thava charNAravendhayugaLam saraNamaham prapadhyE* \[gadhya thrayam – srIranga gadhyam\]’ (Oh periyA pirAtti accompanied nArAyaNa! I am strongly accepting your divine lotus feet as the means), and followed his (lakshmaNa’s) ways; and not stopping there, he divined it through SrI gadhyam that is gadhya thrayam, for others to follow such ways. Isn’t this the proper way for helping all the worlds to reach true goal?

***Ezh pArum uyya ethirAsar udhiththaruLum*** – By the appearance of mere sun of this world, outer darkness of physical world goes away. [rAmAnujar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) is one who possesses the light that is knowledge – due to such sun’s appearance all the worlds’ darkness (ignorance) is destroyed, as said in ‘*ulagiruL neenga* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 9](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-9/)\], and ‘*sarvalOka thamOhanthA*’ (removed darkness of all the worlds).

[![emperumAnAr_thondanUr_0001](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/emperumAnAr_thondanUr_0001.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/emperumAnAr_thondanUr_0001.jpg)*emperumAnAr and his disciples*

It is said ‘*arka: svakara samparkAth dhivA hanthi bhahisthama: \|
santhasthu dharsanA dhEva bhahiranthardhivAnisam*’ (~sun, by its rays, removes outer darkness during the day. Saints, by just the sight remove inner darkness as well), and ‘*nikhilakumathimAyA sarvareebAlasUrya:* \[yathirAja sapthathi\]’ (after night which gives all wrongs to mind, young sun that appears when it dawns).

In \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/)– 49\] starting from ‘*Anadhu semmai’* which ends with ‘*irAmAnusan ith thalaththu udhiththE*’, the great happenings due to [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s appearance can be seen in its meanings.

***ethirAsar udhiththu aruLum chiththiraiyil seyya thiruvAdhirai*** – Like the sun entering the ArdhrA (thiruvAdhirai) star, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) too appeared in ArdhrA (thiruvAdhirai). It is the time when crops are set; here too the crop that is [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/) got the brightness set for their true knowledge. Like said in ‘*AdhithyAjjAyathE vrushti:* \[brahma purANam 29.4\]’ (Sun instigates rain), here too there is rain of krupai (by this sun).

*{vyAkyAnam for this pAsuram is longer than for earlier ones. Perhaps the vyAkyAtha (commentator) piLLailOkam jIyar too has rained more special meanings to this pAsuram for us}*

***chiththiraiyil seyya thiruvAdhirai –*** In the month of chiththirai when flowers blossom is the time when he incarnated in the beautiful thiruvAdhirai star. The beauty for it is based on the incarnation of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is ‘*azhagArum ethirAsar* \[Arththi prabandham – 31\]*’*.

***‘seyyA’ thiruvAdhirai –*** Based on the incarnation of SrImAn ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) who is of reddish hue, this thiruvAdhirai is also reddish. Like said in ‘*subhaga: SrImAn*’, his nature is also like reddish sun.

[thirukkachchi nambi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirukkachi-nambi/) also divined ‘*sivandhu valiya nediyarAy* \[guruparamparai\]*’* (reddish, strong and tall (description of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/))).

– – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – २९
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvArgaL thAngaL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-28/)

**pAsuram 29**

*enthai ethirAsar ivvulagil enthamakkA*  
*vandhu udhiththa nAL ennum vAsiyinAl – indhath*  
*thiruvAdhirai thannin seermai thanai nenjE*  
*oruvAmal eppozhudum Or
*29

[pAsuram 29](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-29)

**Word by word meaning**

enthai – Our swAmi  
ethirAsar – rAmAnujar  
vandhu udhiththa – descended and divined his incarnation  
nAL ennum – in this divine star day  
ivvulagil – in this world  
em thamakkA – for us,  
vAsiyinAl – due to such excellence (of this day)  
nenjE – oh mind!  
Or – know about it  
eppozhudum – at all times  
oruvAmal – without fail  
seermai thannai – (about the) greatness of  
intha – this  
thiruvAdhirai thannin – thiruvAdhirai star day. (ArdhrA)

**vyAkyAnam**

By the previous two pAsurams he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) had divined his advise to all sentient about the greatness of this star day (of [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)); in this pAsuram, more than them unexpectedly his mind had reformed, (*munthuRRa nenju* \[thaniyan for periya thiruvanthAdhi divined by [emperumAnAr](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)\]), so toward such mind he is divining his advise to always think about this star day in its heart, starting this with ‘*enthai ethirAsar’.*

***enthai ethirAsar* –** [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) the head of yathis, who is the reason for our true being and growth;

***ivvulagil*** – birth in this world that even samsAris (those who are attached to material world) hate and wish to leave from.

***enthamakkA vandhu udhiththa*** – due to the relationship as ‘*enthai*’, he came and incarnated in this world for us.

***enthamakkA –*** there is no other reason for him to incarnate in this ‘*kodu ulagam* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.9.7\]*’* (dire world). He came only to save us, as said in *‘mAyum en Aviyai vandhu eduththAn* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 42\]’ (through causeless mercy he pulled my AthmA out of here where it was losing to material desires). As said in ‘*irAmAnusan ippadiyil piRandhadhu maRRillai kAraNam pArththidilE* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 51\]’ (there is no other reason for emperumAnAr to incarnate here (other than to save me out of here)), is how it is for him.

{ emperumAnAr also incarnated to *rescue* chelvap piLLai (emperumAn’s vigraham) from the north and re-establish him at mElkotE (thirunArAyaNapuram) }

pAsuram starting with ‘*kUbaththil vIzhum kuzhaviyudan kuthiththu*’ and ending with ‘*ethirAsAr thAn piRakkum ennai uyppadhA* \[Arththip prabandham – 9\] (~ With the child that fell into a well, its mother too would jump in to save it from that danger. In the same way, even if I am born here due to karmas, my [yathirAja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) would be born here to save me out of it) , and ‘*enthai ethirAsarar emmai eduththu aLikka vandha*’ (~ [ethirAsar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) has come here to save us out of this material world). This is how [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) had said about this.

***enthamakkA vandhu udhiththa nAL ennum vAsiyinAl –*** For our ever dark dangerous hell that is samsAram, he incarnated to show the light, so it is of such greatness. This is as said in ‘*viNNin thalaininRum veedaLippAn* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 95\]’ (from SrIvaikuNtam, for bestowing mOksham (liberation from material world)), ‘*maNNin thalaththu udhiththu* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 95\]’ (he incarnated in to this world).

***indhath thiruvAdhirai thannin seermai thannai*** – Being the reason for incarnation of ananthAzhAn (?), and having the greatness as said in ‘S*ankara bhAskara* \[Arththi prabandham – 32\]’ (how [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) defeated other philosophies, etc), this is having the greatness and eminence that is talked about in this and other places.

[![emperumAnAr_mElkote](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/emperumAnAr_mElkote.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/emperumAnAr_mElkote.jpg)*emperumAnAr – mElkOtE (thirunArAyaNapuram)*

***nenjE oruvAmal eppozhudum Or*** – Oh mind which is the instrument for reflecting upon this great day that incarnated for thinking about itself. In this way, be thinking about it at all times without any break;

***indhath thiruvAdhirai*** – (‘this’ thiruvAdhirai) – The way his ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s) involvement in this is.

By this, as said in ‘*AchAryam samsmarEth sadhA*’ (should always think about AchAryan), the day of incarnation too is of interest for him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) to be thinking about at all times. The reason for that is his ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s) remembrance of his ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s) help (of getting us out of samsAram) *(upakAra smruthi)*, isn’t it?

– – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३०
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (enthai ethirAsar)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-29/)

**pAsuram 30  **
