*eNNarum seerp poigai munnOr ivvulagil thOnRiya Ur*  
*vaNmai migu kachchi mallai mAmayilai – maNNiyil neer*  
*thEngum kuRaiyalUr seerk kaliyan thOnRiya Ur*  
*Ongum uRaiyUr pANan Ur*
30

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-30)

**Word by word meaning**

*seer* – greatness  
eNNa arum *–* that is hard to fully count/comprehend; (such)  
*poigai munnOr* – [poigai AzhvAr, bhUthaththAzhvAr, pEyAzhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/)  
*thOnRiya* – divined their incarnations  
*ivvulagil* – in this world  
*vaNmai migu* – bountiful / generous  
*Ur* – cities / places of  
*kachchi* – thirukkachchi (kAncheepuram)  
*mallai* – thirukkadanmallai (thiruk kadal mallai)  
*mA mayilai* – and great thiru mayilai (mylApore / thiruvallikkENi)  
(respectively).  
*seer* – Great  
*kaliyan* – [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/)  
*thOnRiya* – divined his incarnation  
*Ur* – in the city / place, (where)  
*maNNiyil – river maNNi*  
*thEngum* – is full of  
*neer* – water, (that is),  
*kuRaiyalUr* – thiruk kuRaiyalUr.  
*pANan* – [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/) (divined his incarnation in the)  
*Ur* – city / place of  
*uRaiyUr* – thiru uRaiyUr.

**vyAkyAnam**

Starting with ‘*anthamizhAl naRkalaigaL Ayndhu uraiththa AzhvArgaL* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-5/)\]’, till now, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) explained in detail for everyone to know, about the divine name, month and star day of divine incarnation of AzhvArs, and their divine prabandhams as said in ‘*vAzhvAna thirumozhigaL’*.

After this, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divined in his mind that since AzhvArs’ places of incarnation are also of importance to us similar to ayOdhyA, mathurA, etc., [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) starts to divine about them through four pAsurams; in this first one of that series, starting with [poigaiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/), [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is divining about five of the AzhvArs’ divine places of incarnation, starting the pAsuram with ‘*eNNarum seer’.*

That is, the first three AzhvArs, that is [mudhalAzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/), whose auspicious qualities could not be counted / comprehended as said in ‘*eN il thol pugazh* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.3.3\]’ (~
([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) having uncountable greatness). He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is showing that these are the places in which incarnations were divined by [such AzhvArs](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) whose qualities are of big uncountable groups, saying – ***vaNmai migu kachchi mallai mA maiyilai*** –

That is, big cities like kachchi (kAncheepuram), etc., are the aforementioned three AzhvArs’ places of incarnation.

*vaNmai* (bountiful / prosperity) for kachchi is – as said in ‘*niRaindha seermai neeL kachchi* \[periya thirumozhi – 2.9\]’ (~ kachchi with full of greatness), it is filled with dhivya dhESams, and is also beautiful having decorations of a city as said in ‘*azhagAya kachchi* \[periya thirumozhi 2.9.1\]’ (beautiful kachchi). It is to be said as ‘*ninRan irundhAn kidandhAn* \[periya thirumozhi 2.4.1\]’ (standing, sitting, and lying poses of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), and ‘*idhuvanRO manRAr pozhiR kachchi mANbu’*.

Or, the greatness of helping the samsAris to have true life by seeing the [sarvESvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) lying down in kachchi [vekkA](http://thiruvekka.koyil.org), and see [poigai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) who came and rose (incarnated) in kachchi.

***mallai –*** After saying ‘*mallai kachchik kidandhavan Ur* \[periya thirumozhi 2.6.5\], he said ‘kadal mallaith thala sayanam \[periya thirumozhi 2.6.6.\]’ (~ thirukkadal mallai dhivya dhESam, with sthala sayana perumAL), isn’t it? So kadal mallai that is equal to kachchi. It is said as ‘*vangaththAl mAmaNi vandhu udhu munneer mallaiyAy!* \[thirunedunthANdakam – 9\]’ (~ thirukkadal mallai dhivya dhEsam where priceless gems are washed to the shore by the sea of boats/ships). This place is having priceless jeevAthmA and Isvaran, isn’t it?

That is, it is having both [bhuthaththAzvhAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) as said in ‘*seethaththAr muththukkaL sErum kadal mallai bhUthathAr* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi thaniyan\]’ ((with the inner meaning of) [bhUthaththAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) the priceless pearl of thirukkadal mallai), and the [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) as said in ‘*kadal mallaith thala sayanaththu uRaivAr* \[periya thirumozhi 2.6.1\] (~ sthala sayana perumAL in lying position at thirukkadal mallai)’.

***mA mayilai –*** As said in ‘*neeLOdham vandhalaikkum mA mayilai* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 35\] (~ great city of mayilai where the waves rush to gently touch the feet of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))’, it is suitable for [pEyAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/22/mudhalazhwargal/) to come and incarnate in this place that is a big city. Same is said in ‘*vandhu udhaiththa veN thirigaL* \[mUnRam thiruvanthAdhi – 16\], etc. That (place) is also being in the same (great) way.

[![mudhalAzhvargaL](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhalAzhvargaL.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/mudhalAzhvargaL.jpg)*mudhalAzhvArs*

***seerk kaliyan thOnRiya Ur maNNiyil neer thEngum kuRaiyalUr*** – That is, as said in ‘*koNda seerth thoNdan* \[periya thirumozhi 8.10.10\]’, having auspicious qualities like gyAnam (knowledge), bhakthi (devotion), etc., and due to that, as said in ‘*arumpeRal anbu pukkittu adimai pUNdu uyndhu* \[thirunedunthANdakam – 5\]’, having the wealth of kainkaryam (subservience) through speech and body – such [thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/).

Or, ‘*seerk kaliyan’* to call as [kaliyan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) (having strength) as he grabbed the ring from divine feet, and other things like anguLiyam, dresses, jewels, and then stole His whole wealth that is thirumanthram – such greatness.

It is said, ‘*avaLukkuth thiruvadigaL koduththa thiruvAzhi modhirathO pAdhi ivanukku AchAryan prasAdhiththa thirumanthramum’.* (Like the ring that thiruvadi (hanuman) gave to seetha pirAtti, Acharyan has divined him (us) the thirumanthram).

[![kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar (Large)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large-1024x680.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kaliyan_uthsavam_thiruvali_thirunagari_thirumangai_azhvar-Large.jpg)*thirumangai AzhvAr at thiruvAli thirunagari*

[AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) having such divine wealth, and his place of birth is having the wealth of water in the rivers similar to that in thirunagari, as said in ‘*pongu punal maNNi* \[periya thirumozhi 4.1.4, and iyal sARRu\]*’* (Rich water resources of maNNi river).

Due to this wealth it is said ‘*kali mikka sennel kazhani* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 88\]’ (paddies with bustling and rich grains). This is also like ‘*kali vayal thennan kurugUr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 5.2.11\]’ (paddy fields of [AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/) that are constantly planted and reaped).

That thirukkuRaiyalUr is such that it can be said as a part of thirunagari (in wealth of water, paddy fields, etc).

***kuRaiyalUr seerk kaliyan thOnRiya Ur, Ongum uRaiyUr pANan Ur*** *–* There is togetherness of month and star days for them (both AzhvArs ([thirumangai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/23/thirumangai-azhwar/) and [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/)) incarnated in the month of kArththigai, and star days of kArththigai and rOhiNi).

***pANan Ur Ongum uRaiyUr* –** Eminence of uRaiyUr is – due to the incarnation of him who is in the clan that is eminent due to being amicable to subservience.

{ SrIvachana bhUshaNam explains that those in the last varNams naturally have subservience and so it is a great birth – *naichyam janma sidhdham; AgaiyAl uthkrushta janmamE srEshtam* – 216,217}

Also, as said in ‘*kOzhiyum kUdalum kOyil koNda kOvalar* \[periya thirumozhi 9.2.5\]’ ( ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) like a gOpalakrishNan who is having the place of stay as uRaiyUr, and kUdal (then madhurai)), [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) is happily present in this dhivyadEsam (uRaiyUr), and with [pirAtti](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) being identified with the name of the dhivyadhEsam as *‘thiruvAzh uRanthai’,* and *‘uRaiyUr valliyAr’*, as this is the place of her birth – the greatness due to these, for uRaiyUr.

So it says that the place having such greatness is the avathAra sthalam (place of incarnation) of [thiruppANAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/21/thiruppanazhwar/).

[![thiruppANAzhwar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/thiruppANAzhwar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/thiruppANAzhwar.jpg)*thiruppANAzhvAr – uRaiyUr*

This (uRaiyUr) is the area (thuRai) that is opposite to ‘*thirumugath thuRai’* ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s usual place of bathing (guruparamparA prabhAvam – page 262\]); so a place suitable to have mutual reciprocation between bhagavAn and his devotees due to the emperumAnAr’s relationship in this place *(edhir vizhi kodukkaikku pAngAna dhESam AyiRRu)*.

– – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३१
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (eNNarum seerp poygai munnOr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-30/)

**pAsuram 31  **

*thoNdaradip podiyAr thOnRiya Ur thol pugazh sEr*  
*maNdangudi enbar maNNulagil – eN thisaiyum*  
*Eththum kulasEkaran Ur ena uraippar*  
*vAyththa thiruvanchikkaLam*
31

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-31)

**Word by word meaning**

*maNNulagil –* In the earth,  
*thOnRiya Ur* – the city of incarnation (of)  
*thoNdaradippodiyAr* – [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)  
*thol* – (is the) ancient  
*maNdankudi* – thirumaNdangudi city  
*sEr* – (which is) having  
*pugazh* – greatness,  
*enbar* – say the learned ones;  
*eN thisaiyum* – those in all the eight directions  
*Eththum* – revere (the)  
*kulasEkaran Ur* – city of incarnation of [kulasEkarAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)  
*vAiththa* – (which is) suitable for the svarUpam (true nature)  
*thiru* – (is the) beautiful  
*vanjikkaLam* – city named vanjikkaLam,  
*enRu uraippar* – say the learned ones.

**vyAkyAnam**

In this pAsuram, he is divining about [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/)’s and [kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s places of incarnations.

***thoNdaraip podiyAr thOnRiya Ur thol pugazh sEr maNdangkudi enbar maNNulagil*** – In this earth the place of incarnation of [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) is ‘*thol pugazh sEr maNdangudi enbar’ –* thirumandangudi which is having natural greatness and suitable, is the place of incarnation of [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) who is an expert of the vEdhas, say the learned ones. Staunch vaidhikas who nurture that greatness of (his) incarnation would be according to ‘*maNdangudi enbar mAmaRaiyOr thoNdaradippodi thonnagaram* \[thiruppaLLiezhuchchi thaniyan\] ’ (same meaning as this phrase).

Since it is an ancient city, it has got well established greatness. Also this is very close to thiruppuLLam bhUthangudi dhivyadhEsam isn’t it?

[![Mandangudi Thondaradipodi Azhwar-003](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mandangudi-Thondaradipodi-Azhwar-003-768x1024.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mandangudi-Thondaradipodi-Azhwar-003.jpg)*thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr with his flower basket, at thirumandankudi*

***eN thisaiyum Eththum kulasEkaran Ur ena uraippar vAyththa thiruvanjikkaLam* –** His ([kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/)’s) bhakthi (devotion) towards [bhagavAn](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) and bhAgavathas (devotees) is such that it is revered by everyone in all the eight directions; such [kulasEkarap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) who is ‘*mudi vEndhar SikAmaNi* \[perumAL thirumozhi thaniyan\]’ (crest jewel on the heads of the emperors) incarnated in the place of thiruvanjikkaLam which is a suitable one.

[![kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/kulasekarazhvar_thiruvanjikkalam_2012_DSC01809.jpg)*kulasEkarap perumAL as divining from thiruvanjikkaLam*

*vAyththa* – coming together.

This is in *kEraLa* *dhESam*, under the name of *nisuLA* which is a big city. This is near what is presently called as *thiruviththuvakkOdu* that is the dhivya dhESam of thiruviRRuvakkOdu.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३२
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (thoNdaradippodiyAr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-31/)

**pAsuram 32  **

*mannu thirumazhisai mAdath thiruk kurugUr*  
*minnu pugazh villipuththUr mEdhiniyil – nanneRiyOr*  
*Eyndha paththi sArar ezhil mARan pattar pirAn*  
*vAyndhu udhiththa UrgaL vagai*
32

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-32)

**Word by word meaning**

*mEdhiniyil* – In the world  
*nal neRiyOr* – those in good AchAryAbhimAna nishtai (having AchAryan as everything)  
*Eyndha* – being together (for)  
*paththisArar* – [thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/),  
*ezhil* – beautiful  
*mARan* – [nammazhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), and  
*pattar pirAn* – [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html),  
*vagai* – detail  
*UrgaL* – of the places  
*udhiththa* – they incarnated  
*vAyndhu* – as a group, are:  
*mannu* – the well established  
*thirumazhisai* – [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/), and  
*mAdam* – having belvederes/balconies (*mAdangaL*)  
*thirukkurugUr* – (that is) thirukkurugUr ([AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/)), and  
*minnu* – (having) shining  
*pugazh* – greatness (that is,)  
*villipuththUr* – [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/)  
(respectively).

**vyAkyAnam**

***mannu thirumazhisai etc. –*** In this pAsuram he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining that these are the places of incarnation of [thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/), and of [thirukkurugUr](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org) kArimARan that is, [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), and of [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/) pattar pirAn, that is, [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

***mannu thirumazhisai –*** (In this pAsuram) as he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining the places of incarnation in the same order as their months of incarnation, even though (in the previous pAsuram) after thirumaNdangudi (of [thoNdaradippodi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/08/thondaradippodi-azhwar/) who incarnated in the month of mArgazhi) [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) had not divined about thirumazhisai ([thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/)’s incarnation being next to *mArgazhi* that is the month of *thai*) (instead in that previous pAsuram he had divined next at that time about thiruvanjikkaLam of [kulasEkara AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/18/kulasekara-azhwar/) related to *mAsi* month that comes after *thai*), but here it is to be noted that the ones given are in a sequence.

Or, it can be taken in this way: as he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) had divined earlier as ‘*pugazh mazhisai ayyan aruL mARan* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-4/)\]*’* (where, after [thirumazhisai Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/), mARan that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) was mentioned for the order of incarnation) – for that togetherness also, (here [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is mentioning them one after the other).

***mannu thirumazhisai –*** This place is having the ever-present relationship of [SrI jagannAthar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and ([thirumazhisai) AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/), and is being *[mahIsAra kshEthram](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org)* thus making the earth lighter – such [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/). (as when rishis wanted to know a place where they could do their penances etc., and when [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/) was placed in one plate and rest of the places was placed in another plate in the balance, the other places were lighter compared to [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/), so [thirumazhisai](http://thirumazhisai.koyil.org/) was the chosen place for them).

This is south of [thiruninRavUr](http://thiruninravur.koyil.org), and near to that place.

[![thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited.png)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/thirumazhisai_azhvar_at_thirumazhisai_edited.png)*thirumazhisai AzhvAr – thirumazhisai*

***mAdath thirukkurugUr*** – As said in *‘mAda mALigai sUzhndhu azhagAya thirukkurugUr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.4.11\]’ (beautiful [thirukkurugUr](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org) that surrounds us with palatial galleries), having the decorations and setup as a beautiful city of [(AzhvAr) thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org).

[![nammazhvar_bavishyadhAchar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/nammazhvar_bavishyadhAchar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/nammazhvar_bavishyadhAchar.jpg)*nammAzhvAr with nAthamunigaL*

***minnu pugazh villipuththUr –*** that is – since ‘*pArAr thol pugazhAn pattar pirAn* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 2.3.13\]’ divined his incarnation here, [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/) is having bright (significant) greatness in all directions;

[![srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srI_periyAzhvAr_aani_brahmothsavam_2013_arulalaperumal.tripod.com_.jpg)*periyAzhvAr*

***medhiniyil*** – in the world. As said in *‘SrInagaryAm mahApuryAm thAmraparaNi uththarE thadE* \| SrIthintriNI mUladhAmnE SatakOpAya mangaLam*’* (we prostrate to satakOpar ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) under the tamarind tree in thirunagari ([AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org/))situated on the northern banks of river thAmraparaNi), these are the kind of places where these ‘*SrImAn*’s incarnated;

If asking who they are –

***nanneRiyOr Eyndha paththi sArar –*** (followed by those having good ways) – ‘*nanneRi*’ (good ways) is – AchArya abhimAnam – that is, steadfast in those ways, [thirumazhisai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) is followed lovingly by those like kaNikaNNar and perumpuliyUr adigaL who have surrendered to the AzhvAr who knows the correct path.

In this way, it is paththi sArar (bhakthi sAra), that is, [thirumazhisaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/16/thirumazhisai-azhwar/) who is worshiped by these ananya prayOjanars (not expecting any benefit other than AchAryan);

Or ‘*nanneRiyOr’* could also be applied to the mentioned list of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/). Then it would be (kaNikaNNar, perumpuliyUr adigaL, and) [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html) and[ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) (respectively). It is they who worshiped in fitting ways to the counterpart (AchAryan?) like proper disciples.

***ezhil mARan*** – ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) – It is – jagadhAbharaNar that is vakuLabharaNar. *ezhil* – beauty

***pattar pirAn –*** SrI bhatta nAthar – that is [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html).

These three AzhvArs are such that it is very difficult/rare to get them in this earth, and they incarnated for the protection of the sentient, and this is the detail of the places of their incarnation.

These places are in the west, north, and south of SrIrangam which is in the east.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३३
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mannu thirumazhisai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-32/)

**pAsuram 33  **

*seerArum villipuththUr selvath thirukkOLUr*  
*ErAr perumbUthUr ennum ivai – pAril*  
*madhiyArum ANdAL madhurakavi AzhvAr*  
*ethirAsar thOnRiya Ur ingu* 33

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-33)

**Word by word meaning**

*Arum* – having *(porundhiya)*  
*seer* – greatness, (that is)  
*villipuththUr* – [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/) and  
*selvam* – having wealth (that is)  
*thirukkOLUr* – thirukkOLUr and  
*Ar* – full of  
*Er* – beauty (that is)  
*perumbUthUr* – [SrIperumbUthUr](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/),  
*ennum ivai* – such [dhivyadhEsams](https://koyil.org/)  
*Ur* – (are the) places  
*pAril* – in the earth (where)  
*Arum* – (one(s)) having divine/special  
*madhi* – knowledge  
*ANdAL* – [sUdik koduththa nAchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/)  
*madhurakavi AzhvAr* – [madhurakavi Azhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/) and  
*ethirAsar* – [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
*thOnRiya* – divined their incarnation  
(respectively).

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining here with *‘seerArum villipuththUr’,* the places of incarnation of those who were divined about in an earlier pAsuram that started with ‘*AzhvAr thirumagaLAr ANdAL …* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 21](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-21/)\].

Since they incarnated as said in that pAsuram as ‘*vAzhvAga vandhu udhiththa* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 21](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-21/)\], the places of their incarnation is also having full of greatness and wealth everywhere.

*seerArum villipuththUr –* [SrIvillipuththUr](http://srivilliputhur.koyil.org/) having thriving wealth. That is like the combination of *pon* (gold), *maNi* (gems) and *muththu* (pearls) put together, having golden feet of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) **‘***villipuththUr uRaivAn* \[nAchchiyAr thirumozhi – 5.5\]’ (emperumAn divining his presence in SrIvillipuththUr), and [nAchchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who is the sthree dhanam (wealth) as can be said as ‘***maNi****valli*’, and, incarnating in the place where pearls are formed and as said in ‘*ikkarai ERi iLaiththu irundhEn* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 5.3.7\]’ (came out of the samsAram to the other shore due to your grace), like a (seeker) muktha who has reached the shore, that is [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) – having such combination it is having unlimited ever present wealth.

[![Srivilliputhoor-Aandaal-Temple-wikipedia](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Srivilliputhoor-Aandaal-Temple-wikipedia.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Srivilliputhoor-Aandaal-Temple-wikipedia.jpg)*SrIvillipuththUr temple*

Or, it can be said as referring to [nAchchiyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) that is ‘*kOvalar tham **pon** kodi* \[[thiruppAvai – 11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-11-karruk-karavai/)\]’ (sister of gOpalars (cowherd boys) and looking like a slim (and beautiful) creeper of gold), and [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) that is ‘***maNi**yai vAnavar kaNNanai* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.10.11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/10/thiruvaimozhi-1-10-11-maniyai-vanavar/)\]’ (One who has a form like a (radiant) precious gem, being the controller of those in paramapadham).

Or, it can be said as talking about [AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) and [thirumagaLAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) who have assumed the birth of cowherds and spending time immersed in the qualities (of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) as said in ‘*seer malgum AyppAdi* \[[thiruppAvai – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-01-margazhi-thingal/)\]’ (wealthy place of thiru AyppAdi), they are being complete in krishNan’s qualities as said in ‘*mali pugazh vaN kurugUr* \[thiruvAimozhi 4.2.11\]’ (having much greatness, head of [thirukkurugUr](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org) ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/))).

***selvath thirukkOLUr –*** As said in ‘*selvam malgi avan kidantha thirukkOLUr* \[thiruvAimozhi 6.7.7\]’ (having much wealth, thirukkOLUr, where he is in lying position), it is having vaiththamA**nidhi** (huge wealth being preserved for emergency / also the name of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) there).

***ErAr perubUthUr*** – That is, since ‘*ErAr ethirAsar* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/) – 37\]’ (full of beauty, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) incarnated there, the place is also being ‘*ErAr*’ (full of beauty), that is [SrIperumbUthur](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/).

Or, as said in ‘*senkayal vAvigaL sUzh vayal nALum siRandha perumbUthUr* \[Arththi prabandham – 32\]’ (~ ever great [SrIperumbUthUr](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/) that is full of fields, waters, fish, etc.), it is talking about the fertile place.

***ennum ivai*** – in this way these places that are talked about as popular.

***pAril madhi Arum ANdAL madhurakavi AzhvAr ethirAsar thOnRiya Ur ingu –*** that is – being full of bhagavath gyAnam (knowledge about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), etc), and which extends up to His devotees – having such quality is [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/) – she incarnated in ‘*seerArum SrIvillipuththUr’* (mentioned above).



Like ‘*Ayar kulaththinil thOnRum **(m)ANi** viLakku* \[[thiruppAvai – 5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/12/thiruppavai-05-mayanai/)\] ((krishNan) beautiful lamp/gem who arrived in the clan of cowherds)’, here in the clan of ‘*vEyar’* this ‘lamp’ incarnated.

Having knowledge equivalent to the aforementioned, who does not know any thing other than [nammAzhvar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) as said in ‘*thEvu maRRaRiyEn* \[[kaNNinuN chiruth thAmbu – 2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-2-navinal/)\]’, (that is, [madhurakavi AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/01/17/madhurakavi-azhwar/)),

[![perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691-1024x766.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691.jpg)*madhurakavi AzhvAr with his lord nammAzhvAr – (dhEvap) perumAL kOyil (kAncheepuram)*

and, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) the head of yathis, the places in which they appeared, that is, ‘*selvath thirukkOLUr ErAr perumbUthUr’* (mentioned previously).

***ingu*** – (here) – Gives the meaning that those who are ‘there’ (in SrIvaikuNtam) descended here and appeared.

It is said ‘*yadhAvathArAnmathurA murArE rAmasya sAkEtha purI cha yadhvath \| thadhA yathIndhrasya sadhAmupAsyA mahA bhUtha purI bhabhUva* \[prapannAmrutham 2.28\]’ **(**Like mathuRa due to incarnation of murAri the krishNan, and like ayOdhya due to incarnation of rAman, [SrIperumbUthUr](http://sriperumbuthur.koyil.org/) due to the incarnation of [yathirAja](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), became virtuous/sacred**)**.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३४
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (seerArum villipuththUr)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-33/)

**pAsuram 34**

*AzhvArgaL ERRam aruLichcheyal ERRam*  
*thAzhvAdhum inRi avai thAm vaLarththOr – Ezh pArum*  
*uyya avargaL sey(dha) vyAkkiyaigaL uLLadhellAm*  
*vaiyam aRiyap pagarvOm vAyndhu* 34

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-34)

**Word by word meaning**

*ERRam* – Greatness of  
*AzhvArgaL* – [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/),  
*ERRam* – (and) greatness of  
*aruLichcheyal* – [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) they divined,  
*vaLarththOr* – [pUrvAchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) (preceptors) who nurtured  
*avai thAm* – them to be  
*inRi* – without  
*Adhu* – any  
*thAzhvu* – shortcomings,  
*avargaL* – (and what) those [pUrvAchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) (preceptors)  
*sey(dha)* – divined  
*vyAkkiyaigaL* – as vyAkyAnams (books of commentaries/meanings)  
*Ezh pArum* – for all the seven worlds  
*uyya* – to get the true goal,  
*pagarvOm* – I shall say about  
*uLLadhu ellAm* – all of them  
*vAyndhu* – in appropriate ways *(porundhumpadi)*  
*vaiyam* – for the people of the earth  
*aRiya* – to learn about.

**vyAkyAnam**

Earlier he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) had stood divining elaborately about the order of incarnation of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), etc., as [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) mentioned in ‘*AzhvArgaL vAzhi aruLichcheyal vAzhi* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)\], and ‘*anthamizhAl naR kalaigaL Ayndhu uraiththa AzhvArgaL* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-5/)\].

Going forward, as he divined in the other part of that pAsuram as ‘*thAzhvAdhum il kuravar thAm vAzhi, Ezh pArum uyya avargaL uraiththavaigaL thAm vAzhi* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)\]*’*, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is now elaborately discussing about that part (of pAsuram 3). That is, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is saying that [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) shall announce about the greatness of texts of meanings of aruLichcheyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) which the preceptors ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) provided us for the world to reach the true goal *(uyvukkAga),* starting it with *‘AzhvArgaL ERRam’.*

*ERRam (greatness)* for them is – unlike those like rishis who gained knowledge with their own efforts,

they (AzhwArs) have the greatness of getting ‘*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\]’ (unblemished knowledge), due to causeless mercy of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), and

instead of thinking ‘let me get the goal (mOksham) when ever it happens later’ and so having a sight in worldly affairs, they were considering as life support, nourishment, and enjoyment all as [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) only,

(as they sang in various prabandhams like) ‘*ellAm kaNNan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.7.1\]’ (~ everything is kaNNan (for me)), and ‘*yAvaiyum thirumAl thirunAmangaLE kUvi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.7.3\]*’* (drawing all enjoyments from calling the divine names of emperumAn)*,* and ‘*uNdaRiyAL uRakkam pENAL* \[thirunedunthANdakam – 12\]’ (not knowing eating, not interested in sleep),** and ‘*pandhOdu kazhaL maruvAL* \[periya thirumozhi 5.5.9\]’ (~ won’t play with her play things), and so on,

and so would not sustain themselves if separated from Him even for half a second, and having the mindset like they said in ‘*mAkavaikuntham kANpadharku en manam Ekam eNNum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.3.7\]’ (My mind would only be thinking about seeing the bright SrIvaikuNtam), and ‘*vAnulagam theLindhE enRu eidhuvan* \[periya thirumozhi 6.3.8\]’ (When would the distress of this samsAram (life in material world) be cleared and would reach SrIvaikuNtam), and to get that goal, they have got parama bhakthi. Isn’t this their greatness compared to others?

***aruLichcheyal ERRam*** – greatness of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) is – as said in ‘*aruL koNdu Ayiram in thamizh pAdinAn* \[kaNNinuN chiruth thAmbu – 8\] (With great mercy sang 1000 pAsurams in [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)), it incarnated by the grace of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who gave divine vision, and as pushed by devotion as said in ‘*avAvil anthAdhi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.10.11\]’ (this anthAdhi prabandham that was born due to parama bhakthi), and focused only on talking about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), having distinguished greatness, being enjoyable, imparting knowledge, imparting all the knowledge that needs to be gained, being reason for [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s love, being able to release from material world, able to give the benefits quickly. Isn’t this the greatness of these compared to other texts.

Now, ***thAzhvAdhum inRi avai thAm vaLarththOr* –** ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) do without any mistakes and enrich existing good of such distinguished [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and their distinguished [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

[![srivaishna-guruparamparai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)*AchAryas (perceptors)*

That is, greatness of the author (*vakthru vailakshaNyam*), greatness of the prabandham (*prabandha vailakshaNyam*), and the matter conveyed in them (*prathipAdhya vailakshaNyam*) are enriched (by the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) with more details and relationships, etc., while thinking only about [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/). Since they are *‘thAzhvAdhum il kuravar* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)\] ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) with no blemishes/shortcomings), so they enriched these also without any shortcomings. ‘*vaLarththOr’* shows that a significant number of them were involved in this.

Now, the ones who enriched them did so through the vyAkyAnams (commentary text), so he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) continues to divine about that, as:

***Ezh pArum uyya avargaL sey(dha) vyAkkiyaigaL uLLadhellAm vaiyam aRiyap pagarvOm vAyndhu*** – by this, ‘*Ezh pArum uyya’ is –* as said in ‘*ivaRRAl uyyalAm* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.1.11\]’ (can reach true goal by these ten pAsurams), and ‘*ulaguyya umbargaLum kEttu uyya* \[iyal sARRu\]’ (for those in this world and the other worlds to know and reach true goal), they (the vyAkyAnams of [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) are such that those in all the worlds can listen to the words that are sweet to the ears (that is, ‘sevikkiniya senchol \[10.6.11\]’, as the root reference is aruLichchyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)).

They ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)) are of the nature of following that (aruLichcheyal) exactly, and doing it (vyAkyAnam) without expecting fame, profit, etc., and they are focused on the noble benefit that everyone should reach true goal by getting the rich meanings, and as said by him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) earlier ‘*Ezh pArum uyya avargaL uraiththavaigaL thAm vAzhi seyya maRai thannudanE sErndhu* \[[updhEsa raththina mAlai – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-3/)\]’ (for all the seven worlds to reach the true goal, long live what AzhvArs sang, and along with it the vEdhas), based on faith they follow the pronouncements of vEdhas when conveying the meanings (of [prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), (those vyAkyAnams are) best reference (pramANam) and due to that it can be followed by all the worlds, and be the reason for everyone to reach the true goal.

[![nampillai-goshti1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)*nampiLLai’s kAlakshEpa gOshti (group of discourse) at kOvil (SrIrangam)*

***avargaL sey(dha) vyAkkiyaigaL uLLadhellAm*** – As they are many, their vyAkyAnams are also in that way. He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines in detail in further pAsurams that such and such are those vyAkyAnams.

***uLLadhellAm vaiyam aRiyap pagarvOm vAyndhu*** – That is – as said in ‘*agal gyAlaththavar aRiya neRi ellAm eduththu uraiththa* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 4.8.6\]’ (for the ignorant people of the wide world to know He divined the essence of all the means (to reach Him)) **,**

([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), upon) seeing the misfortune of the (ignorant) people, thinking that their interest might be piqued about one ([vyAkyAnam](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) or the other, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divines his vow that he would inform about all the meanings for all the sentient for them to reach true goal. This is how his fruitful vow is.

[![srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti-1024x753.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti.jpeg)*maNavALa mAmunigaL’s eedu kAlakshEpa gOshti (discourse of thiruvAimozhi vyAkyAnam)*

Or, by saying that so and so divined vyAkyAnam for such and such prabandham, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divines for the sampradhAyam to be without any shortcomings, and so for people to reach true goal.

***pagarvOm vAyndhu*** – [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divines about their vyAkyAnams not based on cursory knowledge, but with the mind immersed in its meanings (*vAyndhu).*

This is how the mindset of significant love of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is, as he himself said in ‘*paNdu pala Ariyarum … piRarkkuk kAdhaludan kaRpiththu* \[Arththi prabandham 28\]’ (what the preceptors divined earlier… taught others with love).

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३५
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvArgaL ERRam)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-34/)

**pAsuram 35**

*AzhvArgaLaiyum aruLichcheyalgaLaiyum*  
*thAzhvA ninaippavargaL thAm naragil – veezhvArgaL*  
*enRu ninaiththu nenjE eppozhudum nee avar pAl*  
*chenRu aNugak kUsith thiri.* 35

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-35)

**Word by word meaning**

*nenjE* – Oh the mind!  
*nee* – you  
enRu *ninaiththu* – think that  
*ninaippavargaL* *thAm* – those who consider  
*AzhvArgaLaiyum –* the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and  
*aruLichcheyalgaLaiyum* – the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that they divined  
*thAzhvA* – as lowly,  
*veezhvArgaL* – would definitely fall  
*naragil* – in hell,  
*thiri* – (and so) spend your life (move around)  
*kUsi* – feeling ashamed  
*eppozhudhum* – at all times  
*chenRu* – to go  
*aNuga* – and reach  
*avar pAl* – such people.

**vyAkyAnam**

Earlier, as he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divined ‘*AzhvArgaL ERRam aruLichcheyal ERRam thAzhvu AdhuminRi avai thAm vaLarththOr* \[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 34\], instead of being one who enriches them and their dhivyaprabandhams, they are not only not doing that, due to their lowly mind they insult, and so will fall. So they are to be given up, he says to his mind, starting with *AzhvArgaLaiyum aruLichcheyalgaLaiyum’.*

[![mamunigal-vanamamalai-closeup](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/mamunigal-vanamamalai-closeup.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/mamunigal-vanamamalai-closeup.jpg)*[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) – [vAnamAmalai](http://vanamamalai.koyil.org/)*

***AzhvArgaL*** – they are – ‘*nimagnarai uyarththath thAzha* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 84\]*’* (extend themselves to uplift the downtrodden (regarding SrIvaishNavam));

they incarnated in all types of births as said in ‘*uyir aLippAn enninRa yOniyumAyp piRandhAi* \[thiruviruththam – 1\]’ (You ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) incarnated as different births (to protect all beings)). Same is said in ‘*yOginassarvyOnishu* \[guruparamparA prabhAvam part 166\]’ (yOgis are born in glorious ways, in all yOnis (classes)). It was divined ‘*kulam thAngu sAdhigaL nAlilum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.7.9\]*’* (~ in all the four classes of births).

***aruLichcheyal*** – they are – due to the divine desire (sankalpam) of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), for everyone to reach goal, in easy thamizh language that is easy for everyone like ‘*sAikaragam*’ (a vessel with a pout?) , as said in ‘*paNNiya thamizh mAlai* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.7.13\]’ (~garland made of thamizh poetry), it is the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that incarnated through [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), and they explain about [sarvEsvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/) – who is simple to approach for everyone in the form of archai (statue) in all [dhivya dhEsams](https://koyil.org/index.php/dhivya-dhesams/), having unlimited innumerable auspicious qualities, and can be followed by all sentient,

and the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) can be said as ‘*sen thamizh vEdham’*, that is, dhrAvida vEdha and its parts, that are called [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

Thinking of them as lowly (**thAzhvA ninaippavar)** is –

being not clear about the (aforementioned) greatness, and being mean by thinking that it is lowly based on the type of birth or type of language, that is they are like ‘*mAnasair anthyajAthithAm* \[manu smruthi 12.9\]’ (born in lowest birth due to offences committed by mind).

‘*dhravida bhAshA nirUpaNasamam inbamAriyil ArAichchiyum* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 75\]*’* is how they were divined as equivalent blemishes (of such people).

If they are thinking about it (lowly) in your mind and not saying out such that others know their thoughts, then still, as said in ‘*unnaich chindhaiyinAl igazhndha* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.6.6\]’ ((hiraNyan) who insulted you in his mind), it would end up being a big evil.

***ninaippavargaL thAm –*** with mind that is suitable for kindness (*irakkam*), the ones who have the audacity to use such mind to earn punishment for being unkind – such people would –

***naragil veezhvArgaL enRu*** *–* (fall in hell); think that – since such people are the target of what is said in ‘*na kshamAmi* \[varAha purANam\]*’* (would not tolerate (those who insult my devotees)), so they would be subject to ‘*kshipAmi* \[[SrI bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 16.19\]’ ((I will) push them (into asura births)), and will fall into the types of hell like *rauravam*.

***nenjE eppozhudum –*** Oh mind which is having significant devotion towards [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that they divined!

At all times –

***nee avar pAl chenRu aNugak kUsith thiri*** – You who is happy knowing about the greatness of our lords, be afraid to go and reach those who create disaster for themselves by offending those who find the way for you to get true life (*ujjeevanam*).

Since it is a disaster to befriend those who destroy *svarUpam* (true nature), be afraid to approach them and connect with them.

You have been with those who enrich your *svarUpam* (true nature), understand the nature of these other people and stay away from them thinking that their friendship is unbearable.

If asking how to know them – as said in ‘*thathAhi viparIthA thE budhdhir AchAra varjithA* \[SrI rAmAyaNam sundhara kANdam 21.10\]’ (because your mental attitude *(aRivu)* is without virtue and is upside down (not in a good state)), by their bad AchAram recognize their bad mind, and if you see them be afraid like when seeing a serpent, fire, etc. These would lead to destruction of our body; those people would lead to destruction of our *svarUpam* (true nature).

By this it is clear that – like saying ‘*AnukUlyasya sangkalpa:* \[SrI vishNu purANam – 1.14.3\]’ (vowing to be a good person), it is also required to say ‘*prAthikUlyasya varjana* \[SrI vishNu purANam – 1.14.3 / ahirbudhya samhithai 37.28 ?\]’ (avoid those that are adverse (to that vow)).

It was divined (by [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) –
‘*vyAkkiyaigaL uLLadhellAm vaiyam aRiyap pagarvOm vAyndhu* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 34](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-34/)\], isn’t it? { that is, this helps us reach the aforementioned goodness ?}

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३६
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (AzhvArgaLaiyum aruLichcheyalgaLaiyum)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-35/)

**pAsuram 36**

*theruLuRRa AzhvArgaL seermai aRivArAr*  
*aruLichcheyalai aRivArAr – aruL peRRa*  
*nAthamuni mudhalAm nam thEsikarai allAl*  
*pEthai manamE uNdO pEsu.* 36

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-36)

**Word by word meaning**

*aRivAr Ar* – Who knows  
*seermai* – the greatness of  
*AzhvArgaL* – [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)  
*theruL uRRa* – who have divine knowledge?  
*aRivAr Ar* – Who knows  
*aruLichcheyalai* – the greatness of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that they divined?  
*allAl* – – Except  
*nam* – our  
*thEsikarai* – [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)  
*nAthamuni mudhalAm* – starting from [SrIman nAthamunigAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/)  
*aruL peRRa* – who got the divine grace of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/),  
*pEthai manamE* – Oh the ignorant mind  
*pEsu* – you think through and say, (whether)  
*uNdO* – whether there can be anyone else (who know the greatness of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)).

**vyAkyAnam**

In the [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-35/) as he divined that those who do not know the greatness of distinguished pramANams ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), and its authors ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)) are to be given up, it is established that only those who know the greatness of these are the only ones to be regarded.

So when asked – who are those that are to be regarded, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) replied – is there anybody else – it is our [nAthamunigAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) and other [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/).

[![perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691-1024x766.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/perumal_koil_rappaththu_uthsavam_2015_nammazhvar_madhurakavi_azhvar_nathamunigal_DSC_0691.jpg)*aruL peRRa nAthamunigaL with aruL mARan (nammAzhvar) – (dhEvap)perumAL kOyil*

Ones in the previous pAsuram and the ones in this pAsuram are like those who abuse and praise respectively.

***theruL uRRa AzhvArgaL seermai aRivAr Ar –*** Since they are same in getting divined the unblemished knowledge (*mayarvaRa mathi nalam* ([thiruvAimozhi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/))), being ‘*theruL uRRa AzhvArgaL’* ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) having divine knowledge) is being their identity.

Nature of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) –

– As said in ‘*gyAnAnandha mayasthvAthmASEshOhi paramAthmana:* \[SrImath bhAgavatham\]’ (AthmA is of knowledge and bliss (gyAnAnandham) and servant of paramAthmA),

– by His grace got the state as said in ‘*uNarvum uyirum udambum maRRu ulappinavum pazhudhEyAm* \[[thiruvAimozi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.8.3\]’ (knowledge that captures information, life, and body)

– have understood the apex of truth (*thathva yAthAthmyam*) as said in ‘*uNarvenum perum padham therindhu* \[periya thirumozhi 1.1.1\]’ (took a step in to the big state that is gyAnam (knowledge)), and ‘*meymmaiyai miga uNarndhu* \[thirumAlai – 37\]’ (got knowledge of Athma svarUpam as is), and ‘*thAmaraiyAL kELvan oruvanaiyE nOkkum uNarvu* \[mudhal thiruvanthAdhi – 67\]’ (the gyAnam (knowledge) would only surrender to the [husband of – thAyAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who was born in the beautiful lotus flower), and ‘*uNarndha mey gyAniyar* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 60\]’ (the assembly (gOshti) of learned gyAnis of truth), and ‘*gyAninas thathvadharSina:* \[[SrI bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 4.34\]’ (gyAnis who saw in their mind the svarUpam of AthmA),

– and due to that being saviour (thArakar) for [Isvaran](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/12/thathva-thrayam-iswara-who-is-god/), and being the best of gyAnis (learned ones), as said in ‘*gyAnIthvAthmaiva mE matham* \[[SrI bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 7.18\]’ (In case of gyAni he is the life itself of me), and ‘*aRivAr uyir AnAi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – 6.9.8\]’ (Oh You having gyAnis as your AthmA!),

– while others are after artha (objects/wealth), kAma (desires), and having ignorance/in the dark, and live around like mad/drunk, these ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)) do not have any trace of darkness (in mind) as said in ‘*maruL il … vaN satakOpan* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.10.11\]’, and by that strength search for the bright mOksham, and get to SrIvaikuNtam. In [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ case aren’t they full of knowledge about the five things that one should know *([artha panchakam](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2015/12/artha-panchakam.html))*.

***theruL uRRa –*** is – being rooted in that (the aforementioned).

In this way they are being like ‘*nAttArOdu iyalvu ozhindhu nAraNanai nANNi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.2\]*’* (gave up interaction with the people and got SrIman nArAyaNan).

***seermai*** *– is –* Compared to those who have got the knowledge of [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/), [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) are better like the difference between an atom and a mountain (*parvatha paramANuvOttai vAsi)*, and having the greatness of having distinguished birth/life, activities *(vruththam)*, and knowledge.

That is, the greatness explained in *‘AzhvArgaL ERRam* \[updhESa raththina mAlai – 34\]’.

*seermai – greatness/glory.*

In the vyAkyAnam of ‘*thirumanthraththinudaiya *seermai*kkup pOrumpadi* \[mumkshuppadi – 3\]’, it was divined as ‘*gauravam’* (dignity).

nAyanar ([azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nAyanAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nayanar/)) also divined ‘*idhukku mUlam … patta pOdhu ezhu pOdhu aRiyAdhirundha *prabhAvam** \[AchArya hrudhayam – 93\]*’* (describes about the greatness of AzhvAr)*.*

[AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’ greatness is as said in ‘*viNNuLArilum seeriyar* \[thiruviruththam – 79\]’ ((those who are always worshipping emperumAn) are greater than those in the other worlds), and ‘*pErALan pErOdhum periyOr* \[periya thirumozhi 7.4.4\]’ (mahAthmAs who recite the divine names of the One having greatness) , and ‘*mikka seerth thoNdar* \[periya thirumozhi 11.1.9\]’ (SrIvaishNavas who are ananyaprayOjanars (not expecting any other benefit from him)).

Or, considering the phrase ‘*theruLuRRa AzhvArgaL seermai’* as being theruLuRRa is their seermai (being given divine knowledge is their greatness).

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is saying that except those whom he is going to list, who would know the greatness of the aforementioned.

***AzhvArgaL seermai aRivAr Ar –*** Are those who do not by habit distinguish between dhEham (body / prakruthi) and AthmA, going to go to the level of those who have understood the glory of their ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’) divine knowledge, in order to know their ([AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)’) greatness?

***aRivAr Ar –*** Or are the unfavorable (prathikUlar) who think that dhEham is Athma, going to be able to know the greatness of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) who are favourable (anukUlar).

So, he is saying ‘*aRivArAr’* sounding like it is rare (to find who know the greatness).

Furthermore, who would know the greatness of the prabandhams that are authored by the [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) which convey the meaning of prapaththi?

***aruLichcheyalai aRivAr Ar*** – Who would understand the greatness of its meanings and welcome and inculcate their divine verses that are [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)?

The word ‘*seermai*’ (greatness) is to be applied to this phrase also from previous phrase – it was divined as ‘*AzhvArgaL ERRam aruLich cheyal ERRam* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 34](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-34/)\]*’* only isn’t it (thus greatness is applicable to both). When understanding the greatness of prabandham phrases like ‘*theruL koLLach chonna Or Ayiraththu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 2.10.11\]’ (~ among the one thousand pAsurams said with divine knowledge), and such, it would imply that [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) have been graced, isn’t it?

Would those who attend to pleasuring words based on their svAthanthriyam (feeling independent from [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)), celebrate the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) of limitless enjoyment by understanding that the prabandhams are part of gaining their *svarUpam* (true nature)?

The limitless enjoyment is as said like in ‘*pAlOdu amudhu enRa Ayiram* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.6.11\]’ (~ among the one thousand pAsurams that are enjoyable like the mix of milk and food), and ‘*thoNdarkku amudhu* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.9.10\]’ ((said this thiruvAimozhi) as nectar for devotees) , and ‘*sencholAl eduththa dheiva nanmAlai* \[periya thirumozhi 1.1.10\]’ (divine garland made of beautiful words).

It is part of gaining svarUpam is as said like in ‘*paththarAgak kUdum payilumin* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.6.11\]’ (can become devotees so practice (this decad of thiruvAimozhi)), and *‘uriya thoNdar Akkum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.9.11\]’ ((those who learn this decad) it would make them ananyArha SEshabhUthar (subservient to Him only)).

In these, [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) understands the meaning of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), and explain to us.

Furthermore, [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is saying those who understand its greatness are; (of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) :

***aruL peRRa nAthamuni* mudhalA(m) *nam thEsikarai allAl* –** They are – starting from [nAthamuni](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) who got the grace of ‘[aruL mARan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’, they are in the seat of AchAryan, and enriching the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) with their passion – they are: the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) shown in ‘*nAtham pankajanEthra* … *dhEvAdhipAth* *\[[bhagavath vishayam thaniyans](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/bhagavath-vishayam-thaniyans/)\]’* *(*[nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) [uyyakkOndAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/24/uyyakkondar/) … dhEvarAjar ([nAlUrAchchAn piLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/21/nayanarachan-pillai/))).

((up to) *nam dhEsikar) –* His ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)’s) dhEsikar (AchAryan) is [thirumalai AzhvAr (thiruvAimozhip piLLai)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), as said in ‘*dhEvap perumAL kaik koNdaruLum thirumalai AzhvAr’* ([thirumalai AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) who is graced by dhEvap perumAL).

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is saying ‘*nam’ dhEsikar* due to his state of devotion (towards [his AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) /
[AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)).

[![srivaishna-guruparamparai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/srivaishna-guruparamparai.jpg)

***aruL peRRa nAthamuni*** – aruL – grace; [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) got the grace of [AzhvAr (nammAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), as well as the grace of mannanAr (emperumAn at [kAttumannAr kOyil](http://kattumannarkoyil.koyil.org) where he performed kainkaryam).

Only those who are the targets of grace of bhagavath and bhAgavathas would understand the greatness of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and the greatness of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) and live, isn’t it? Is it possible for others to understand?

***pEdhai manamE uNdO pEsu*** – Oh young mind! Is there anyone other than these able ones? Try to say and see if possible. There is no such meaning. So, he says no one occurs to the mind. By this, it says that what cannot be known with own efforts, would be known without any effort for those who are graced (by [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and His devotees).

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३७
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (theruL uRRa AzhvArgaL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-36/)

**pAsuram 37**

*OrAN vazhiyAy upadhEsiththAr munnOr*  
*ErAr ethirAsar innaruLAl – pArulagil*  
*Asai udaiyOrkkellAm AriyargAL kURum enRu*  
*pEsi varambu aRuththAr pin* 37

[pAsuram 37](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-37)

**Word by word meaning**

*munnOr –* [pUrvAcharyas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) (preceptors)  
*upadhEsiththAr* – were teaching  
*OrAN vazhiyAy* – in one purusha kramam (one to one / one after one).  
*pin* – Later,  
*Er Ar* – fully beautiful  
*ethirAsar* – [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
*in aruLAl* – by his kind grace,  
*enRu pEsi* – precepted (niyamanam) that  
*Asai udaiyOrkkellAm* – for all those who are interested in this,  
*pArulagil* – in the earth,  
*AriyargAL* – oh [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)!  
*kURum enRu* – you teach them  
*aRuththAr* – (and so) divined the removal of  
*varambu* – boundary of teaching.

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining about how the meaning of prapaththi was nurtured by the preceptors as a series starting from [SrIman nAthamunigAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/), and how [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) by his infinite grace divined and removed such boundary, and divined the way and carried it out; starting with ‘*OrAN vazhiyAy upadhEsiththAr’.*

Not having any difference between the meanings of prapaththi and of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), it is talking about – for growing [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), to begin with he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) divined the meaning of prapaththi first.

It was divined as ‘*dhvayArththam dhIrga SaraNAgathi enRadhu sArasangrahaththilE* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 210\]*’,* wasn’t it?

One who teaches [dhvayam](http://ponnadi.blogspot.com/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html) and [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) is the one who would be complete in being an AchAryan, is what they divined about this.

As said in ‘*samanthrarAja dhvayamAhayasmai* \[[nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) thaniyan as recited by the lineage of araiyar\]’ (who was taught thirumanthram dhvayam.. (by [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/))), it is only after divining dhvayam that [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) divined [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and other prabandhams to periya mudhaliyAr ([SrIman nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/)).

In the same way, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) divines by nurturing dhvayam and [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), isn’t it? So he first grew dhvayam first. Only after becoming experts in dhvayam would one start enriching on [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), isn’t it?

***OrAN vazhiyAy –*** Teaching only one or few eminent souls is how earlier [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) were carrying out this.

***munnOr –*** they are the ones before [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), that is, those starting from ‘*aruL peRRa* \[upadhESa raththinamAlai – 36\]’ [nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/). They considered the dignity of meanings and so were teaching in secrecy and protected it. nambi ([thirukkOttiyUr nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/)) too got promise from [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) before divining its meaning to him.

***eR Ar ethirAsar innaruLAl –*** unlike that, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is the lord of yathis, instead of focusing on the greatness of the meanings, saw the deterioration of these people, and based on only having loving kindness, did he propagate it.

***eR Ar ethirAsar –*** That is, as said in ‘*rUpamEvAsyai thanmahimAnam vyAchashtE* \[yajur vEdham\]’ (he said about the greatness of its beauty/form), and can be said as ‘*Er Arum seyya vadivu* \[Arththi prabandham – 30\]*’* (([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) of) complete beauty and elegant form), – by complete shining grace of his divine auspicious body he is of attraction to everyone, he could not tolerate as he saw the poor state of samsAris, and due to his causeless mercy only did he advise in this way.

[emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) corrected and protected the world with his quality of mesmerizing physical appearance and his quality of soul (Athma guNam).

[![EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/EmperumAnar_thirukoshtiyur.jpg)*emperumAnAr as divining from thirukkOshtiyUr*

If asked who are the eligible –

***pAr ulagil Asai udaiyOrkkellAm –*** for those living in this world who have got even little interest.

***Asai udaiyOr –*** Like saying ‘*nidhi udaiyOr’,* it is to be said as ‘*paththudai adiyavakku* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.3.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruvaimozhi-1-3-1-paththudai-adiyavar/)\]’ (to the adiyArs who have the devotion).

In this world those who are interested in this, is rare indeed.

So without looking at the superiority or inferiority based on their birth, living, and knowledge (*janma, vruththa, gyAnam),* and looking only at the indication of interest by being amicable (to the teachings), you tell them the greatest meanings that I have told you;

Since he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) is devoted to the divine feet of the one ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) who said, ‘*maRRu onRillai surungach chonnOm mAnilaththu evvuyirkkum* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 9.1.7\]’ (there is no upAyAntharam (other means), will say it short to everyone in this wide world), he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) divined: ‘*pAr ulagil Asai udaiyOrkkellAm’.*

**AriyargAL –** As said in ‘*kAryam karuNamAryENa* \[SrI rAmAyaNam yudhdha kANdam – 116.49\]*’* (for the one having good virtues, it is apt to be kind), you also just by kindness do the teaching (he said). He is removing the boundaries by speaking based on his sweet kindness, isn’t it? In the same way he is divining them also to teach.

***AriyargAL –*** He was addressing those who were present with him at that time in front of theRkAzhvAn, saying that – like me you also use the little interest shown, and teach all such people – saying so he removes the hurdles.

Or,

***AriyargAL –*** is also referring to those he established as the set of [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) that include [kUraththAzhvAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/kurathazhwan/) and such 74 noble ones.

By this it gives the meaning that those who have learned from a very valued AchAryan *(peru madhippan)* themselves shall teach, and those who have the interest (*sradhdhai*) shall learn from them.

***AriyargAL kURum enRu pEsi varambu aRuththAr pin –*** Previous [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), as said in ‘*idham thE nAthapaskAya* \[[srI bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) – 18.67\]’ (what I have said, secretly), told their disciples not to teach everyone but just be involved in it themselves, and so had kept it in secrecy. Afterwards, since he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) is ever interested in betterment of others, told by mouth that you spread it by your teachings.

***munnOr varambu aRuththAr pin –*** Like that time when [perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) (SrI rAman) stopped and destroyed the boundary put by the mudhalis (mAhArAjar and his groups) (by accepting vibhIshaNan?), here too he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) crossed the boundaries put in by them (earlier [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/)). Isn’t he who established the boundary (sampradhAyam/visishtAdhvaitham?) did like this?

As said in ‘*rAmAnujasya karuNAvaruNAlayasya* \[rAmAnuja prapaththi\]’ (to [rAmAnujar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is full of mercy), such sea of mercy breaking the boundary of shores.

{ What follows from here till end of this vyAkyAnam is connected together with a very interesting play of words. and is thought provoking too }

That is, like the **kings** who change the narrow **one-man** lane into a broad road, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) also changed the path of **‘*Or AN vazhi*’** one-by-one way, by his sweet grace, into a broad path by asking to teach to all those that are amicable, thus removing the barriers.

It is said ‘*SrImAn rAjapadhamcha kAradhayayA rAmAnujAryOmuni:* ’ (due to his kindness rAmAmunja muni performed **kingly** presidency).

As he performed like said in ‘*rAmAmunja peru vazhi vetti’.  *

Isn’t he ‘*vishNu lOka maNi maNdapa **mArga** dhAyi* \[dhAtI panchakam – 5\]*’* (gifts the **path** to vishNu lokam’s maNi maNdapam (SrI vaikuNtam))*?*

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३८
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (OrAN vazhiyAy)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-37/)

**pAsuram 38**

*emperumAnAr tharisanam enRE idharku*  
*namperumAL pErittu nAtti vaiththAr – ampuviyOr*  
*indhath tharisanaththai emperumAnAr vaLarththa*  
*andhach cheyal aRigaikkA.*
38

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-38)

**Word by word meaning**

*ampuviyOr* – For the residents of earth  
*aRigaikkA* – to know (about),  
*andhach cheyal* – that deed/achievement of  
*emperumAnAr* – [SrI bhAshyakArar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)  
*vaLarththa* – enriching/growing  
*indhath tharisanaththai –* this SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam,  
*namperumAL* – [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) of thiruvarangam  
*nAtti vaiththAr* – established firmly  
*pEr ittu* – (with) the divine name  
*idhaRku* – for this SrIvaishNava sampradhAyam  
*emperumAnAr tharisanam enRE* – as emperumAnAr dharisanam.

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining about [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s nurturing of the prapaththi mArgam (way of prapaththi), and divining SrI bAshyam and other granthams to protect that way, and nurturing this sampradhAyam based on that, and for every one to know this [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) naming this sampradhAyam based on [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s name, and establishing that firmly – by starting this pAsuram with ‘*emperumAnAr tharisanam’*.

While [SrIman nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/) and [yAmuna munigaL (ALavandhAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/01/alavandhar/) are enriching the dharSanam, [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) pointed out its name as ‘*emperumAnAr dharSanam*’ based on [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s goal as only helping the others.

[![namperumal-nachiar_serthi2](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/namperumal-nachiar_serthi2-1024x768.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/namperumal-nachiar_serthi2.jpg)*namperumAL in sErththi (together with thAyAr, a special once-in-a-year treat)*

It is similar to what is said in ‘*maryAdhAnAmcha lOkasya karththA kArayithA cha sa:* \[SrI rAmAyaNam sundhara kANdam 35.11\]’ (~SrI rAma is the doer of the laws of justice, and is one who makes them follow it).

That is, the noble meanings he got from [thirukkOttiyUr nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/) after walking several times, he donated that in a big way even at the expense of himself, and returned (to SrIrangam); then [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who thought ‘*namakkAvArai nAmE thEdik koLvOm* (\~~we shall find the one who would be suitable for us), and so [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) gave very special name for this based on [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), and said, from today ‘identify this path as emperumAnAr dharSanam’ (*‘emperumAnAr dharSanam ennungOL’),* and so divined his establishing of this, in this way in the world.
