Or, instead of ‘*nAtti vaiththAr*’, when it is recited taught as ‘*nAttuviththAr*’ (made someone establish this), then, when [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) broke the command, crossed the boundary and taught prapaththi to others, seeing that greatness, [thirukkOttiyUr nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/) too in the same way gave him the divine name as ‘[emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’, and said, ‘from today say this as emperumAnAr dharSanam \[guruparamparA prabhavam – page 195\]’, and was nurturing it, so [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who divined to [(thirukkOttiyUr) nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/) to let this name be known, He Himself divined this through [nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/).

He ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) removed the loneliness of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) that is said in ‘*ALumALAr* \[thiruvAimozhi 8.3.3\]’ (he is not having any one (and he himself is holding his conch and discus, nobody is involved in his divine feet, and so on)), and for removing the loneliness of the samsAris, by doing such teaching.

If asked what is the reason for [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) to establish this about dharSanam, he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) says,

***‘ampuviyOr indhath tharisanaththai emperumAnAr vaLarththa andhach cheyal aRigaikkA’.***

Due to inclusion of the name [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in it, the dharisanam which [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) nurtured, the dharisanam which is of esteemed vaidhIkam, and is without any blemishes, which he grew through his teachings (upadhESam) – ([namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) established this name for the dharisanam) for the people of the beautiful world to know this deed of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/).

***andhach cheyalai aRigiakkA(ga)*** – That is, for the people of the world to know such deed, and reach the true goal. That is, for the people of the world to know and reach true goal, he performed these deeds *as a help for the world* – [namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) wanted the people to know this so he named it as *emperumAnAr dharisanam*.

By this, his growing of the the dharsanam is through the prapaththi sAsthram is the fact that is well established.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ३९
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (emperumAnAr tharisanam)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-38/)

**pAsuram 39**

*piLLAn nanjIyar periyavAchchAn piLLai*  
*theLLAr vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai*  
*maNavALa yOgi thiruvAimozhiyaik kAththa*  
*guNavALar enRu nenjE kURu.* 39

[pAsuram 39](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-39)

**Word by word meaning**

*nenjE* – Oh mind,  
*kURu* – you shall say, thatn  
piLLAn *–* [thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/), and  
*nanjIyar* – [nanjIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/), and  
*periyavAchchAn piLLai* – [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/), and  
*theL Ar* – one who is having clear mind, that is  
*vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLAi* – [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/), and  
*maNavALa yOgi* – [vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALach chIyar (jIyar)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/)  
are the ones  
*kuNavALar enRu* – having great qualities, who/as they  
*kAththa* – protected  
*thiruvAimozhiyai* – [thiruvAimozhi prabandham](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)  
(through their [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)).

**vyAkyAnam**

Now, [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is the meaning of [dhvayam](http://ponnadi.blogspot.com/2015/12/rahasya-thrayam.html), was given birth by the ‘mother’ [satakOpan (nammAzhvAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), and was spread by the affectionate mother [rAmAnujan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) as said in ‘*eenRa mudhal thAy satakOpan, moimbAl vaLarththa idhath thAy rAmAnusan* \[[thiruvAimozhi thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-thaniyans-invocation/)\]’, and in the same way he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) too was growing it;

due to their grace, matching their opinions of its meanings, through creation of vyAkyAnams for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is the essence of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), those who protected it are [piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/) et al, says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), starting this pAsuram with ‘*piLLAn*’.

[![pillan_055_4762658378_l](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/pillan_055_4762658378_l.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/pillan_055_4762658378_l.jpg)*empeumAnAr overseeing and blessing piLLAn’s marriage*

***piLLAn*** *–* he is: As [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) was thankful to [thirukkOshtiyUr nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/) for his great mercy, he gave [nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/)’s name ([kurugEsar / thirukkurugaip pirAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/)) to his sishya as [thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/), whom he considered as his son; such is this person who has the greatness of having the name of [nambi](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/02/27/thirukkoshtiyur-nambi/), and because of that, he was being important than others for him ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)), and learned from him ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) all inner meanings of vEdhAntham, and was knowledgeable in all sAsthras, and grew thamizh and samskrutha vEdhanthams as ubhaya vEdhAntha pravarththakar (one who enriches/spreads it).

**nanjIyar –** he is: loved as ‘*nammudaiya jIyar*’ (our jIyar) by the divine son of fully knowledgeable [kUraththAzhvAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/kurathazhwan/), that is [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/) who knows all the SAsthrams; and ([nanjIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)) learned all the meanings in the sannidhi (presence) of bhattar, without any doubt or confusion, and after that explained [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) a hundred times and due to that had the sadhAbhishEkam (honour of completing a hundred).

[![nanjeeyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/nanjeeyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/nanjeeyar.jpg)*nanjIyar*

***periyavAchchAn piLLAi*** – he is – surrendered to the divine feet of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) who is like the incarnation of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/), and for avoiding the hurdles for any kainkaryams to his [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) he had left all the other goals/achievements along with any trace, and learned and heard all the meanings clearly in his [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s sannidhi, and being liked very much by his [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/).

[![periyavachchan_pillai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/periyavachchan_pillai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/periyavachchan_pillai.jpg)*periyavAchchAn piLLai*

***theLLAr vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai*** – Having such great clarity in spreading the meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), and due that, earning the phrase of ‘*sakrushNa dhvayau* \[[thiruvAimozhi bhagavath vishaya thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/bhagavath-vishayam-thaniyans/)\]’ ([nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) having [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) and [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/)), and being talked together with [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) for doing personal kainkaryams to [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), excelling as per precept, and being *abhimAna nishtAgragaNyar* (one of the leading in loving (the AchAryan)).

[![vadakkuthiruveedhipillai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vadakkuthiruveedhipillai-522x1024.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vadakkuthiruveedhipillai.jpeg)*vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLAi*

***maNavALa yOgi –*** he is – To be said as ‘*abhayapradharAja puthrar*’, he fully reached the divine feet of [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) ‘s divine son [nayanArAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nayanarachchan-pillai/), and learned the full and inner meanings of sampradhAyam, rahasyams, and [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) from his teachings, and also learned all the SAsthrams as part of these, and being able to win over other philosophies, and having the talent of speech as can be said as *‘vAdhi kEsari’*. That is, [vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/).

[![vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)*vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALA jIyar*

Such people as mentioned above –

***thiruvAimozhiyaik kAththa –*** that is, having the great quality of protecting well by doing their individual vyAkyAnams for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is the best in pramANams (references/base) – protecting it from those having less knowledge.

They authored the [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) starting from *ArAyirappadi* (vyAkyAnam having the length of 6,000 groups of words), and ending in panneerAyirappadi (12,000 groups of words), and this is explained by him ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) himself clearly in later pAsurams.

***kAththa gunavALar enRu nenjE kURu –*** Oh the mind which is prostrating the qualities of such people who are having the quality of protecting it through the greatness of their [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/).

As an outlet of your happiness for their [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), always say about their qualities like said in ‘*thadhvAchAvadhathi* \[thaiththiriyam AraNyakam 1.23\] (he is saying that by his mouth). Other parts of us are the pathway for the mind. According to that, he is saying ‘*kURu’* (say it).

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४०
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (piLLAn nanjeeyar …)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-39/)

**pAsuram 40  **

*mundhuRavE piLLAn mudhalAnOr seydhu aruLum*  
*andha viyAkkiyaigaL anRAgil – andhO*  
*thiruvAimozhip poruLai thErndhu uraikka valla*  
*guruvAr ikkAlam nenjE kUru.* 40

[pAsuram 40](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-40)

**Word by word meaning**

*mundhuRavE* – Before itself  
*piLLAn mudhalAnOr* – [thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/) and others, the five of them  
*seydhu aruLum* – divined the authoring of  
*andha viyAkkiyaigaL* – those [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) (commentaries / explanations);  
*anRAgil* – If these were not there  
*andhO* – O! (*aiyyO! – alas!)*  
*guru Ar* – who are present as AchAryas  
*ikkAlam* – at this time  
*valla* – who can  
*thErndhu –* clearly know  
*uraikka* – and explain the  
*thiruvAimozhip poruLai –* great meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) *(arththa visEsham)*  
*nenjE* – Oh mind  
**kURu** – you shall say!

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining in a negating way about the greatness of [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) that they authored earlier, as ‘***mundhuRavE piLLAn mudhalAnOr seydhu aruLum****’.*

That is, as said in ‘*gyAnAnyalpee bhavishyanthi* \[bhAgavatham\]’ (becomes less in knowledge), before the sampradhAyams become less and less, already, at earlier time itself, the five AchAryas from [piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/) to [jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/) divined –

***andha viyAkkiyaigaL*** – those distinguished [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).

***anRAgil –*** if they had not authored them; if in those times if they who are visionaries (dhIrgadharSi) had not authored the [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), then today how we would have suffered – saying so he feels sad.

**andhO** – Same as said in ‘*na chEth rAmAnujEth yEshA chathurA chathurAkshari \| kAmavasthAm prapadhyanthE janthavO hantha mAdhrusa:* \[varavaramuni mukthakam – 5 / uththara dhinacharyA – 20\]’

(Oh! If there was no ‘rAmAnuja’ the most prudent four lettered manthra, what state would worms like me would have ended up in, isn’t it?).

***thiruvAimozhip poruLai thErndhu uraikka valla guru Ar ikkAlam nenjE kURu –*** When explaining [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) is it not needed to have wisdom that is complete in knowledge? Who is there now with clear knowledge to explain this? Where would they be seen?

Looking at the feeble state of knowledge in this time, (and on the other hand) the profoundness of meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) as said in *‘dhrAvida vEdhasAgaram* \[[thiruvAimozhi thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-thaniyans-invocation/)\]*‘* (an ocean of dhrAvida (thamizh) vEdham), and, ‘*ALavu iyanRa anthAdhi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/thiruvaimozhi-1-4-11-alavu-iyanra/) 1.4.11\]’ ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/thiruvaimozhi-1-4-11-alavu-iyanra/) with unlimited glories), he ([maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is saying who is having the capability to understand this correctly and author a suitable vyAkyAnam for it.

***thErndhu uraikka valla guru Ar –*** When it is rare to find even those who can understand the greatness of those existing [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), as said in *‘aRiyak kaRRu vallAr* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – 5.5.11\]’ (), and grow it, it is very rare to find anyone now who can follow the divine mind of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) and author a vyAkyAnam, isn’t it?

[![srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti-1024x753.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti.jpeg)*Completion of thiruvAimozhi eedu discourse by maNavALa mAmunigaL*

***uraikka valla*** – by this, there being rarity in (finding one who can) match the meaning to the letters.

***uraikka valla guru Ar ikkAlam –*** During the time (now) when there are those who steal **things** *(poruL)*, would it be possible to get those who would enrich the **meanings** *(poruL)*

{in thamizh ‘*poruL*’ is for both ‘thing’ and ‘meaning’. It is a similar case in samskrutham for the word ‘*artham*’}.

Even then, time is such that they would escape with ‘*kaipporuL*’ (important things / what is left), isn’t it?

They would steal ‘*piRar nan poruL* \[[kaNNinuN chiruth thAmbu – 5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu-5-nambinen/)\]’ (Others’ good things / AthmA which is [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)’s property), isn’t it?

As the time is cruel, as said in ‘*kadal aLavAya thisai ettinuLLum **kali** iruLE midai tharu kAlaththu* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 59\], would there be one who with their sharp true knowledge analyze the meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) and say it?

***nenjE kURu –*** Oh mind! which is obedient to the [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) AchAryas starting from the time of [bhAshyakArar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/). Like them who see the same meanings (in [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)), try to show me even one person as so and so, during the current time.

So getting them is being rare isn’t it?

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४१
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (mundhuRavE piLLAn)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-40/)

**pAsuram 41**

*theLLArum gyAnath thirukkurugaip pirAn*  
*piLLAn ethirAsar pEraruLAl – uLLArum*  
*anbudanE mARan maRaip poruLai anRu uraiththadhu*  
*inbamigum ARAyiram.*
41

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-41)

**Word by word meaning**

[thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/),  
*theL Arum* – (who is having) full clarity in  
gyAnam – knowledge,  
pEr – (by the) special *(periya)*  
aruLAl – grace of (kataksham)  
ethirAsar – [SrI bhAshyakArar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/),  
Arum – with full of  
anbudanE – devotion  
uL – in his divine mind,  
anRu – during that earlier time  
uraiththadhu – divined  
poruLai – grand meanings of  
mARan – what nammAzhvAr divined, that is  
maRai – dhrAvida (thamizh) vEdham, [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/),  
migum – the vyAkyAnam which is full of  
inbam – sweetness, is  
ARAyiram – ArAyirappadi vyAkyAnam (having 6000 sets of 32 letters).

**vyAkyAnam**

Earlier, starting with ‘*piLLAn nanjIyar … thiruvAimozhiyaik kAththa gunavALar* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-39/)\]’, where he divined the list of each of the five [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) separately, out of that,

in this pAsuram, as said in ‘*kurugaippirARku anbAm ethirAsar* \[[bhagavath vishayam thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/bhagavath-vishayam-thaniyans/)\]’ ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is most dear to [thirukkurukaippirAn piLLAn](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan)),

by the limitless kindness of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) who is ‘*prapanna jana kUtasthar* \[AchArya hrudhayam – 36\]’ (head of the people who performed SaraNAgathy (surrendered to [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/))),

the count of groups of words vyAkyAnam authored by [thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/) is *shad sahasram* (six thousand),

says [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/).

[![azhwar-emperumanar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/azhwar-emperumanar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/azhwar-emperumanar.jpg)*AzhvAr and emperumAnAr – [AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org) (thirukkurugUr)*

***theLLArum gyAnath thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn*** – Having suitable complete wisdom in clarity of knowledge for authoring the first vyAkyAnam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), that is [thirukkurugaip pirAn piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/).

***ethirAsar pEr aruLAl –*** By the limitless kindness of [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/), as said in ‘*un perun karuNai thannai* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 70\]’. This is the reason for him doing the vyAkyAnam.

***uLLArum anbudanE –*** That is, not doing it for *kyAdhi* (fame), *lAbham* (profit), etc., due to the limitless love for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/). Due to unlimited compassion towards the sentient.

***mARan maRaip poruLai*** – As said in ‘*aruLinAn avvarumARaiyin poruL* \[[kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu – 8](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/02/kanninun-chiru-thambu-8-arul-kondadum/)\]’ (essence of that rare (difficult to acquire/learn) vEdham), it being [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s, in the form of vEdham, being hard for others to identify its meanings, such [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)’s meanings was divined as *ArAyiram* (in six thousand sets of 32 letters).

It was written with love, that suits with ‘*avAvil anthAdhi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.10.11\]’ ().

***anRu uraiththadhu –*** that is, listening from [bhAshyakArar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) and thinking through it, getting clarity of the meanings, is when he had authored the vyAkyAnam.

If asking what its count is –

***inbamigum ARAyiram*** – As said in ‘*amar suvai Ayiram* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.3.11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/thiruvaimozhi-1-3-11-amarargal-thozhuthu/)\]’ (well-fit sweet and sound meaning), being fully interesting and sweet *(rasa ganam)*, being delightful to the devotees, it is set in the length of delightful six thousand that he divined. That good taste is obtained from the *mUlam* (original text – [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)), isn’t it?

Since it is done with love, this would also be delightful, isn’t it?

Since he is loved like a son of [paurANikar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) (well versed in puraNams, that is, [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)), he has written it in the count of SrI vishNu purANam of six thousand, isn’t it?

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४२
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (theLLArum gyAna)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-41/)

**pAsuram 42**

*thanjeerai gyAniyargaL thAm pugazhum vEdhAnthi*  
*nanjeeyar thAm bhattar nal aruLAl – enjAdha*  
*Arvamudan mARan maRip poruLai Ayndhu uraiththadhu*  
*Er onbadhinAyiram.*
42

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-42)

**Word by word meanings**

gyAniyargaL thAm – Those having knowledge of thathvam (truth of existence)  
pugazhum – would praise  
tham seerai – his greatness  
vEdhanthi – who is the learned one  
nanjeeyar thAm – that is [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/),  
nal aruLAl – due to the good grace of  
bhattar – [SrI parAsara bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/),  
Ayndhu – ([nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)) thought through / researched the  
mARan mARaip poruLai – meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) of mARan (nammAzhvAr)  
uraiththadhu – and divined  
enjAdha – with never decreasing  
Arvamudan – devotion  
Er – a beautiful  
onbadhinAyiram – onbadhinAyirappadi vyAkyAnam (9,000 padi).

**vyAkyAnam**

[maNvALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divines that, after that, by the grace of [periya bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/), [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/) divined in a great way a vyAkyAnam that is half time more than ArAyirappadai (of piLLAn) for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – as onbadhinAyiram (nine thousand) – starting the pAsuram with ‘*nanjeeyar*’ and so on.

That is, having knowledge and other qualities that are apt for authoring a vyAkyAnam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), the knowledge that is praised by those having knowledge in vEdham, etc.

Or, having the greatness of qualities that are auspicious for the world, like following the path of AchAryan as said in *‘AchAryavAn* \[chAndhOkyOpanishath – 6.14.2\]’ (One having AchAryan is the one who understands truth of existence (thathvam))*’*, and such qualities, so having greatness that is celebrated by the knowledgeable ones, and who is identified as vEdhAnthigaL, that is [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/).

Now due to the greatness of being called ‘vEdhAnthi [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)’, [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/) divined his visit quite far and corrected him – he having such greatness.

[![parasara-bhattar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/parasara-bhattar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/parasara-bhattar.jpg) *bhattar with nanjIyar at his lotus feet  *

***nanjeeyar thAm*** – such a highly valued person

***bhattar nal aruLAl –*** Due to [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/)’s own mercy. For him [bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/)’s mercy worked out directly and seen – for him to author a vyAkyAnam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/).

***bhattar nal aruLAl –*** *nallaruL* – like saying *‘namperumAL’ (an adjective which highlights the greatness/proximity to heart?)*. There it was the mercy of Him, he who is mentioned in [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/); here it is the grace of who taught about [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) ([bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/)). This grace is being better than His grace – that was reason for one thousand (pAsurams in [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)); this is reason for nine thousand (onbadhinAyirappadi). This is being nine for one {means being more merciful/kind}.

***aruLAl enjAdha Arvamudan:*** Due to his ([bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/11/parasara-bhattar/)’s) grace, auspicious thing happened to him ([nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)). Like said as ‘*nalam aruLinan* \[[thiruvAizmohi 1.1.1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-1-1-1-uyarvara-uyarnalam/)\]’ (divined goodness). By such grace of him only he got unbounded love in this. *enjal* – contracting; (enjAdha is the opposite of it).

***Arvamudan mARan maRaip poruLai Ayndhu uraiththadhu –*** Qualifying for the prabandham of one having ‘*ArAdha kAdhal’’* (never-satiating love), with love as said in ‘*Arvam peruga* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 3.5.8\]’ (overflowing love), and thinking through the meanings of thamizh vEdham [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) that is ‘*mARan paNiththa thamizh maRai* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 9](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/12/upadhesa-raththina-malai-9/)\]’ (thamizh vEdham divined by [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)), and to match its greatness what is the length/number of the vyAkyAnam done by him?

When asked so, He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) says,

***EronbadhinAyiram –*** (beautiful nine thousand) **–** Qualifying for the beautiful thamizh maRai ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)). This (vyAkyAnam) having full of beauty is – due to smartness in connection of words, and dignity of meanings, it is being full of beauty.

He being ‘vEdhAnthi [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)’, he divined this matching the count (9,000) of SrIbAshyam which is vEdhAntha SAsthram.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४३
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (tham seerai gyAniyargaL)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-42/)

**pAsuram 43**

*nampiLLAi thammudaiya nal aruLAl Eviyidap*  
*pin periyavAchchAn piLLai adhanAl – inbA*  
*varu paththi mARan maRaip poruLaich chonnadhu*  
*irupaththu nAlAyiram.*
43

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-43-new)

**Word by word meaning**

*nampiLLai*  
*thammudaiya* – by his  
*nal aruLAl* – good grace  
*Eviyida* – commanded,  
*pin* – after that  
*adhanal* – due to that precept  
*periyavAchchAn piLLai*  
*chonnadhu* – divined  
*mARan maRaip poruLai* – meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) (that came due to)  
*paththi* – devotion (that came due to)  
*inbA* – delightful  
*varu* – bhagavath katAksham (to [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/));  
*irupaththu nAlAyiram* – (vykyAnam for it is) – irupaththu nAlAyirappadi (24,000).

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining that, after that, based on [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s order, [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) divined a vyAkyAnam that is three times bigger than the one said in [previous pAsuram](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-32/) (onbadhinAyirappadi vyAkyAnam of [nanjeeyar](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nanjiyar/)).

***nampiLLai thammudaiya nal aruLAl Eviyida*** – Being one who enriches the sampradhAyam, who is glorified as as ‘*kAruNyapUrNam kalivairidhAsam* \[[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) thaniyan\]’ (being full of kindness, having the name of thirukkalikanRi dhAsar dhAsyam nAmam [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)), being a *krupAmAthra prasannAchAryar* (teaches purely based on looking at the pitiable state of those sentient who are interested in learning and following), that is [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/),

being interested only in being beneficial to others, with his grace as said in ‘*koLvadhilaiyAgiya kuLirndha aruL thAn* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam thaniyan\]’, asked him to do a vyAkyAnam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/); as per that, based on the precept that is only due to grace, ([periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/)) thought of it as ‘kriyathAm ithi \[SrI rAmAyaNam AraNya kAndam – 15.7\]’ (it shall be built), and as ‘*kUvip paNi koLLAy* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.5.7\]’ (call me in front of you and divine your acceptance of my servitude),

[![periyavachan-pillai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/periyavachan-pillai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/periyavachan-pillai.jpg)*periyavAchchAn piLLAi*

***pin periyavAchchAn piLLAi*** – after such a command, as said in ‘*paraVanasmi* \[SrI rAmAyaNam AraNya kANdam 15.7\]*’* (adiyen dhAsa bhUthan), being a servant of that one,

***adhanAl*** – based on the command of the AchAryan – by this it distinguishes him from [naduvil thiruveedhip piLLai bhattar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/20/naduvil-thiruvidhi-pillai-bhattar/), and [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) who wrote vyAkyAams on their own accord (after listening to kAlakshEpams of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)).

***adhanAl inbA varu paththi mARan maRaip poruLai –*** If what is desired to be done very much is decreed to be done, then one would rush for it. For [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) too which is ‘*pAlOdu amudhanna Ayiram* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 8.6.11\]’ (being most enjoyable like the mix of milk and nectar/food), such a decree was made for doing vyAkyAnam. That is why he authored vyAkyAnam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) that was created by the devotion instigated by [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) (that is, *inbA varu paththi mARan maRaip poruLaich chonnadhu).*

***inbA varu paththi*** – The matter ([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) to think about is sweet, as can be said as ‘*susukham* \[[srI bhagavath gIthA](http://githa.koyil.org/) 9.2\]’ (pleasant/sweet to follow in action), the devotion (bhakthi) is being of unlimited happiness, AzhvAr who is apt *(prApthar)* and respected/confidential *(Apthar)*, by the force of overflowing devotion like a flooding river, divined [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is thamizh vEdham, and [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) divined its meanings as a vyAkyAnam for it.

***irupaththu nAlAyiram*** – is the meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) of *paththi* (devotion) mARan.

Like saying ‘*kAdhal kurugUrch chatakOpan* \[[thiruvAimozhi 2.1.11](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruvaimozhi-2-1-11-soratha-epporutkum/)\]’ (having uncontrollable love that is [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/) of [AzhvAr thirunagari](http://azhwarthirunagari.koyil.org)), since this came due to ‘*inbA varu paththi*’ (grace through which the devotion came), it incarnated as ‘*bhakthAmrutham* \[[thiruvAimozhi thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-thaniyans-invocation/)\]’ (as nectar for devotees). In this way, the unbounded sweetness that is the meanings of [mARan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)‘s [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), is of twenty four thousand.

As said in ‘*chathurvimsathsahasrANi SlOkAnAm ukthavAn rushi:* \[SrI rAmAyaNam bAla kANdam – 4.2\]’ (rushi divined it having twenty four thousand slOkas), the count of one that is best of ithihAsams, that is, SrI rAmAyaNam, is how [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) divined his vyAkyAnam.

***inbA varu paththi mARan maRaip poruLai –*** As said in ‘*irAmAyaNam ennum paththi veLLAm* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 37\]’ (~ flood of devotion that is rAmAyaNam), is how this ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)) is also of flood of devotion. So its vyAkyAnam is also formed in the same way (of count).

*‘SrI rAmAyaNam enRum thiruvAimozhi enRum iraNdu mahA prabandhangaL uNdu’* (there are two great prabandhams named SrI rAmAyaNam and [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)) – is how these two are said as equivalent isn’t it?

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४४
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (nampiLLai thammudaiya)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-43/)

**pAsuram 44**

*theLLiyadhA nampiLLai cheppu neRi thannai*  
*vaLLal vadakkuth thiruveedhip – piLLai indha*  
*nAdu aRiya mARan maRaip poruLai nangu uraiththadhu*  
*eedu muppaththARayiram.*
44

[pAsuram 44](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-44)

**Word by word meaning**

*theLLiyadhu A –* With clarity  
*(what) [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)*  
*cheppum* – divined about  
*neRi thannai* – the ways (meanings),  
*[vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)*  
*vaLLal* – having audhAryam (generosity),  
*indha nAdu* – (for) those in this world  
*aRiya* – to know,  
*uraiththadhu* – divined  
*nangu* – well  
*mARan maRaip poruLai* – the meaning of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/),  
*muppaththARayiram* – which is muppaththARAyirappadi (36,000)  
*eedu* – called eedu.

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines that, after [that](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-43/), [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) divined as vyAkyAnam for [(nam)piLLai’](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)s explanation of dhivya sUkthi ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – divine words), and it is ‘*eedu muppaththARayiram’.*

***theLLiyadhA nampiLLai cheppu neRi thannai –*** Being clear, deep/profound, and having the expertise in discerning what is required and what is not, such [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s way of dhivya sUkthis,

***cheppu neRi thannai*** – by this it implies that except the way in which he ([nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)) divined, he ([vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)) does not know of any other ways.

As said in ‘*gurupramANI kruthachiththavruththaya:*’ (Direct the activities of the mind keeping guru as pramANam (reference)), is how he is following his AchAryan, isn’t it?

***vaLLal vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai*** – Not for just those living during the same time, but for even those in later generations also to know and reach true goal, he wrote the eedu – [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) having such generosity.

[![vadakkuthiruveedhipillai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vadakkuthiruveedhipillai-522x1024.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/vadakkuthiruveedhipillai.jpeg)*vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai*

***indha nAdu aRiya –*** Like said in ‘*nAdu nagaramum nangu aRiya* \[[thiruppallANdu – 4](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu-4-edunilam/)\]’ (for the villages and cities to know), including those having knowledge and not having knowledge, for every on in the country to know, and get involved.

***mARan maRaip poruLai*** – meaning of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is AzhvAr’s, and which is in the form of vEdham. It is as said in ‘*mARan senthamizh vEdhaththin sezhum poruLai* \[sampradhAya chandhriakai – 11\]’ (~ beautiful meaning of [nammazhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s beautiful thamizh vEdham).

***nAdaRiya nanguraiththadhu –*** Like he ([nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)) divined [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) for making ‘*Urum nAdum ulagamum thammaip pOl* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 6.7.2\]*’* (~ the village, country and world like him), he ([vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)) also divined eedu very well for the world to know.

***eedu muppaththARayiram* –** It is an additional twelve thousand compared to [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/)’s vyAkyAnam, is what he has divined.

***eedu*** *– meaning.* He divined the meanings, and to get involved in it.

In the grantham of [anthimOpAya nishta](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/p/anthimopaya-nishtai.html)i it is divined ‘*idhu thAn sruthaprakASikaiyil’ \[*Srutha prakASikai is a detailed commentary for [emperumAnAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/)‘s SrIbhAshyam*\]*. That is, eedu vyAkyAnam’s count matches SruthaprakASikai’s count.

As said in ‘*gurubhyO(a)rhdha: sruthassapdhaisthath prayukthaichcha yOjitha:* \[SrIbhAshya sruthaprakASikA thaniyan\] (Heard from Acharyas, and the words used by them are included – such..), here too [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) has included the words heard (from [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)), and authored the vyAkyAnam, isn’t it? [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s ways of explanation is the one that [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) has divined in vyAkyAnam.

In a later pAsuram as he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is going to say ‘***ezhuth****ErAr thamizh vEdhaththu eedu thanai* \[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 48\]’, [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) has the involvement of documenting it only (as the original author is [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) who lectured this).

Even though this vyAkyAnam was compiled before sruthaprakASikai, it is okay for the count of this to be referenced with that grantham (since there is a match in the count).

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४५
SrI:  
SrImathE SatakOpAya nama:  
SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (theLLiyadhA nampiLLai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-44/)

**pAsuram 45**

*anbOdu azhagiya maNavALach cheeyar*  
*pinbOrum kaRRu aRindhu pEsugaikkA – tham periya*  
*pOdhamudan mARan maRaiyin poruL uraiththadhu*  
*Edhamil panneerAyiram.*
45

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-45)

**Word by word meaning**

*anbOdu –* With love  
*azhagiya maNavALach cheeyar* – [vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/)  
*pinbOrum* – his later generations also  
*kaRRu aRindhu* – to learn and know  
*pEsugaikkA* – and explain,  
*tham* – with his  
*periya* – great  
*pOdhamudan* – knowledge  
*uraiththadhu* – divined his saying of  
*mARan maRaiyn poruL* – meaning of [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) of [nammAzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/);  
*Edham il* – it is non-blemished  
*panneerAyiram* – panneerAyirappadi (12,000).

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines, now, [vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/), by his wonderful knowledge, gave meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is panneerAyiram (12,000 padi).

***anbOdu azhagiya maNavALach cheeyar* –** He divined it out of overflowing love towards [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/).

This is like said in ‘*bhAshyabhakthirachUchudhath* \[SrIbAshyam sruthaprakAsikA thaniyan – 10\]’ (devotion towards SrIbAshyam flowed into its vivaraNam (explanation)).

Or, ***anbOdu azhagiya maNavALach cheeyar –*** It can also be said that [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/) divined it out of love towards all sentient beings. This is as said in ‘*neRiyuLLi uraiththa kaNakkaRu nalaththanan* \[[thiruvAimozhi 1.3.5](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruvaimozhi-1-3-5-pinakkara-aruvagai/)\]’ (([emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/)) who has unlimited auspicious qualities, analysed the path of vEdham and spoke mercifully).

[![vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)*azhagiya maNavALa jIyar*

***pinbOrum kaRRaRindhu pEsugaikkA –*** Later generations also would need to explain using this. To help in that, (he divined such that) future generations can also learn from this and are able to explain to others. Even though there are four other vyAkyAnams (for [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)), for surety of meanings of words, this would be the most useful one for explaining it.

***tham periya podhamudan*** – With his eminent knowledge which helped give meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/).

***mARan maRaiyin poruL uraiththadhu –*** Having the greatness of incarnation from [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)’s divine lips, the meaning of such [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is dhrAvida (thamizh) vEdham.

***uraiththadhu –*** as text *(urai)*, divined a vyAkyAnam reflecting that.

***Edhamil panneerAyiram –*** Edhamil – not having any blemishes; for such [thiruvAimozhi](//divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), such vyAkyAnam of panneerAyiram (12,000) is divined. That is, it is following the divine mind of [AzhvAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/).

This is being double the size of [piLLAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/14/thirukkurugaippiran-pillan-english/)’s vyAkyanam, but going back with half the size of [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/)’s vyAkyAnam. So this is being not too small and not too long.

If there is any pramANam (reference) that matches this count, then this should be considered as divined according that pramANam’s count.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४६
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (anbOdu)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-45/)

**pAsuram 46**

*periyavAchchAn piLLai pinbuLLavaikkum*  
*theriya viyakkiyaigaL seyvAL – ariya*  
*aruLichcheyal poruLai Ariyargatku ippOdhu*  
*aruLichcheyalAyththu aRindhu*. 46

**Word by word meaning**

*periyavAchchAn piLLai* *seyvAl* – Since [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) authored  
*viyAkkiyaigaL* – vyAkyAnams (commentary explanation of meanings)  
*pinbuLLavaikkum* – for other three thousand (of the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/))  
*theriya* – for everyone to know,  
*ippodhu –* at the current time  
*Ariyargatku –* [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) later to him  
*aruLichcheyal Ayththu –* are able to explain/divine  
*ariya* – the difficult  
*poruLai –* special great meanings (arththa viSEshangaL) of*  
aruLichcheyal –* aruLichcheyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)) of [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/)*  *

**vyAkyAnam**

Starting with (the pAsuram of ) ‘*piLLAn nanjeeyar* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-39/)\]*’,* as he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) wanted to, he showed about those who authored vyAkyAnams for dhrAvida (thamizh) vEdham that is [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), and about the count lengths of those vyAkyAnams; and now regarding the other prabandhams that are related parts of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), he is divining who all authored them, and that [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) divined [vyAkyAnams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) for all of them.

***periyavAchchAn piLLai*** – Since there are his divine son *[nayanArAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nayanarachchan-pillai/)* and *[nAlUrAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalurachchan-pillai/)*, here he is specifically mentioning ***[periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/)**.*

[![periyavachan-pillai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/periyavachan-pillai.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/periyavachan-pillai.jpg)*periyavAchchAn piLLai*

***pinbuLLavaikkum theriya*** – Other than [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) which is *‘satakOpa vAngmayam* \[[thiruvAimozhi thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/thiruvaimozhi-thaniyans-invocation/)\]’ (filled with [nammAzhwAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/18/nammazhwar-english/)‘s divine words); that is starting from [thiruppallANdu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/06/thiruppallandu/) through siriya/periya thirumadal, the twenty three [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/); for them –

***theriya vyAkkiyaigaL seyvAl –*** As he considers only the growth of others as his being, since he authored the vyAkyAnam for understanding clearly –

***ariya aruLichcheyal poruLai*** – As said in ‘*ariya innisai* \[periya thirumozhi 1.2.10\]’ (hard to sing), and in ‘*aRiviththEn Azh poruLai* \[nAnmugan thiruvanthAdhi – 1\]’ (shall start saying about the deep meanings), this is how the difficulty/greatness of meanings of [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) is.

As said in ‘*senchol kavi* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.7.1\]’ (poem that is of beautiful words), and ‘*sevikkiniya senchol* \[[thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) 10.6.11\]’ (beautiful words that are sweet to the ears), and ‘*sencholAl eduththa dheiva nanmAlai* \[periya thirumozhi 1.1.10\]’ (divined a divine garland using beautiful words), and ‘*senthamizh* \[periya thirumozhi 2.8.2\]’ (beautiful thamizh (pAsurams)), starting from the time of hearing it, they are of unbounded sweetness, due to being thamizh language they are being very soft ones, and are very easy;

still, it is difficult to determine the meanings, isn’t it?

Having such difficulties and greatness (*arumai perumai*), the meanings of aruLichcheyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), *‘**Ariyargatku ippOdhu*****’ –** for the [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) after [(periya)AchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) , or, ***ippOdhu –*** *also –* after he divined the vyAkyAnams, or, for those living at the same time as him, since he divined (earlier) at that time, it is being possible for latter ones to divine/explain them.

As said in ‘*ariyadhu eLidhAgum* \[iraNdAm thiruvanthAdhi – 22\]’ (what is difficult would become easy), due to the grace of [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/), ‘***aruLichcheyaLAyththu aRindhu’ –*** that is, by his extraordinary vyAkyAnams, for meanings that are very hard to know, it is now possible for others to understand, enjoy it themselves, and divine as advice to others.

Compared to other [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), isn’t this the distinguishing greatness of him ([periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/))?

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४७
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (periyavAchchAn piLLai pinbuLLavaikkum)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-46/)

**pAsuram 47**

*nanjeeyar seydha viyakkiyaigaL nAliraNdukku*  
*enjAmai yAvaikkum illaiyE – tham seerAl*  
*vaiya kuruvin thambi mannu maNavALamuni*  
*seyyumavai thAmum sila.* 47

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-47)

**Word by word meaning**

[*nanjeeyar*](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)  
*seidha –* divined  
*viyAkkiyaigaL* – vyAkyAnams (commentary / meanings)  
*nAliraNdukku* – for a few only,  
*illai* – not  
*enjAmai* – without skipping anything,  
*yAvaikkum* – (not) for all [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/).  
*thambi* – [Divine younger brother](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/)  
*vaiya kuruvin* – of [piLLailOkAcharyar](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/11/archavathara-anubhavam-pillai-lokacharyar.html)  
*mannum* – who is well established  
*maNavALamuni* – [azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nainAchAryar (nAyanAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/), {subsequently in the vyAkyAnam, there is mention of this being both nAyanAr and [vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/) }  
*tham seeral* – by his auspicious qualities  
*seyyumavai* *thAmum* – the vyAkyAnams he/they authored  
*sila* – are for some [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) only.

**vyAkyAnam**

He (maNavALa mAmunigaL) is divining that, in this, AchAryas like [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/) also divined the authoring of vyakyAnams for a few [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), saying ‘***nanjeeyar seydha viyAkkiyaigaL nAliraNdukku’.***

That is, unlike [periyavAchchAn piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/05/periyavachan-pillai-english/) doing vyAkyAnam for all the [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), earlier
[nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/) mercifully authored vyAkyAnams for a few [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) only.

[![nanjeeyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/nanjeeyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/nanjeeyar.jpg)*nanjeeyar*

***nAliraNdukku*** – is not exact numbers but it is just a word. That is, it indicates that it is ‘a few’. He divined later in this pAsuram as ‘*sila*’ (a few) which means the same here.

What is seen as his authoring of vyAkyAnam, are available for [thiruppAvai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/11/thiruppavai-english/) and [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/) only. If any more are there (found), consider that as well.

***enjAmai yAvaikkum illaiyE –*** That is, it is Not the case that he authored vyAkyAnams for [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/) without anything skipped. ‘*enjAmai’* is (not having shortcoming, not getting destroyed) like said in ‘*enjAmal vaiththadakki* \[periya thirumozhi 2.10.1\]’ (without getting them destroyed He kept everything in his stomach).
‘*illaiyE’* -\> the ‘E’ shows certainty *(thERRam).*

***tham seerAl vaiya kuruvin thambi –*** When it comes to aruLichcheyal ([dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)), compared to all the other [AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/), ([azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nAyanAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/11/archavathara-anubhavam-nayanar-anubhavam.html)) having deep focus, by his wisdom and other auspicious qualities, like said in *‘kAththa kuNavALar* \[[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 39](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-39/)\]’ ([AchAryas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) of auspicious qualities who saved [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) ), it is by his greatness that he too divined vyAkyAnams for a few prabandhams.

As said in ‘*mannu padhinmar maRaip poruLil mARan seer*, *thunnu madhurakavi soRporuLum anna nadaiththingaL mukavalliyurai semporuLum then mudumbai, engaL maNavALarkkiRai* \[?\]’ (?), is how his focus is.

[![pillailokacharyar-nayanar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/pillailokacharyar-nayanar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/pillailokacharyar-nayanar.jpg)*piLLai lOkAchAryar and his divine younger brother nAyanAr*

***vaiya kuruvin thambi*** – Reason for all this greatness is – being born after piLLai lOkAchAryar. That is, the much celebrated [piLLai lOkAcharyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/)’s divine younger brother is [azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nayanAr (nAyanAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/); him having the relation that creates nobleness. Like saying king’s son, for him too the identity is ‘*jagathguruvarAnuja’* \[AchArya hrudhayam thaniyan\]’ ([piLLai lOkAcharyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/18/pillai-lokacharyar/)’s [younger brother](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/)). Similar to ones like ‘*thambiyudan dhasarathyAnAnum* \[yathIndhra pravaNa prabhAvam – 25\]’.

***mannu maNavALamuni*** – being well established in the meanings, who is popularly known as [‘vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar’](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/).

[![vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/03/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar.jpg)

In this way both of them (nAyanAr and vAdhi kEsari jIyar) – ***seyyumavai thAmum sila –*** have done vyAkyAnams for a few prabandhams. By ‘*thAmum’* it connects with the few prabandhams mentioned earlier (by [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)).

It is seen that [nainar (azhagiya maNavALap perumAL nAyanAr)](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/15/azhagiya-manavala-perumal-nayanar/) has divined vyAkyAnams for [thiruppAvai](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2014/11/thiruppavai-english/) and [kaNNinuN chiruththAmbu](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/01/kanninun-chiru-thambu/), and jIyar ([vAdhikEsari azhagiya maNavALa jIyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/03/22/vadhi-kesari-azhagiya-manavala-jiyar-english/)) has divined svApadhEa vyAkyAnam (inner meanings) for thiruviruththam. If there are any further more, they can be considered as well.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४८
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (nanjeeyar seidha)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-47/)

**pAsuram 48**

*seerAr vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai ezhudhu*  
*ErAr thamizh vEdhaththu eedu thanai – thArum ena*  
*vAngi mun nampiLLai eeyuNNi mAdhavarkkuth*  
*thAm koduththAr pin adhanaith thAn.* 48

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-48)

**Word by word meaning**

*[vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/),*  
*seer Ar* – who is having greatness  
*ezhudhu* – merciful writing of  
*Er Ar* – fully distinguished  
*thamizh vEdhaththu* – [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)’s  
*eedu thannai* – eedu, that is muppaththARAyirappadi vyAkyAnam (36,000 padi vyAkyAnam);  
*mun* – earlier  
*[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)*  
*thArum ena* – asked to give it  
*vAngi* – and obtained it,  
*pin* – and later  
*thAm* – that [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)  
*koduththAr* – mercifully gave  
*adhanaith thAn* – that eedu  
*eeyuNNi mAdhavarkku* – to [eeyuNNi mAdhava](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/)r.

**vyAkyAnam**

So, as he vowed earlier he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) explained that there are these vyAkyAnams, and now, that which is said as ‘*nampiLLai cheppu neRi* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 44](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-44/)\]’ (meanings of thiruvAimozhi as explained by [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)), which is having in itself the meanings of all [dhivya prabandhams](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/), which is having the greatness that by listening to it once then it can be concluded as everything is listened – he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) thinks that he should divine such eedu’s history also, and so he divines two pAsurams about that too, for every one to know,

– and he ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is divining that history in the order in which it is said of bhagavath vishayam starting with – ‘*ivar eedu aLiththaRku Eyndha mAdhavar* \[[bhagavath vishya thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/)\]’ (from [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) to ([eeyuNNi) mAdhavar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/), and so on).

***seerAr vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai –*** Him having full of greatness is – by the grace of [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), he was able to understand and write the divine meanings that the [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) divined, and having the maturity of knowledge etc., so that he is able to help others.

Or, when ‘*seerAr’* is taken as adjective to ‘*thiruveedhi*’, as said in ‘*seerAr nedumaRugu* \[periya thirumozhi 7.9.10\]’ (having great and long streets); that (place) is being complete with the wealth of srIvaishNava SrI including him.

***vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai*** – differentiates from [*naduvil thiruveedhip piLLai*](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/20/naduvil-thiruvidhi-pillai-bhattar/). It is the north street from his street where he is divining his presence. It is close to *AdhikEsavap perumAL kOyil (temple)* that is near *rAjan thuRai* (in SrIrangam)*.* In this way he is in a different place from where he is divining the vyakyAnams. So that itself became an identity for him.

For his AchAryan [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) too, the identity is ‘*mAdath thiruveedhip piLLai’,* isn’t it?

It is like saying ‘*kOyilil vAzhum vaittaNavan* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 5.1.3\]’ (living by your temple, am a SrIvaishNavan (having that strength/pride *(midukku)*).

In this way what [he](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/) who is being identified based on the place that enriches the knowledge, (who wrote the eedu, now [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) asked him to give it) –

***ezhudu ErAr thamizh vEdhaththu eedu thannai*** ***thArum ena vAngi*** – that is, he wrote ‘*nampiLLai cheppu neRi* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai –
44](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-44/)\]’ (meanings of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) as explained by [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)). So, considering that he simply documented[nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s words , he was also mentioned along with piLLAn and others. It implies that this is all [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s divine work, isn’t it?

***ErAr thamizh vEdhaththu eedu thanai*** – As said by ‘*ErArndha thamizh maRai* ’ (thamizh vEdham, that is [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/), is full of beauty), the beauty here is that having greatness that is not present in anything else, that is, full of beauty from the combination of words and meanings, and for that thamizh vEdham ([thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/)) the eedu vyAkyAnam being ably attractive like a decoration for it.

Based on that, ‘being beautiful’ can be an adjective to eedu as well.

***eedu thanaith thArum ena vAngi*** – In this way, writing such an *eedu muppaththARAyiram* (36,000 padi) vyAkyAnam which attracts the minds, and placing it in front of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), at that time (he) opened and performed divine eyeing, became very happy, ‘but you wrote during my time and without my permission, so handover the grantham which was written in this way’, saying so he got it from his divine hands, –

***mun nampiLLai*** – at that time, [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/). That is, during the time when the proper relationship between AchAryan (master) and Sishyan (disciple) were in vogue; [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) who was managing those principles very well;

***eeyuNNi mAdhavarkkuth thAm koduththAr pin*** – he kept it with him in his own presence, and then gave it to [eeyuNNi mAdhavar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/). That is, incarnated in the lineage of ‘eeyuNNi’, after surrendering to his ([nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s) divine feet, was given his AchAryan [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)’s divine name that is mAdhavap perumAL , and being his much loved disciple.

[![nampillai-goshti1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/nampillai-goshti1.jpg)*[nampiLLai](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/09/16/nampillai/) thiruvAimozhi kAlakshEpam –eeyNNi mAdhava perumAL is facing 2nd from right*

***thAm koduththAr pin*** – Being known as ‘*mAdhava sishyar’* (disciple of [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/)), and his identity being tied to that as said by the words ‘*seemAdhavan adikku anbu seyyum* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi – 3](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/08/ramanusa-nurranthadhi-3/)\]’ (being devoted to the divine feet of SrI mAdhavan (here it implies [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) being being devoted to [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/) whose original name is mAdhavAchAryar)), and he who conducted upanyAsam for [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) such that it can be the count of thirty six thousand as written,

and gave it to him as his (receiver’s) gain.

Like distributing one’s own wealth to one’s own preferred people, he gave it in the hands of him, saying, ‘without revealing this to anyone, constantly meditate upon it’. He gave this great wealth to [mAdhavap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/). {This name implies husband of SrIdhEvi who represents wealth – he is giving this eedu wealth to the person named so}.

***pin*** – after ([vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)) kept it in front of him.

***adhanaith thAn –*** the text that was written without his permission, that one.

So, in this way he gave the great meanings to (eeyuNNi) [mAdhavap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/), saving it with him for helping everyone (connected to him) later.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ४९
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (seerAr vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-48/)

**pAsuram 49**

*Angavar pAl peRRa siRiyAzhvAn appiLLai*  
*thAm koduththAr tham maganAr tham kaiyil – pAngudanE*  
*nAlUr piLLaikku avar thAm nalla maganArkku avar thAm*  
*mElOrkku eendhAr avarE mikku.* 49

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-49)

**Word by word meaning**

*Angu –* In that place,  
*avar pAl peRRa* – as he got from [nanjeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/14/nanjiyar-english/) {must be [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/) or [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/)}  
*siRiyAzhvAn appiLLai* – [eeyuNNi mAdhavap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/) (his another name)  
*thAm koduththAr* – himself gave it  
*tham maganAr tham kaiyil* – to the hands of his divine son named [padhmanAbhap perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/eeyunni-padhmanabha-perumal/);  
*pAngudanE* – In the same way  
*avar thAm* – that padhmanAbhap perumAL  
*nAlUr piLLaikku* – to one named [nAlUr piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalur-pillai/);  
*avar thAm* – he himself  
*nalla maganArkku* – to good divine son nAlUrAchchAn piLLai;  
*avarE* – he himself  
*eendhAr* – by grace gave it  
*mElOrkku* – to the noble ones of later time  
*mikku* – in a big/special way.

**vyAkyAnam**

He ([maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) divines about how this vyAkyAnam was carried out in sampradhAyam way, starting from [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/)’s grace, as obtained by [eeyuNNi mAdhavap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/) who has got the divine name of siRiyAzhvAn appiLLai, (who gave it to [padhmanAbhap perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/eeyunni-padhmanabha-perumal/), who gave it to [nAlUr piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalur-pillai/), who gave it to [nAlUrAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalurachchan-pillai/), who after praying to dhEvap perumAL and getting the command of dhEvap perumAL spread it to several of next generation including) [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), who is the AchAryan of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), with this pAsuram ***Angavar pAl peRRa siRiyAzhvAn appiLLai***.

***Angu –*** In front of him, being in divine assembly (gOshti); or, from the situation of getting it from the divine hands of [vadakkuth thiruveedhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/17/vadakku-thiruveedhi-pillai-english/);

***avar pAl peRRa*** – Being the chief of gOshti, and being the principal one doing upanyAsam of eedu – from such [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/), he ([eeyuNNi mAdhavar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/)) got the meanings like getting wealth, as said in ‘*uRu perum selvamum* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 19\]’. The scene of that place, the preceptor, and the grantham! (*oru dhEsamum dhEsikarum kOSamum irundhapadi)*.

***siriyAzhvAn appiLLai thAm –*** His ([eeyuNNi mAdhavap perumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/)) other name (*siRu pEr*) being this. Such is the wealth that he got, he –

***thAm koduththAr tham maganAr tham kaiyil –*** Like how one would show their savings, he that is [mAdhavap perumAL,](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/21/eeynni-madhava-perumal/) passed it on into the hands of his divine son who is identified as [padhmanAbhap perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/eeyunni-padhmanabha-perumal/). That is, after bestowing the meanings of eedu muppaththARAyiram (36000 padi), he handed over the SrIkOSam (text) in his divine hands as well. That is why it is said ‘*mAdhava padhmanAbha* \[[eedu thaniyan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/03/bhagavath-vishayam-thaniyans/)\]’.

In this way they both were advising this grantham in OrAN vazhi, and not publishing the SrIkOSam but nurturing it in kOyil AzhvAr (pUjA room) as part of their [thiruvArAdhanam (daily worship)](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/07/srivaishnava-thiruvaaraadhanam.html), based on the condition of [nampiLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/16/nampillai-english/); this is how the eedu of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) was handled.

In this way, protecting it like protecting wealth, this was taken care of in the thirumALigai (divine house of SrIvaishNavas) at perumAL kOyil (kAncheepuram), *bhattargaL thiruveedhi* (name of the street).

***pAngudanE nAlur piLLaikku avar thAm –*** That is, surrendering to the divine feet of [padhmanAbhap perumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/eeyunni-padhmanabha-perumal/), and with his ([nAlUr piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalur-pillai/)) obeisance to that feet, prostrating**,** speaking with pleasant words, etc., made him happy as said in ‘*kurukkaLukku anukUlarAi* \[periyAzhvAr thirumozhi 4.4.2\]’ (well disposed to do services to AchAryan), so in this way, padhmanAbhap perumAL who was pleased by the obeisances and services, decided to bestow eedu that had been forwarded along one-on-one, to nAlUr piLLai whose services served as the means.

So he took him in front of pEraruLALap perumAL, and thinking that he should get an authentic vow that he would not reveal it to anyone, and so through archakar he requested for SrI SatakOpam to be pressed on his ([nAlUr piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalur-pillai/)’s) divine head;

he ([nAlUr piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nalur-pillai/)) who understands the intention of minds, understood the way in which it was pressed in the head to imply that the text should not be released to anyone, (but) he looked at dhEvap perumAL’s divine face, and as said in ‘*aruLALar thiruvadiyai UnRinavar*’ (one who pressed the SrI satakOpam of dhEvap perumAL), showed him the sign, pressing it in the head;
