Or, as saying in ‘*paranthAmam ennum thivam tharum* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 94\]’ (will give the place of SrI vaikuNtam), and ‘*thannai eydhinarkku atthAnam koduppadhu than thagavu ennum charaN koduththE* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 66\]’ (for those who have surrendered to him he gives that place (SrIvaikuNtam) by giving his grace due to mercy), by his grace they would get the goal of paramapadham and the experience of [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and services, and live as per their true nature;

As said in ‘*pAvaLarum thamizh mAlai paNNiya nUl ivai ayndhum ayndhum vallAr, pUvaLarum thirumagaLAl aruL peRRup pon ulagil polivar thAmE* \[periya thirumozhi – 11.6.10\]’ (~ those who are able to follow the meanings of this decad of prabandham will by the grace of thAyAr who is in the lotus flower, live well in SrI vaikuNtam), starting with ‘*gyAnam anuttAnam* … *thAnE vaikuntham tharum*\[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 61](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/upadhesa-raththina-malai-61/)\]’ – and then starting with ‘*uyyaa ninaivu uNdAgil* … *parama padham ungaLukkAm* \[[upadhEsa raththina mAlai – 62](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/upadhesa-raththina-malai-62/)\]’ is how [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) divined definitively about the decoration of those in the state of AchArya abhimAnam (love of/for Acharyan), and he also divined ‘*mAmalarAL kOn madiyil vaiththu ugakkum vAzhvu namakku ethirAsan aruLum vAzhvE* \[Arththi prabandham – 20\]’ (the life we get where thAyAr’s husband happily keeps us in his lap (in SrI vaikuNtam), is the life that [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) bestows upon us).

[![ethiraja_sampathkumarar](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/ethiraja_sampathkumarar-1.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/ethiraja_sampathkumarar-1.jpg)*emperumAn in emperumAnAr’s lap*

***vAzhndhiduvar thAm*** – those who are distinguished compared to those in the state of bhagavath abhimAnam (love towards emperumAn),

***endhai ethirAsar innaruLukku ilakkAgi enRum vAzhndhiduvar –*** Those who are the receivers of [emperumAnar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)’s grace one time, would get the life there of eternal service (kainkaryam). It is said ‘*aruLAlE adiyEnai abhimAniththu aruLi, anavaratham adimai koLLa* \[Arththi prabandham – 35\]’ (due to his grace he loves me and accepts me for performing eternal service (to him)).

***enRum sathirAga vAzhndhiduvar –*** As said in ‘*athra parathra chApi* \[sthOthra rathnam – 2\]’ (there and here), **even if they go there they would enjoy the experience of Him based on the thought that He is loved by [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)**, and they would not have the inferior state of doing it for their own happiness.

***vAzhndhiduvar* –** There is no doubt that the life would be good. It is said too as ‘*nissamsayasthu thadhbhaktha paricharyArathAthmanAmi*’ (He who is involved in kainkaryam to guru would not have any doubts (about getting the true goal)).

**enRum sathirAga vAzhndhiduvar –** As the benefit of his grace, as said in ‘*pallANdum paramAthmanaich chUzhndhu irundhu Eththuvar pallANdE* \[[thiruppallANdu – 12](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/thiruppallandu-12-pallandu-enru/)\]’ (will eternally be around [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) and praise him with their pallANdu (mangaLASAsanam/wish Him live long), eternally they would be involved in the mangaLAsAsana kainkaryam (wishing Him well) which follows the true nature of [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/), and they would live very well.

This is also divined in ‘ *“ALumALAr” engiRavanudaiya thanimaiyaith thavirkkaikkAyiRRu bhAshyakArarum ivarum upadhESippadhu* \[SrI vachana bhUshaNam – 256\]’ (ALumALAr pAsuram of [thiruvAimozhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi/) – 8.3.9 says that there is no one [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) keeps for kainkaryam, He carries his divine conch etc., himself, nobody is there to carry them and follow Him (except iLaiyaperumAL/lakshmaNa), and so on, saying He is being alone), to such lonely [emperumAn](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/), [periyAzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-periyazhwar.html) and [emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) do mangaLASAsanam and call others to join them, so that His loneliness would be removed).

So he ([emperumAnAr](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/)) takes care of doing ‘*thiruththith thirumagaL kELvanukku Akkugai* \[[rAmAnusa nURRanthAdhi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/07/ramanusa-nurranthadhi/) – 78\]*’* (reformed and made me to exist for the divine pirAtti’s husband). It is this benefit that one can see directly by their eyes.

So, like how [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) started this prabandham as ‘*enthai thiruvAimozhip piLLai innaruLAl’* \[[upadhESa raththina mAlai – 1](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai-1/)\]*,* here at the time of discussion of benefits *(palam)* [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) has divined in the same way as ‘*enthai ethirAsar innaruLukku enRum ilakkAgi’,* and has concluded the prabandham so.

– – – – – – – – – –


## upadhESa raththina mAlai – ७४ (and conclusion)
SrI: SrImathE SatakOpAya nama: SrImathE rAmAnujAya nama: SrImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

[\<\< Previous (indha upadhESa raththina mAlai thannai)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/02/upadhesa-raththina-malai-73/)

**pAsuram 74 – divined by [erumbiappA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/)** (disciple of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/))

*mannuyirgAL ingE maNavALa mAmunivan*  
*ponnadiyAm senkamalap pOdhukaLai – unnich*  
*chiraththAlE theeNdil amAnavanum nammaik*  
*karaththAlE theeNdal kadan.* 74

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-74)

  
**Word by word meaning**

uyirgAL – Oh chEthanas (sentients)  
man – well established  
ingE – in this world!  
unni – (If we) think about  
pon – the beautiful  
adiyAm – divine feet of  
maNavALa mAmunivan – [SrI maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)  
senkamalap pOdhugaLai – (that are like) beautiful reddish lotus flowers  
theeNdin – and if got it touched  
chiraththAlE – by our head, then,  
amAnavanum – amAnava purushA (at the entry of SrIvaikuNtam)  
theeNdal – touching  
nammai – us  
karaththAlE – by his SrI hastham (divine hands)  
kadan – would be his duty **{**adiyEn have heard that this also means that amAnavan touching us is not necessary since we would be happy here itself due to [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s divine feet touching our head here**}**.

**Short explanation** (Given by Dr. M. varadharAjan swami in his book of thamizh translation of original vyAkyAnam of upadhESa raththina mAlai).

In his uththara dhinacharyA, [eRumbi appA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/) describes the divine feet of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), as ‘*unmeelath padhma garbha … pAchayugmam… dhayALu:* \[uththara dhinacharyA – 6\]. What it says is as follows.

A flower that is in the process of blossoming – the brightness of its inside that is of reddish hue – the bottom part of his divine feet is of such nature; top part of his feet is whitish like that of gathered milk; it is with beautiful nails, that are whitish like that of full moon days’ moon. The tip part of such nails are having a slight bend; the feet are very soft; they are *aprAkrutham* (not made of worldly matter, but divine matter); since he is incarnation of Adhi SEshan, *it is aprAkrutham.* It is the very best;

Such divine feet should be kept in his head – so pleads his disciple [erumbi appA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/).

[![srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti-1024x753.jpeg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/srisailesa-thanian-mamunigal-eedu-goshti.jpeg)*namperumAL creating the most distinguished thaniyan for his AchAryan maNavALa mAmunigaL*

*amAnavan* – One having four arms, holding conch and disc in his hands, in the virajA river before the entry to SrI vaikuNtam (where he gives his hands to help us out of the virajA river to enter the inner area of SrI vaikuNtam). This is explained in rahasya grantham of *archirAdhi* (page – 98). It is said as ‘*amAnava: – thath purushau amAnava: sa ainAn bramhA gamayathi* \[chAndogya upanishath – 5.10.2\]’. For this, as said in ‘*asamsAree vaingutha: purusha:*’, ranga rAmAnuja muni has done vyAkyanam for this as one who is not a samsAri.

**{**The following thought suddenly occurred to adiyEn one day while reciting upadhESa raththina mAlai in a temple. Kindly correct adiyEn’s mistakes in this. This is followed by its translation in English.

[மணவாள மாமுனியும்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) எழுபத்து நாலு சிம்ஹாஸநாதிபதிகளான கணனைக்கிணங்க அவ்வளவு பாட்டுக்கள் இப்பிரபந்தத்துக்கிட வேணும் என்று திருவுள்ளமாய், அப்போது அவர் சிஷ்யர் எறும்பியிலப்பா தன் ஆசார்யன் விஷயமாக ஒரு பாட்டு இதில் கடைசியில் சேர்க்கப் பிரேரிதராய் நெடுங்காலும் அதற்கு ஹேதுவென் என்று பார்த்து, நம்பெருமாள் திருமுன்பே விண்ணப்பிக்க, அவரும் அர்ச்சக முகேன [மணவாள மாமுனிகளுக்கு](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) ஆக்ஞையிட, பின் எறும்பியிலப்பாவும் பரம பிரீதியோடே இப்பாட்டை இட்டருளினார், என்பது பிரஸித்தமிறே.

இத்தால் நமக்கு உண்டான விசேஷம் ஒன்றுண்டு. “*இந்த உபதேச ரத்தின மாலை தன்னை*” வியாக்யானத்தில், இத்தை ஒரு மாலையாக, “ஆழ்வார்கள் பதின்மர் ஒரு கையாகவும், ஆண்டாள், மதுரகவியாழ்வார், யதிராசராமிவர்கள் நடுநாயகமாகவும், ‘நாதமுனி முதலாம் நம் தேசிகர்’ என்று தமக்கு முன்புண்டான ஆசார்யர்கள் ஒரு கையாகவும், இப்படி எல்லாரையும் சேர்த்துப் பிடித்து, ஒரு மாலையாம்படியிறே செய்தருளிற்று” என்று [பிள்ளை லோகம் ஜீயர்](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/08/pillai-lokam-jiyar/) வியாக்கியானமிட்டருளினார்.

ஆசார்ய ரத்ன ஹாரத்தில் கடைசியாய் [மணவாள மாமுனிகள்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) விளங்குவது போலே, இப்படிப்பட்ட இந்த மாலையிலும் விலக்ஷணமாக, கடைசியாய் [மணவாள மாமுனிகள்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) சேர்க்கப் பட்டாரிறே.

அங்கே [இவரை](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) ஸ்ரீ சைலேச தயா பாத்ர தனியன் மூலமாய்ச் சேர்த்த நம்பெருமாள், இங்கும் அர்ச்சக முகேன [இவரைச்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) சேர்த்தருளினார்.

வட மொழி மூலமாய் அத்தை அங்கே சேர்த்தவர், இங்கே [தன் ஆசார்யன்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) உகந்த அழகிய தமிழ் மூலமாய்ச் சேர்த்தார்.

[இவரைப்](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)போலே [அவரும்](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) ‘ஓரொருவர்’ இறே.

Translation:

[maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) thought in his divine mind to write this prabandham in 74 pAsurams, to match the number of seventy four simhAsanAdhipathis established by emperumAnAr. His disciple [erumbi appA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/) wished to add a pAsuram to this in praise of his AchAryan. After thinking about a way for this for a very long time, he went in front of namperumAL and pleaded to Him about this. He too through the archakar told [maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) to grant this wish; then [eRumbi appA](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/10/27/erumbiappa/) happily added this last pAsuram in to this prabandham – this is very well known.

There is a wonderful matter for us regarding this. In the vyAkyAnam by [piLLai lOkam jeeyar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/04/08/pillai-lokam-jiyar/) for the previous pAsuram of *‘indha upadhEsa raththina mAlai thannai*’, it is said as:

“That this prabandham is having the characteristic of a garland can be seen in the way [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) has put it together. That is, on one side are the ten [AzhvArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/), and then, with [ANdAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/12/16/andal/), [madhurakavi AzhvAr](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2012/10/archavathara-anubhavam-madhurakavi.html), and [ethirAjar](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/06/emperumanar/) in the center, and then, all the [Acharyas](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) before him such as ‘*nAthamuni mudhalAna nam dhEsikar* \[[upadhEsa raththinamAlai – 36](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2016/01/upadhesa-raththina-malai-36/)\]’ ([preceptors](https://guruparamparai.wordpress.com/2012/08/17/introduction-contd/) starting from [SrIman nAthamunigaL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/22/nathamunigal/)) are on the other side of the garland – this is how [he](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) has collected them well together and made it like a garland.”

Now, like how in the garland of AchArya rathna hAram [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is set as the last one, here too in this garland [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) is added last in the most distinguished way.

[namperumAL](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) who added [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) there, has, through the archakar, has added him here as well.

He added him there through the samskrutha thaniyan of *‘SrISailESa dhayA pAthram’* and here He has added [his AchAryan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) through the thamizh language that his AchAryan ([maNavALa mAmunigAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)) is fond of.

Like [his AchAryan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), [He](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/08/17/divya-dhampathi/) too is *‘Or oruvar’.*

**Concluding comments**

adiyEn got this wonderful opportunity to live in the world of upadhESa raththina mAlai for the past few weeks while trying to translate into English.

There may be several mistakes in the translation, which adiyEn would be happy to correct those if pointed out.

Dr. M. Varadharajan swami’s thamizh translation of original vyAkyAnam by piLLai lOkam jeeyar, was of unlimited help as he made it very easy for adiyEn to quote the sources of references, and to understand the meanings of many samskrutha phrases present in the original vyAkyAnam. Without that, it would have taken adiyen much more time to complete this translation. pallANdu to Dr. M. Varadharajan swami.

Thanks so much to Sri. Sarathy Thothathri swami for reviewing each and every day, correct the structure, spellings, and meanings as appropriate and publishing on time every day. Without his involvement, it would have been very hard to keep going.

Finally thanks to the readers who have sent in comments once in a while, and checking in often.

pallANdu to adiyEn AchAryan’s divine feet for his upakAram of making me involved in sath sampradhAyam.

– – – – – – – – – –

## SaraNAgathi gadhyam – pravESam (Introduction)
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/saranagathi-gadhyam/)

[thaniyans](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/saranagathi-gadyam-thaniyans/)

[![namperumal-nachiar_serthi](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/namperumal-nachiar_serthi.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/namperumal-nachiar_serthi.jpg)

#### Highlights from [periyavAchchAn piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periyavachchan-pillai/)‘s vyAkhyAnam

[srI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) had expounded on *bhakthi yOgam* (path of bhakthi or devotion) in his treatise *srI bhAshyam*, to attain *mOksham* (liberation from materialistic realm) . This was meant to counter the hypothesis put forward by *kudrishtis* (those who give wrong interpretation of the vEdhas) who had said that only *gyAna yOgam* (path of knowledge) would lead to *mOksham*. [srI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) was concerned that his followers would also think that *bhakthi yOgam* only would liberate them from this *samsAram*(materialistic realm) and would follow that to attain *mOksham*.

In SaraNAgathi gadhyam, he emphasises on *saraNAgathi* (surrendering to [srIman nArAyaNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/)) as a path to attain *mOksham*.One may ask, if saraNAgathi is the path to *mOksham*, why then did he not expound this in his srI bhAshyam to counter the *kudhrishtis*? The reason for this is that just as a brAhmaNa can not teach vEdha to a chathurtha varNika (4th class of people), one can not let out the sacred, *rahasya* (secretive) meanings of SaraNAgathi to everyone openly.

In what way is SaraNAgathi superior to *bhakthi yOgam* as a means for attaining *mOksham*?

- bhakthi is limited to *thraivarNikas* (persons belonging to the first
  three varNas, viz., brAhmaNa, kshathriya and vaisya and even in these
  three classes, the males only) whereas SaraNAgathi can be carried out
  by anyone without any distinction.
- bhakthi is a difficult method to follow while SaraNAgathi is very
  simple.
- bhakthi gives results after the person who follows it exhausts all his
  prArabdha karmas (karmas, or deeds, are of two types, sanchita and
  prArabdha; sanchita karma is the sum total of all the karmas that the
  [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)(soul)
  had earned while being born repeatedly. prArabdha is that which God
  takes out as a portion from the full bundle of sanchita and lets the
  jIvAthmA to complete in a set of births in its term in the samsAram
  following the pApa / sin and puNya / virtue karmas with which it was
  sent to this earth). SaraNAgathi yields results in the same birth in
  which the
  [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)
  had performed SaraNAgathi.
- While following the path of bhakthi, one has to be very careful in not
  transgressing what is told in vEdhas. However that is not the case
  with SaraNAgathi as it is very simple to perform. One has to take lot
  of efforts to carry out bhakthi while in the case of SaraNAgathi, it
  is readily available for practicing.
- bhakthi is not synchronous with the svarUpam (characteristics or basic
  nature) of
  [AthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/)
  while SaraNAgathi is. In other words, the svarUpam of AthmA is to be
  subservient (sEshabhUthan) to SrIman nArAyANan as well as to be
  dependent (pArathanthriyan) on him and these are fulfilled while
  following SaraNAgathi whereas bhakthi is attained through the
  self-efforts of AthmA which is not the svarUpam of AthmA.
- And, bhakthi is not a match for the result which is attained while
  SaraNAgathi is.

SaraNAgathi is also mentioned in vEdhAntha. In yAgyikIya upanishad, twelve different characteristics are mentioned for a [jIvAthmA](https://granthams.koyil.org/2013/03/06/thathva-thrayam-chith-who-am-i/) and the highest place among the twelve is given to SaraNAgathi. It has been followed by [pUrvAchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) also and is dear to the heart of SrIman nArAyaNan. Thus, being acceptable to vEdhAntha, being aligned to the swarUpam of jIvAthma, having been followed by [AzhwArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) and [pUrvAchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) and being close to the heart of SrIman nArAyaNan, made [srI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) to expound it so that his followers would also be benefited by it.

He chose the [panguni uthram](http://ponnadi.blogspot.in/2013/03/panguni-uthram-and-emperumanar.html) day for performing SaraNAgathi when [namperumAL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sriman-narayanan/) and [ranganAchchiyAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/sri-mahalakshmi/) were seated next to each other. All the hurdles of samsAram were constantly going through in his mind and in order to get rid of these, he surrendered to the divya dhampathi. He had performed SaraNAgathi earlier when he took samAsrayaNam under his AchAryA [periya nambi](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/periya-nambi/). While SaraNAgathi is to be performed only once, why did [srI rAmAnuja](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) perform it a second time? It was because of the fear that the samsAram was creating as well as the strong urge to be with God soon. Even [AzhwArs](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/azhwars/) performed SaraNAgathi repeatedly ([nammAzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/nammazhwar/) did it 5 times and [thirumangai AzhwAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thirumangai-azhwar/), 10 times). Same is the case with [AchAryas](http://acharyas.koyil.org/) too. Hence in order to get rid of samsAram and to reach SrIvaikuNtam to perform kainkaryams (service) to the dhivya dhampathi he carried out SaraNAgathi.

We shall now move on to the 1st chUrNai of this treatise.


## upadhEsa raththina mAlai – thaniyan
srI:  
srImathE satakOpAya nama:  
srImathE rAmAnujAya nama:  
srImath varavaramunayE nama:

[Full Series](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/index.php/2015/11/upadhesa-raththina-malai/)

**thaniyan – divined by [kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/)**

***in ‘kattaLaik kalith thuRai’*** (name of a particular form of thamizh poetry)

*munnam thiruvAimozhippiLLai thAm upadhEsiththa nEr*  
*thannin padiyaith thaNavAdha sol maNavALamuni*  
*than anbudan sey upadhEsa raththinamAlai thannaith*  
*than nenju thannil tharippavar thALgaL charaN namakkE*

[Listen](http://yourlisten.com/sarathy.thothathri/upadhesaraththinamalai-thaniyan)

**Word by word meaning:**

*munnam* – earlier  
*[thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) thAm, upadhEsiththa* – he had divinely advised/instructed  
*nEr thannin* – the meanings of thathvam (true knowledge);  
*thaNavAdha* – he follows without fail, always thinks and follows  
*padiyai* – those ways,  
*maNavALa mAmuni* – (such ) [srI maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)  
*than* – out of his  
*anbudan* – love/kindness toward the well-being of the world,  
*sey* – divined  
*upadhEsa raththinamAlai* – the prabandham with such title (instructions put together to form a garland of precious stones), its exclusive meanings  
*tharippavar* – those who bear it  
*tham nenju thannil* – in their mind;  
*thALgaL* – such people’s divine feet,  
*charaN* – it is the place to surrender  
*namakku* – for us.

**Simple meaning:**

{This thaniyan is written by [kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/) who is a disciple of [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/). Remembering about [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)‘s deep respect and affection towards his [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), [aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/) has started the thaniyan with the name of that [AchAryan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), which would have very much pleased [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), which would have been the very goal of [aNNan](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2013/10/16/koil-kandhadai-annan/).}

[srI maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/), due to his love and care towards the well-being of everyone in the world, divined to us the prabandham called upadhEsa raththina mAlai, based on the teachings earlier of his AchAryan [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](https://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/2012/09/19/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/), which [mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/) always thinks about and follows. Those who make the extra-ordinary meanings of this prabandham to strongly stay in their mind – their divine feet is the place for us to be.

[![ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/ramanujar-srisailesa-mamunigal.jpg)[emperumAnAr](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/emperumanar/) – [thiruvAimozhip piLLai](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/thiruvaimozhi-pillai/) – [maNavALa mAmunigaL](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/mamunigal/)

[![koilannan](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/koilannan.jpg)](https://divyaprabandham.koyil.org/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/koilannan.jpg)[kOyil kandhAdai aNNan](http://acharyas.koyil.org/index.php/koyil-annan/)

– – – – –
